Ambasaderi wa EU mu Rwanda , Nicola Bellomo yagize ati " Inkunga yacu ni imwe mu nkunga yagutse yiswe # TeamEurope .
Ni uburyo bwo kwerekana ubufatanye .
Bikubiye kandi mu ntego za EU mu gufasha ibihugu by' inshuti mu guhangana n' icyorezo cya coronavirus .
Inkunga u Rwanda rwahawe izatangwa mu byiciro bibiri .
Icya mbere kizatangwamo miliyoni 36 z' amayero , ikindi gitangwemo miliyoni 15 .
5 z' amayero mu gihe cy' imyaka ibiri y' ingengo y' imari , 2019 / 2020 na 2020 / 2021 .
Uretse miliyoni 52 z' amayero zahawe Guverinoma y' u Rwanda , EU yatanze indi nkunga ya miliyoni 1 .
8 z' amayero agenewe imiryango itegamiye kuri Leta ikorana bya hafi n' inzego z' ibanze mu guhangana n' ingaruka za coronavirus ku mibereho myiza y' abaturage .
Ambasaderi w' Umuryango w' Ubumwe bw' u Burayi mu Rwanda , Nicola Bellomo , aherutse gushima uko u Rwanda rurimo guhangana n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , yizeza ko uyu muryango uzakomeza gufatanya na rwo muri uru rugamba no mu zindi gahunda z' iterambere .
Yakomeje ashimira ingamba u Rwanda rwafashe mu gukumira no guhangana n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , zirimo gahunda ya guma mu rugo , gukaraba intoki , guhana intera n' izindi nyinshi .
Ambasaderi Bellomo yavuze ko bishimira ubufatanye burambye hagati ya EU n' u Rwanda , bushingiye nanone ku bufatanye hagati y' imigabane ya Afurika n' u Burayi .
Yavuze kandi ko muri ibi bihe bya Coronavirus barimo gukorana n' u Rwanda mu kurebera hamwe uko inkunga yakwifashishwa guhangana n' iki cyorezo .
Mu mwaka wa 2020 / 21 , u Rwanda ruteganya kuzakoresha ingengo y' imari ingana miliyari 3245 .
7 Frw ivuye kuri 3017 .
1 Frw yakoreshejwe mu mwaka w' ingengo y' imari ushize .
Minecofin iherutse gutangariza abagize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ko ingengo y' imari ya 2020 / 21 , izibanda mu guhangana n' ingaruka icyorezo cya Coronavirus , cyagize mu bukungu n' imibereho myiza y' abaturage , ikazakoreshwa mu gushyira mu bikorwa gahunda y' igihugu yo kuzahura ubukungu izakoreshwamo agera muri miliyari 882 Frw mu myaka ibiri y' ingengo y' imari , ni ukuvuga uyu wa 2019 / 20 n' utaha wa 2020 / 21
uzatangira muri Nyakanga .
Mu nyandiko y' igenamigambi ryo kuzahura ubukungu bwashegeshwe n' ingaruka za Coronavirus , gahunda y' imibereho myiza y' abaturage izatwara 133 616 548 506 Frw .
Kwita ku batishoboye , gushyigikira ibikorwa by' ubuvuzi , ubuhinzi , gutera inkunga ibigo bya leta , imishinga y' ibikorwa remezo , inkunga ya leta mu kigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu n' izindi ngamba , bizitabwaho mu kuzahura ubukungu .
Prime Life Insurance yatangije " Ikimina cyacu " " " " , ubwishingizi buzorohereza Abanyarwanda kwizigamira
Sosiyete y' Ubwishingizi ya Prime Life Insurance yatangije ku mugaragaro ubwishingizi bwitwa Ikimina cyacu bwitezweho gusobanurira neza Abanyarwanda akamaro ko kwizigamira no kuborohereza kubigeraho .
Sosiyete y' Ubwishingizi ya Prime Life Insurance yatangije ku mugaragaro ubwishingizi bwitwa Ikimina cyacu bwitezweho gusobanurira neza Abanyarwanda akamaro ko kwizigamira no kuborohereza kubigeraho .
Ikimina cyacu ni gahunda Prime Life Insurance yatekerejeho igendeye ku buryo bwa gakondo bw' Abanyarwanda bwo kwizigamira busanzwe buzwi nk' ibimina , ariko yo ibushyira mu buryo bw' ikoranabuhanga kandi burushaho gutanga umutekano ku mafaranga y' ababugannye .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Prime Life Insurance , Habarurema Innocent , yavuze ko ' Ikimina cyacu ' cyatangijwe nyuma yo kubona hakiri imbogamizi mu buryo bwo kwiteganyiriza butekanye , bworohereza abaturage kandi bukanabungukira .
Yashimangiye ko basanze bakwiye gushyiraho ubu buryo kugira ngo barusheho kugira uruhare mu iterambere ry' Abanyarwanda .
Yakomeje ati " Igituma bagomba kugana Prime Life Insurance mu buryo bw' umwihariko , ni uko noneho bafite umutekano wizewe w' amafaranga yabo kandi bakayabonaho n' inyungu .
Ikindi akaba ashobora kuyategurira umushinga runaka w' igihe kigufi cyangwa kirekire .
Kumenya amafaranga ufitemo n' inyungu zayo ubirebera muri telefoni yawe .
Ku wifuza kwinjira muri ubu buryo bwo kwiteganyiriza abikora yifashishije telefoni igendanwa aho yandika * 177 # , agahitamo ahanditse " Ubuzima no Kwizigamira " " " " ubundi agakurikiza amabwiriza .
Ku watangiye gukoresha ubu buryo buri mwaka yungukirwa 3 % by' amafaranga by' ubwiteganyirize bwe , kandi mu gihe yamaze gutanga ubwiteganyirize bw' amezi atatu akaba yabikuzaho agera kuri 50 % , amezi atandatu 70 % naho nyuma y' umwaka akabikuza 100 % .
Habarurema yagiriye inama Abanyarwanda ko kwizigama bitakabaye bikorwa n' usaguye , ahubwo ni ukureba kure .
Umwe mu bamaze ukwezi batangiye gukoresha Ikimina Cyacu , Habanabariho Th√©oneste avuga ko kuri we amaze kubibonamo inyungu nyinshi .
Yagize ati " Iki kimina iyo ukigiyemo uba wizigamye kandi ufite n' ubwishingizi icya rimwe , kuko tuzi ahahise ariko uko ejo bizagenda ntabyo tuzi , niyo mpamvu nyamukuru kuri njyewe nahisemo iki kimina .
Abanyarwanda bibukijwe kugira umuco wo kwiteganyiriza no kwigira ku bihe igihugu kimazemo iminsi kubera icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Umuyobozi w' Inama y' Ubutegetsi ya Prime Life Insurance , Ceaser Nkusi Nkwesi , yavuze ko " Kwizigamira ntabwo bisaba amafaranga menshi , bisaba gusa gufata icyemezo ukabifata nk' igikorwa cy' ingirakamaro mu buzima bwawe kigufasha mu bihe biri imbere , cyane cyane ibitunguranye bisaba amafaranga .
Uwayobotse ikimina cyacu mu gihe yitabye Imana , Prime Life Insurance iha umuryango we umusanzu yari amaze kugezamo n' inyungu zawo hakaniyongeraho n' impozamarira ingana na 5 % y' ubwizigame bwose .
Uretse ubu bwiteganyirize bw' Ikimina Cyacu , Prime Life Insurance Ltd ifite ubundi buryo bwo kwiteganyiriza burimo guteganyiriza amashuri y' abana mu byiciro byose , Ubwishingizi bw' umuryango , guteganyiriza iza bukuru , ubwishingizi bw' abakozi mu ngeri zose , ubwishingizi bwo gutabara ndetse n' ubwishingizi ku nguzanyo .

Umubare w' abatunze miliyoni 1 $ wikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize
Reporo y' Ikigo cyitwa Boston Consulting Group ( BCG ) , ku butunzi bw' abatuye Isi , yerekanye ko umubare w' abatunze miliyoni imwe y' amadolari kuzamura wiyongereye , aho wikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize .
Reporo y' Ikigo cyitwa Boston Consulting Group ( BCG ) , ku butunzi bw' abatuye Isi , yerekanye ko umubare w' abatunze miliyoni imwe y' amadolari kuzamura wiyongereye , aho wikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize .
Iyi raporo yasohotse kuri uyu wa Kane , yerekanye ko mu mpera za 2019 , abarenga miliyoni 24 ku Isi yose , buri umwe afite ubutunzi bubarirwa nibura muri miliyoni imwe y' amadolari cyangwa kurenzaho ugereranyije na miliyoni 8 .
9 bari bayitunze mu 1999 , bivuze ko bikubye hafi gatatu .
Mu myaka 20 ishize kandi , ubutunzi bw' abantu ku giti cyabo ku Isi yose bwikubye hafi gatatu buva kuri miliyari ibihumbi $ 80 mu 1999 bugera kuri miliyari ibihumbi $ 226 , mu mpera za 2019 .
Uteranyije ubutunzi bw' abatunze miliyoni y' amadolari ku Isi yose , bungana na 50 % , by' ubutunzi bw' Isi yose mu 2019 .
Abenshi mu batunze nibura miliyoni 1 $ , ni abo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Mu 2019 , mu Bushinwa , abatunze nibura miliyoni 1 $ , bikubye inshuro 29 , ugereranyije na 1999 .
Ibiciro ku isoko byiyongereyeho 10 , 1 % muri Mata 2019
Ikigo cy' igihugu gishinzwe ibarurishamibare mu Rwanda ( NISR ) , cyatangaje ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro bikomatanyirijwe hamwe mu mijyi no mu byaro , byiyongereyeho 10 , 1 % , ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ikigo cy' igihugu gishinzwe ibarurishamibare mu Rwanda ( NISR ) , cyatangaje ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro bikomatanyirijwe hamwe mu mijyi no mu byaro , byiyongereyeho 10 , 1 % , ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ihinduka ry' ibiciro mu Rwanda muri Werurwe 2020 , ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 13 , 1 % , ugereranyije n' ukwezi nk' uku kwa 2019 .
Itangazo ryashyizwe ahagaragara na NISR , kuwa 10 Gicurasi 2020 , rigaragaza ko bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro byiyongeraho 10 , 1 % mu kwezi kwa Mata 2020 ' ni ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidasembuye byazamutseho 18 , 7 % n' ibiciro by' ibinyobwa bisembuye n' itabi byazamutseho 21 , 3 % ' .
Ku rundi ruhande ariko , iyo ugereranyije ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) n' ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ibiciro byagabanutseho 1 , 8 % , ukomatanyije mu mijyi no mu byaro .
NISR iti " Iri gabanuka ahanini ryatewe n' ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidasembuye byagabanutseho 3 % n' ibiciro by' amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi n' ibindi bicanwa byagabanutseho 3 , 3 % " " " " .
Uko ibiciro byazamutse mu mijyi no mu byaro
NISR yatangaje ko ibiciro mu mijyi byiyongereyeho 8 % mu kwezi gushize kwa Mata 2020 ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ihinduka ry' ibiciro mu kwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 8 , 5 % .
Ikomeza igira iti " Bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro byiyongeraho 8 % mu kwezi kwa Mata , ni ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidasembuye byazamutseho 15 , 8 % , ibiciro by' ibinyobwa bisembuye n' itabi byazamutseho 17 , 4 % n' ibiciro by' amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi n' ibindi bicanwa byazamutseho 6 , 5 % " " " " .
Iyo ugereranyije Mata 2020 na Mata 2019 , usanga ibiciro by' ibintu bitarimo ibiribwa n' ibikomoka ku ngufu byarazamutseho 4 , 6 % .
Wagereranya ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) n' ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) , ibiciro byagabanutseho 0 , 2 % .
Iri gabanuka ahanini ryatewe n' ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidasembuye byagabanutseho 2 , 1 % .
NISR ivuga ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro mu byaro byiyongereyeho 11 , 7 % ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ihinduka ry' ibiciro mu byaro mu kwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 16 , 5 % .
NISR yagize iti " Bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro byiyongeraho 11 , 7 % mu kwezi kwa Mata ni ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidasembuye byazamutseho 20 % n' ibiciro by' ibinyobwa bisembuye n' itabi byazamutseho 23 , 2 % " " " " .
Ugereranyije ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) n' ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) , ibiciro byagabanutseho 3 % .
Iri gabanuka ahanini ryatewe n' ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidasembuye byagabanutseho 3 , 4 % n' ibiciro by' amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi n' ibindi bicanwa byagabanutseho 8 % .
Banki zavuguruye inguzanyo za miliyari 255 Frw mu korohereza abakiliya mu bihe bya Coronavirus
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda yatangaje ko amabanki amaze kuvugurura inguzanyo 7952 zifite agaciro ka miliyari 255 Frw , mu korohereza abakiliya bayo kwishyura , nyuma y' ingaruka ingamba zafashwe mu gukumira Coronavirus zagize ku bukungu bwabo .
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda yatangaje ko amabanki amaze kuvugurura inguzanyo 7952 zifite agaciro ka miliyari 255 Frw , mu korohereza abakiliya bayo kwishyura , nyuma y' ingaruka ingamba zafashwe mu gukumira Coronavirus zagize ku bukungu bwabo .
Ku wa 18 Werurwe nibwo Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda yatangaje ingamba zirimo kwemerera amabanki gusubiramo amasezerano y' inguzanyo yagiranye n' abakiliya , kugira ngo azorohereze abayabereyemo imyenda mu gihe cyo kwishyura .
Nka Banki ya Kigali kimwe n' izindi z' ubucuruzi zashyizeho igihe gishobora kugera ku mezi atatu umuntu ashobora guhabwa atishyura inguzanyo yahawe cyangwa inyungu zayo , igihe bigaragara ko ibikorwa bye byagizweho ingaruka n' ibi bihe bikomeye .
Imyanzuro y' Akanama ka Komite ishinzwe politiki y' ifaranga yateranye kuri uyu wa 29 Mata 2020 , igaragaza ko kugeza ku wa 10 Mata , amabanki yavuguruye inguzanyo 7952 mu 8667 z' abari basabye koroherezwa , zifite agaciro ka miliyari 255 Frw .
BNR kandi yari yagabanyije igipimo cy' amafaranga y' ubwizigame banki zitajya munsi kiba 4 % kivuye kuri 5 % kugira ngo nazo zifashe izindi nzego z' ubucuruzi zazahungabanywa na COVID - 19 .
Mu zindi mpinduka Banki Nkuru y' Igihugu yakoze , harimo ko yagabanyije inyungu ku nguzanyo ihabwa amabanki ivanwa kuri 5 % ishyirwa kuri 4 .
5 % , hagamijwe kuzifasha kugira ngo zikomeze gutanga amafaranga mu baturage bayakeneye muri ibi bihe , no mu bukungu bw' igihugu muri rusange .
Ikigega cya Miliyari 100 Frw , imwe mu ngamba zigiye kwifashishwa mu kuzahura ubukungu bw' u Rwanda
Guverinoma y' u Rwanda igeze kure gahunda igamije kuzahura ubukungu nyuma y' uko inzego hafi ya zose mu gihugu zigizweho ingaruka n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , kubera ibikorwa byafunzwe mu kwirinda ko gikwirakwira .
Guverinoma y' u Rwanda igeze kure gahunda igamije kuzahura ubukungu nyuma y' uko inzego hafi ya zose mu gihugu zigizweho ingaruka n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , kubera ibikorwa byafunzwe mu kwirinda ko gikwirakwira .
Ubukungu byitezwe ko bushobora kuzamuka ku kigero cya 2 % aho kuba 8 % Ikigega cya miliyari 100 Frw kizatangira mu cyumweru kimwe kiri imbere Ibigo bito n' ibiciriritse bigiye gufashwa kubona ingwate
Ku Isi yose ubukungu bukomeje kuzahara ari nayo mpamvu za leta zafashe ingamba zitandukanye zo kwivana mu bibazo .
Nka Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ziherutse gutangaza ko muri iki gihembwe hagati ya Mata na Kamena izaguza miliyari $ 2 , 999 , kubera ihungabana ry' ibikorwa n' ingengo n' ingengo y' imari .
Banki y' Isi iherutse gukora ikigereranyo yerekana ko ubukungu bwa Afurika buzasubira inyuma mu buryo bukomeye ku nshuro ya mbere mu myaka 25 biturutse kuri Coronavirus .
Imibare ya Banki y' Isi yo kuwa 9 Mata igaragaza ko ubukungu bwo muri Afurika yo munsi y' Ubutayu bwa Sahara , bwagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus ndetse ko buzamanuka ku kigero cya - 2 .
1 % buvuye kuri 2 .
4 % bwariho mu 2019 .
Ikigega Mpuzamahanga cy' Imari ku Isi , IMF , nacyo giherutse gutanga ikigereranyo ko umusaruro mbumbe w' Isi muri uyu mwaka uzamanuka ku mpuzandengo ya - 3 % naho uw' ubukungu bw' ibihugu byateye imbere kurusha ibindi bumanuke ku kigero cya - 6 % .
Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr Ndagijimana Uzziel , ati " Ni ibintu bikomeye bidaheruka mu mateka y' Isi .
Muri Afurika yo munsi y' Ubutayu bwa Sahara , hateganyijwe ko ubukungu buzamanuka - 1 .
6 % [ ‚Ä¶ ] natwe rero birumvikana ko ubukungu bwacu butazagenda uko busanzwe buteganyijwe .
Dr Ndagijimana yavuze ko icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyagize ingaruka ku ngeri zose atanga urugero nko ku bukerarugendo aho amahoteli n' indege byahagaze mu kwirinda ko iki cyorezo cyakomeza gukwirakwira .
Raporo y' Ishami ry' Ubukerarugendo mu Rugaga rw' Abikorera , PSF , iherutse kugaragaza ko muri Werurwe bwagize igihombo cya Miliyari 34 .
9 Frw , bitewe n' inama zasubitswe n' ibindi bikorwa by' ubukerarugendo byahagaritswe .
Ibi bihombo byaje bisanga urwego rw' ubukerarugendo mu Rwanda rufite inguzanyo za miliyari 87 .
7 Frw , aho urwego rw' amahoteli arirwo rwihariye inguzanyo nini kuko rufite izingana na miliyari 83 .
Minisitiri Dr Ndagijimana yavuze ko ubu igipimo cy' ubukungu bw' u Rwanda kigaragaza ko butazazamuka ku kigero cya 8 % nk' uko byari byitezwe , aho ubu imibare yagiye ivugururwa ikava kuri 5 .
1 % , nyuma biramanuka bigera kuri 3 .
5 % " ubu turi hafi kuri 2 % nubwo bitari byarangira neza " " " " .
Yavuze ko ibi bipimo bidashingira ku buryo ubukungu bw' igihugu bumeze ahubwo harebwa no ku ruhando mpuzamahanga .
Ati " Uko ibintu bihinduka ku Isi , niko imibare igenda isubira inyuma " " " " .
Hagiye gutangizwa ikigega cya miliyari 100 Frw cyo mu kuzahura ubukungu
Mu ngamba zigamije kuzahura ubukungu , u Rwanda rwashyize ingufu mu buhinzi , hategurwa ibihembwe by' ihinga biri imbere ku buryo abahinzi bahabwa amafumbire n' imbuto kugira ngo hazaboneke umusaruro mwiza bityo igihugu gikomeze kwihaza mu biribwa kinasagurira amasoko .
Ikindi ni ukwihutisha imishinga yari yaratangiye itanga akazi , cyane iy' ibikorwa remezo , nk' inyubako n' ibindi .
Ati " Hari imishinga y' imihanda , iy' amazi , iy' amashanyarazi , kugira ngo amafaranga agere ku bantu " " " " .
Hari kandi gukomeza gushyira ingufu muri gahunda zo gufasha abatishoboye yaba mu kubaha imirimo , kubaha inkunga ku badashobora gukora n' inguzanyo iciriritse ishobora kwifashishwa mu gukora imirimo ibyara inyungu .
Indi gahunda yihariye igamije gufasha abashoramari n' abikorera mu byiciro bitandukanye bagizweho ingaruka n' iki cyorezo , aho leta yashyizeho gahunda yo gutangiza ikigega kibafasha kubona amafaranga yo gukoresha .
Ati " Ni ikigega cyafasha amabanki gutanga inguzanyo iciriritse yafasha ibyo byiciro byose kugira ngo bigaruke mu kazi byongere bikore , bibyare umusaruro uzagire ingaruka mu kuzamuka k' ubukungu muri rusange .
Yakomeje atangaza ko " Icyo kigega cyaranogejwe , harimo inkunga yihariye ku mahoteli kuko bigaragara ko ubukerarugendo bizamara igihe kugira ngo bwongere buzanzamuke kuko ntibiterwa n' uko ibihe byifashe mu Rwanda ahubwo uko byifashe ku Isi hose .
Dr Ndagijimana yavuze muri icyo kigega hashyizwemo ingamba zihariye zifasha amahoteli kuvugurura amasezerano y' inguzanyo afite mu mabanki akaba igihe kirekire n' inyungu zikagabanuka , ndetse ku buryo mu gihe yatangiye gufungura , abona amafaranga aciriritse kugira ngo imirimo yongere ikore .
Yavuze ko icyo kigega " kizafasha ubucuruzi ubwo aribwo bwose bwagizweho ingaruka , hari ibipimo bizagenderwaho kugira ngo ababirimo babone amafaranga aciriritse ku gihe cyiza noneho bongere bakore bihutishe imirimo " " " " .
Ibigo bito n' ibiciriritse nabyo biri mu bizahabwa inguzanyo n' ingwate kuko ingwate zikunze kuba ikibazo kuri bene ibyo byiciro .
Ni ikigega biteganyijwe ko gishobora kujyamo nka Miliyari 100 Frw avuye muri leta , ariko hagakomeza gushakwa n' abandi bashyiramo amafaranga kugira ngo cyaguke .
Ati " Turateganya ko mu gihe cy' icyumweru kimwe cyaba gitangiye " " " " .
Mu kugabanya icyuho kiri hagati y' ibyoherezwa mu mahanga n' ibitumizwayo , u Rwanda rurateganya gukomeza guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda , abanyarwanda bagakangukira kubigura kugira ngo bisimbure ibyo hanze .
Leta ntiteganya kugabanya imirimo
Kuva icyorezo cya COVID - 19 cyatangira , ibigo byinshi cyane iby' abikorera , byafashe ingamba zitandukanye zigamije gutuma bidafunga imiryango kubera igabanuka ry' amafaranga byinjizaga .
Ibyinshi byahagaritse abakozi , ibindi byumvikana nabo bagabanyirizwa imishahara .
Dr Ndagijimana avuga ko abikorera bagerageje guhangana n' iki cyorezo , ku buryo n' abagabanya imirimo n' imishahara , bagerageje kwita ku nyungu z' abakozi .
Ba nyakabyizi nibo Dr Ndagijimana asanga barahuye n' ikibazo gikomeye , ariko ko bishingiye ku ngamba leta yafashe mu kuzahura ubukungu , hari icyizere ko ibibazo bizakemuka vuba .
Yavuze ko nta gahunda ihari yo kuba leta yagabanya imirimo ati " turacyafite ubushobozi bwo guhemba abakozi " " " " .
Ku barimu , Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , yavuze ko aba leta bazakomeza guhembwa nk' abandi bakozi ariko ko ku bo mu mashuri yigenga bazafashwa binyuze mu buryo bwo koroshya inguzanyo n' ubundi bwashyizweho .
Uruganda rwa Kinazi rwasabye abantu kwita ku buziranenge igihe bagiye kugura ifu y' ubugari
Uruganda rutunganya ifu ikomoka ku myumbati rwa Kinazi ( Kinazi Cassava Plant ) , rwatangaje ko rukora ibishoboka byose ngo ifu yarwo igere ku isoko ifite ubuziranenge , ariko rusaba abantu kujya bashishoza mu gihe bagiye guhaha kuko hari abashobora kunyura ku ruhande bakabagurisha itujuje ubuziranenge ku buryo yabagwa nabi .
Uruganda rutunganya ifu ikomoka ku myumbati rwa Kinazi ( Kinazi Cassava Plant ) , rwatangaje ko rukora ibishoboka byose ngo ifu yarwo igere ku isoko ifite ubuziranenge , ariko rusaba abantu kujya bashishoza mu gihe bagiye guhaha kuko hari abashobora kunyura ku ruhande bakabagurisha itujuje ubuziranenge ku buryo yabagwa nabi .
Tariki 7 Kamena buri mwaka , Isi yizihiza umunsi mpuzamahanga wahariwe ubuziranenge bw' ibiribwa , buri wese asabwa kugira uruhare mu guharanira ubwo buziranenge .
Ishami ry' Umuryango w' Abibumbye ryita ku Buzima ku Isi , OMS , ritangaza ko ibiribwa bitujuje ubuziranenge bihitana abantu bagera ku bihumbi 420 buri mwaka .
OMS igaragaza ko abana bari munsi y' imyaka itanu aribo bibasirwa cyane n' ibi biribwa , kuko abapfa bagera ku bihumbi 125 buri mwaka .
Kugeza ubu imyaka umunani irashize uruganda rwa Kinazi rufite icyicaro mu Ntara y' Amajyepfo mu Karere ka Ruhango rugeza ifu ku banyarwanda n' abanyamahanga .
Uru ruganda rusaba abantu gukomeza gukoresha ifu yarwo ariko banirinda izindi fu bashobora kugura kandi zitujuje ubuziranenge ku buryo byanabaviramo gupfa .
Umuyobozi w' Uruganda , Mbabazi Christian , mu kiganiro yahaye IGIHE , yavuze ko kugeza ubu uru ruganda ruhagaze neza kuko rwakira umusaruro w' abaturage kuva mu bice bitandukanye by' Amajyepfo mu Turere dutanu , ariko ubu bageze no mu Burasirazuba mu Karere ka Bugesera , aho batangiye gukorana n' abaturage baho bakabagezaho umusaruro .
Ati " Uruganda rufite ubushobozi bwo kwakira toni 120 z' umusaruro w' abaturage ku munsi murumva ko ari mwinshi , ibi byanatumye tuva mu Majyepfo tujya no mu Burasirazuba ariko dukomeje gukangurira n' ibindi bice by' igihugu guhinga imyumbati bakagemurira uruganda , kuko usanga uruganda rugikora ku kigero cya 35 % gusa .
Ubuziranenge buhagaze gute ?
Mbabazi yavuze ko ku bijyanye n' ubuziranenge hari byinshi leta yakoze harimo gushyiraho ibigo bishinzwe ubwo buziranenge ku rwego rw' igihugu , ibi bikaba aribyo bigenzura ibyo bakora , bikaba ari nabyo bibaha ibyangombwa .
Ati " Ibyo bigo byose bikorana na Minisiteri y' Ubucuruzi n' Inganda ku buryo bashobora no kuba baguhana mu gihe basanze ukora ibitujuje ubuziranenge cyangwa bakaba banagufungira .
" Nk' ubu mu gice cyacu cy' abakora ifu hari abandi usanga nabo bakora iy' imyumbati , twe nka Kinazi turi banini ariko hari abandi bato kandi badafite ibyo byangombwa .
Abo iyo bakoze nta byangombwa cyangwa nta buziranenge nibwo usanga bakoze ibyo bashatse n' igiciro bakaba bakigira gito , ariko bikarenga aho kuko abantu barya ibintu bihumanye .
Tujya tuganira na leta bakatubwira ko babikurikirana kandi nkeka ko uko ibintu biza bizagenda bikosoka .
Hari ibyago ku muntu warya ibitujuje ubuziranenge
Mbabazi yavuze ko abantu bakwiye kujya bagenzura ifu bagiye kugura , bakareba niba yujuje ibisabwa ndetse ifite n' ibirango bitangwa n' Ikigo gishinzwe Ubuziranenge .
Ati " Twebwe nk' uruganda ibyo dukwiye gukora turabikora no ku rwego rw' igihugu ni uko , hano mu ruganda dufite itsinda ku buryo nta kintu cyasohoka kitabanje kugenzurwa ko cyujuje ubuziranenge , icyo dusaba abantu ni ukurya ifu yacu ariko bakwiye kumenya ko ushobora kurya ibihumanye bikaba byakugiraho ingaruka .
Uru ruganda ruvuga ko nubwo rutarabona abantu barwiyitirira ariko hari bamwe bumva ko bashobora kuba bafata ifu ya Kinazi , bakayipfunyika mu bindi bipfunyiko byabo , bakaba bayigurisha ku mafaranga menshi mu mahanga kuko isanzwe ari nziza .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe ubuziranenge muri uru ruganda , Ngabonzima Viateur , yavuze ko mu ruganda bagenzura isuku y' abantu , imashini n' ibindi byose .
Ati " Ifu y' uruganda rwa Kinazi yahawe ikirango cy' ubuziranenge gitangwa n' Ikigo gitsura ubuziranenge , RSB , twanarenze imbibi ku buryo ifu yacu yemewe n' ikigo cy' Abanyamerika kigenzura ubuziranenge bw' ibiribwa , ubu ishobora gucuzwa ku isoko rya Amerika .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe umusaruro winjira muri uru ruganda , Rutagungira Eve Nicolas , we yavuze ko uruganda rukorana neza n' abaruzanira imyumbati , kuva rwatangira mu 2012 .
Kugeza ubu uruganda rwa Kinazi rufite isoko mu Rwanda no ku mugabane w' u Burayi , ibijya hanze bikaba biri ku kigero kirenze 40 % , aho ruteganya no kwagura rukajya muri Amerika kuko naho hari isoko rinini .
Uru ruganda rutangaza ko ifu yarwo idakorwamo ubugari gusa , ahubwo ishobora kuvangwa n' andi mafu igakorwamo keke , Capati , Pizza n' ibindi .
COVID - 19 : Amabwiriza yagenaga amafaranga ntarengwa SACCO zemerewe kubikuriza abanyamuryango yakuweho
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda , BNR , yakuyeho amabwiriza yari yashyizeho agena amafaranga ntarengwa amakoperative yo kubitsa no kugurizanya ( SACCOs ) yemerewe kubikuriza abanyamuryango bayo .
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda , BNR , yakuyeho amabwiriza yari yashyizeho agena amafaranga ntarengwa amakoperative yo kubitsa no kugurizanya ( SACCOs ) yemerewe kubikuriza abanyamuryango bayo .
Izo ngamba zari zashyizweho ku wa 24 Werurwe 2020 nyuma y' iminsi ibiri ibikorwa byinshi bihagaritswe , abaturage bagasabwa kuguma mu ngo hirindwa ikwirakwira ry' icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Izo ngamba zavugaga ko nta SACCO yemerewe kurenza amafaranga ibihumbi 150 , abikuzwa n' umunyamuryango umwe usanzwe , mu cyumweru .
SACCO kandi ntabwo yari yemerewe kubikuriza arenze ibihumbi 500 Frw mu cyumweru ku mucuruzi w' ibiribwa cyangwa ucuruza ibikoresho by' ibanze mu gihe aho SACCO ikorana n' amatsinda , buri tsinda ryari ryemerewe kubikuza amafaranga yo kugabana ku buryo buri munyamuryango w' itsinda atarenza ibihumbi 50 mu cyumweru .
Nyuma y' uko inama y' abaminisitiri yateranye kuwa 30 Mata 2020 yemereye bimwe mu bikorwa gukomeza , BNR yakuyeho ayo mabwiriza .
Itangazo ryashyizweho umukono na Guverineri wa BNR , John Rwangombwa rigira riti " Ibipimo ntarengwa byihariye byo kubikuza byari byashyizweho n' itangazo ryo kuwa 24 Werurwe 2020 bikuweho kugira ngo abanyamuryango b' ayo makoperative babashe gukora imirimo yabo nta nzitizi .
BNR yasabye SACCO gukomeza gukurikiza amategeko n' amabwiriza asanzwe agenga urwego rw' imari iciriritse .
Uko ikoranabuhanga ryunguye bamwe rigahombya abandi kubera Coronavirus
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus kimaze kwandurwa n' abarenga miliyoni enye kigahitana abasaga ibihumbi 287 , ku Isi yose , kiravumirwa ku gahera n' abakora ibikorwa by' ubucuruzi , nubwo bamwe mu bafite ibigo by' ikoranabuhanga bakomeje kubyinira ku rukoma .
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus kimaze kwandurwa n' abarenga miliyoni enye kigahitana abasaga ibihumbi 287 , ku Isi yose , kiravumirwa ku gahera n' abakora ibikorwa by' ubucuruzi , nubwo bamwe mu bafite ibigo by' ikoranabuhanga bakomeje kubyinira ku rukoma .
Bitewe n' ingamba zitandukanye zo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus , ibihugu bitandukanye byafashe cyane cyane gahunda ya ' guma mu rugo ' , abaturage benshi barifashisha ikoranabuhanga mu gusaba serivisi , kugura no gutuma ibicuruzwa ndetse no kuganira no gukora inama .
Bitewe no gukorera mu rugo , ibigo bitanga serivisi z' ikoranabuhanga rifasha abantu kuganira no kuba bakora inama ari benshi byarungutse .
Urugero ni nka Zoom ikomeje gufasha abantu benshi gukora inama .
Nubwo hari ibibazo by' umutekano byakomeje kuvugwa kuri Zoom , ntibyabujije abayikoresha ndetse n' igiciro cyayo kwiyongera , aho cyikubye inshuro zirenga ebyiri kuva mu Ukuboza .
Umubare w' abakoresha Zoom wavuye kuri miliyoni 10 ku munsi ugera kuri miliyoni 200 .
Ikoreshwa mu nzego zose kuva ku bakora inama z' abaminisitiri kugeza ku bashumba bifuza kuvugana uko umukamo uhagaze n' ibindi .
Hari kandi abakoresha ubundi buryo .
Muri Werurwe , Microsoft Teams , yavuze ko abayikoresha mu kuganira , gukora inama n' irindi tumanaho bageze kuri miliyoni 44 , rikaba ari izamuka rya 40 % .
Teamviewer nayo ikoreshwa mu kuganira no gukora inama , nayo itangaza ko irimo gukoreshwa cyane muri iyi minsi mu buryo budasanzwe naho ubuyobozi bwa ' Slack ' , buvuga ko abayikoresha umunsi ku munsi bakomeje kwiyongera .
Uburyo bwo kureba filime n' indi myidagaduro , bwakuruye benshi muri iki gihe cya guma mu rugo .
Urubuga rwa Netflix kuri ubu rwabaye ubuzima kuri bamwe mu bakunda imyidagaduro cyane cyane abakunda kureba filime , ni rumwe mu zungutse cyane .
Netflix ni Ikigo cy' Abanyamerika cyerekana amashusho binyuze kuri internet .
Yerekana ibiganiro byo mu bihugu bitandukanye biciye kuri internet birimo nka filime mbarankuru n' iz' ubundi bwoko , ariko bigasaba kubanza kuba umufatabuguzi .
Netflix irebwa mu bihugu 190 hirya no hino ku Isi , aho ifite abakiliya basaga miliyoni 182 .
Yabonye abayikoresha bashya bagera kuri miliyoni 16 muri ibi bihe bya Coronavirus .
Uburyo bwo kwerekana amashusho bwa Disney + , ni irindi koranabuhanga ryungutse kubera Coronavirus , kuko nko mu mpera za Werurwe bwatangijwe mu bindi bihugu birimo n' u Bwongereza .
Icyo gihe Disney + yari ifite abakiriya barenga miliyoni 33 , ubu ifite abagera kuri 55 , bituma ihanganye ku isoko na Netflix .
Ikigo Spotify , gifasha abantu kubona umuziki , filime n' ibindi muri guma mu rugo cyabonye abakiliya miliyoni 130 baguze ifatabuguzi .
Ibigo bifite ikoranabuhanga rifasha abantu kubona imyitozo ngororamubiri bakora muri iki gihe cya Coronavirus , biri mu byungutse cyane .
Urugero ni ClassPass , urubuga rutuma abantu babona imyitozo bakora .
Uru rubuga ruvuga ko abarukoresha biyongereye cyane .
Urundi rubuga rwa Peloton , rwerekana amashusho ajyanye no kunyonga igare .
Nubwo byasabye ko Peloton ifunga studio zayo nyuma yo kugaragaramo uwanduye Coronavirus , ibyo yinjije byazamutseho ibirenga 60 % .
Ushyira amashusho kuri YouTube , Joe Wicks , na we yungukiye kuri Coronavirus kuko yaciye agahigo akajya no mu gitabo ' Guinness World Record ' kubera kwerekana amashusho y' imyitozo ngororamubiri igihe kirekire ndetse ibigo bikomeye muri siporo biravugwa ko byatangiye kumurwanira .
Urubuga Amazon rwo guhahiraho , na rwo rwagize ibihe byiza mu gihe cya Coronavirus .
Uru rubuga rwashinzwe na Jeff Bezos , umuherwe wa mbere ku Isi , agaciro karwo kageze kuri miliyari 24 z' amadolari muri Coronavirus .
Agaciro k' imigabane ya Amazon ku isoko karazamutse cyane .
Amazon yahaye akazi abandi bantu 175 000 bo kuyifasha guhaza abakiliya babaye benshi muri iki gihe cya guma mu rugo .
Agaciro k' ibyacurujwe kageze kuri miliyari 75 .
5 z' amadolari ni ukuvuga ko kiyongereyeho 27 % mu mezi ya Coronavirus .
Abantu bareba filime kuko ntaho barimo kujya .
Nko mu Bwongereza , kugurisha imodoka byasubiye hasi ku rwego ruto ruheruka kubaho mu 1946 .
Sosiyete itwara abantu , Uber , yagabanyije abakozi mu biro byayo .
Aba ariko ntabwo barimo abashoferi bikorera ndetse na bo barimo guhangana n' iki cyorezo .
Mu bindi bigo by' ikoranabuhanga byungutse kubera Coronavirus , ni ibicuruza imikino ( Gaming ) , aho abantu benshi bayihugiraho .
BRD yabaye banki ya mbere yo mu Rwanda igenzuwe na Fitch Ratings , ihabwa inota rya B +
Banki y' u Rwanda Itsura Amajyambere , BRD , yabaye iya mbere yo mu Rwanda igenzuwe n' Ikigo Mpuzamahanga gikurikirana ibijyanye n' imyenda n' Ubushakashatsi mu by' Imari , Fitch Ratings , iyiha inota rya ' B + ' rigaragaza ko imari yayo ihagaze neza ndetse n' ahazaza hayo hameze neza .
Banki y' u Rwanda Itsura Amajyambere , BRD , yabaye iya mbere yo mu Rwanda igenzuwe n' Ikigo Mpuzamahanga gikurikirana ibijyanye n' imyenda n' Ubushakashatsi mu by' Imari , Fitch Ratings , iyiha inota rya ' B + ' rigaragaza ko imari yayo ihagaze neza ndetse n' ahazaza hayo hameze neza .
Ubusanzwe Fitch yatangaga amanota kuri za Guverinoma nk' u Rwanda .
Nko mu 2016 Fitch Ratings yahaye u Rwanda inota rya ' B + ' ishingiye ku kuba izamuka ry' ibiciro ku masoko ryari riri hasi kandi u Rwanda rukaba rwarabashaga kurigumisha ku gipimo gikwiye bigendanye n' iterambere ry' ubukungu .
Hiyongereyeho kuba amafaranga y' umwenda rwari rufite yari make ugereranyije n' icyiciro ruherereyemo .
Ku wa Mbere w' iki cyumweru , iki kigo gikorera muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , cyahaye BRD inota rya B + bitewe n' uburyo iyi banki ifite ubushobozi bwo kuba itahungabana biturutse ku nguzanyo yatanze no kuba ari banki ifite ibigo cyangwa ibigega biyishyigikiye cyangwa se nayo ubwayo ifite imikorere ihamye .
Iri nota ryahawe BRD rigaragaza intambwe iyi banki imaze gutera , uburyo imaze kwaguka ndetse n' intumbero yayo mu kuba banki ihagaze neza mu mutungo .
BRD itangaza ko rizagira uruhare rukomeye mu kuyifasha kureshya abandi bafatanyabikorwa mu rwego rw' imari ku buryo byagira uruhare mu iterambere ry' u Rwanda .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa BRD , Kampeta Sayinzoga , yavuze ko kuba iyi banki yahawe iri nota bizayifasha kugera ku ntego yayo yo guhindura imibereho y' Abanyarwanda .
Ati " Twavuye kure kandi dutewe imbaraga n' iri gereranya rije mu bihe bikomeye .
Rishingiye ku bufasha bukomeye BRD yahawe n' abafatanyabikorwa bayo mu kuyihindura banki ihamye .
Abakozi ba BRD bari gukora ubutaruhuka kugira ngo bagere ku byo abafatanyabikorwa bayo bayitezeho no gukoresha neza igishoro .
BRD ni banki ya leta yashinzwe muri Kanama 1967 nubwo yahawe ibyangombwa bitangwa na Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda muri Kanama 2009 .
Ifite imari shingiro igera kuri miliyari 7 .
Ifitwemo imigabane n' inzego zitandukanye zirimo Guverinoma y' u Rwanda ifite 97 % binyuze mu Kigega Agaciro Development Fund gifitemo imigabane ingana na 55 % n' Ikigo cy' Igihugu cy' Ubwiteganyirize , RSSB , gifitemo imigabane ingana na 42 % .
Iri mu rugendo rwo gufasha u Rwanda muri Gahunda y' Igihugu yo kwihutisha Iterambere ( NST1 ) ndetse no gushyira mu bikorwa Intego z' iterambere rirambye .
Imikorere yayo yagiye ihinduka mu myaka ishize ibasha gukuraho ibihombo yakunze kugira aho byagabanutse ku kigero cya 77 % mu 2019 ugereranyije n' imyaka ibiri yari yarabanje .
Ibi byaturutse mu kuvugurura uburyo inguzanyo zatangwagamo .
Yanogeje kandi uburyo bwo gukurikirana abakiliya bayo byanayifashije mu kugabanya inguzanyo zitishyurwa aho zavuye kuri 19 .
34 % mu 2018 zigera kuri 7 .
52 % mu mpera za 2019 .
BPR Plc yatanze miliyoni 100 Frw zo gufasha abagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus
Banki y' Abaturage y' u Rwanda ( BPR Plc .
yatanze miliyoni 100 Frw zo gufasha abaturage bahungabanyijwe n' ingamba zafashwe zo gukumira icyorezo cya Coronavirus , inorohereza abakiliya bayo barimo n' abagizweho ingaruka .
Banki y' Abaturage y' u Rwanda ( BPR Plc .
yatanze miliyoni 100 Frw zo gufasha abaturage bahungabanyijwe n' ingamba zafashwe zo gukumira icyorezo cya Coronavirus , inorohereza abakiliya bayo barimo n' abagizweho ingaruka .
Amezi abiri agiye gushira u Rwanda rufashe ingamba zidasanzwe zigamije gukumira icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Nubwo ingamba zorohejwe , hari imwe mu miryango yagizweho ingaruka kuko hari ibikorwa byahagaritswe ku buryo imibereho ya bamwe yahindutse .
Ubuyobozi bwa BPR bwatangaje ko buzi neza ingaruka imiryango imwe n' imwe yagiye ihura nazo kubera ingamba zo guhashya Coronavirus , ariyo mpamvu biyemeje gutanga inkunga yabo ya miliyoni 100 Frw .
Itangazo iyo banki yashyize hanze rigira riti " COVID - 19 n' ingaruka zayo ku bantu no ku bucuruzi zaratunguranye .
Banki izirikana ko hari bamwe mu banyamuryango bacu bahuye n' ingorane mu mibereho yabo ya buri munsi .
" Tunejejwe no gutangaza ko nk' umuryango mugari wa BPR twahaye Guverinoma y' u Rwanda umusanzu wa miliyoni 100 Frw , mu buryo bwo kunganira Leta muri gahunda irimo zo gufasha abagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus .
BPR yatangaje ko uretse gufasha abatishoboye , hanafashwe izindi ngamba zigamije gufasha abakiliya bayo bagizweho ingaruka na COVID - 19 .
Zimwe mu ngamba zafashwe harimo gushyiraho uburyo bw' ikoranabuhanga bufasha abakiliya gukoresha konti zabo bitabaye ngombwa ko bajya gutonda imirongo ku mashami ya banki , bikaba byakongera ibyago byo kwandura Coronavirus .
Iyi banki yasabye abakiliya gukomeza gukoresha ubwo buryo bw' ikoranabuhanga burimo telefoni igendanwa bakanze * 150 # , gukoresha application ya banki na serivizi zayo ziboneka hakoreshejwe internet .
BPR ikomeza ivuga ko guhererekanya amafaranga bikozwe muri ubwo buryo bw' ikoranabuhanga nta kiguzi umukiliya acibwa , bikazamara amezi atatu .
Abakiliya bashobora no kugana abahagarariye iyi banki ( agents ) bari hirya no hino mu gihugu begereye aho batuye , bagahabwa serivisi za banki
BPR Plc ivuga ko abakiliya bari basanzwe bayifitemo inguzanyo bemerewe igihe kiri hagati y' amezi atatu n' atandatu batishyura bitewe n' imbogamiziri buri mukiliya yagiye ahura nazo .
Abakiliya ba BPR imishahara yabo yakoreshejwe mu gufasha Abanyarwanda guhangana na Coronavirus , bemerewe gusaba inguzanyo ingana n' umushahara wabo w' ukwezi batabonye , ikazatangira kwishyurwa nyuma y' ukwezi kandi bemererwa kuba bayishyura mu gihe cy' amezi 12 .
BPR kandi ivuga ko abigomwe umushahara batazabasha kwishyura inguzanyo bari basanzwe bishyura , bazahabwa igihe cy' ukwezi batishyura kuko bizwi ko batazahembwa .
Iyi nguzanyo [ personal loan ] yishyurwa kugera ku mezi 12 bitewe n' ubushake bw' umukiliya .
BPR isobanura ko iyi nguzanyo nshya umukiliya aba ahawe ayishyura ku nyungu ingana n' iyo yari asanzwe yishyuriraho inguzanyo yari afite .
Abaye adafite inguzanyo ahabwa ku nyungu isanzwe ya banki .
BPR yanatekereje ku bakozi bakorera ibigo ariko ibikorwa byabo bikaba byarahagaze bityo bikaba bitazabasha kubahemba kandi bari basanzwe bafite inguzanyo .
Aba bemerewe kutishyura inguzanyo mu mezi atatu mu gihe ibyo bigo bikisuganya ngo byongere gutangira ibikorwa bibahembe .
Ibisabwa ku batanze umushahara w' ukwezi kwa kane bifuza inguzanyo ni ukwandikira BPR Plc kuri email [ email protected ] ukavuga amazina n' ibyo usaba .
Ku bakorera ibigo bifite ikibazo cyo kubahemba muri iki gihe bakwandika basaba guhabwa amezi yo gusubika kwishyura inguzanyo .
Umukoresha na we ashobora kwandikira BPR Plc asaba ko ifasha abakozi be batazabasha kwishyura inguzanyo kuko atazabahemba .
Aba banyuza ubusabe bwabo kuri email [ email protected ] , bagasaba kwemererwa kutishyura inguzanyo mu gihe cy' amezi atatu .
Ku bakeneye ibindi bisobanuro kuri izi ngamba banki yashizeho zo gufasha abakiliya muri iki gihe cya Covid - 19 cyangwa ikindi kibazo kuri serivisi za banki , bashobora guhamagara umurongo wa banki ku 1500 .
Miliyari hafi 900 Frw zizakenerwa mu kuzahura ubukungu bw' u Rwanda nyuma ya Coronavirus
Gahunda yo kuzahura ubukungu nyuma y' icyorezo cya Coronavirus igaragaza ko u Rwanda rushobora kuzakoresha agera muri miliyari 882 Frw mu myaka ibiri y' ingengo y' imari , ni ukuvuga uyu turimo wa 2019 / 20 n' utaha wa 2020 / 21 uzatangira muri Nyakanga .
Gahunda yo kuzahura ubukungu nyuma y' icyorezo cya Coronavirus igaragaza ko u Rwanda rushobora kuzakoresha agera muri miliyari 882 Frw mu myaka ibiri y' ingengo y' imari , ni ukuvuga uyu turimo wa 2019 / 20 n' utaha wa 2020 / 21 uzatangira muri Nyakanga .
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyatumye ibikorwa byinshi bifungwa , ndetse n' ubwo Guverinoma iheruka gufata umwanzuro ko bimwe bifungurwa nyuma y' iminsi isaga 40 , byasabwe gukoresha abakozi bake , kandi bigafungura hagati ya saa kumi n' imwe za mu gitondo na saa mbili z' ijoro .
Minisiteri y' Imari n' Igenamigambi yakoze gahunda igamije kuzahura ubukungu bw' u Rwanda , zirimo gushyigikira ibikorwa by' ubuvuzi , kwita ku batishoboye , gutera inkunga ibigo bya leta , inkunga ya leta mu kigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu n' izindi ngamba zigamije guhangana n' ingaruka za Coronavirus .
Bumwe mu buryo burimo kwifashisha mu korohereza ibigo byagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus , harimo uburyo bwo kuvanaho imwe mu misoro , aho kubara avansi y' umusoro ku nyungu z' ibigo n' iz' abantu ku giti cyabo , bizashingira ku byacurujwe uyu mwaka .
Ibinyabiziga bikora imirimo ibyara inyungu nabyo bizishyura avansi y' umusoro ku nyungu hashingiwe ku mubare w' amezi y' umwaka bizaba byarakozemo iyo mirimo ibyara inyungu , ndetse udupfukamunwa dukorerwa mu Rwanda natwo twasonewe umusoro ku nyungu , mu rwego rwo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus .
Imisoro yinjira izagabanukaho arenga miliyari 200 Frw
Komiseri mu Kigo cy' Imisoro n' amahoro , ushinzwe Imisoro y' Imbere mu gihugu , Kayigi Aimable , yabwiye itangazamakuru ko ibibazo n' ingamba bijyanye na Coronavirus bizagabanya ingano y' umusoro winjiraga mu gihugu uhereye hagati ya Werurwe ubwo u Rwanda rwafungaga ibikorwa kugeza muri uku kwezi kwa Gicurasi ubwo bimwe muri byo bitangiye gufungurwa .
Yakomeje ati " Mu mibare twari dufite , twabonaga ingaruka bishobora kuzagira ku mafaranga leta yinjizaga , bishobora kugera nko kuri miliyari nka 234 Frw ku bijyanye n' umusoro .
Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri y' Imari n' Igenamigambi Ushinzwe Imari ya Leta , Richard Tusabe , avuga ko Leta yiyemeje guhara uyu musoro mu kwifatanya n' Abanyarwanda bafite ibikorwa byahungabanye kubera COVID - 19 mu bijyanye n' ubukungu n' imibereho y' abaturage .
Ati " Sinavuga ngo tugarukiye aha , turakomeza dusuzume , nibigenda neza vuba turasubira mu buzima busanzwe , nibitagenda neza vuba nabyo turakomeza dufatanye kwiga ingamba zashyirwaho , zose zigamije kubungabunga ubuzima bw' umunyarwanda .
Hagiye gushingwa ikigega cya miliyari 100 Frw
Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr Ndagijimana Uzziel , aheruka kuvuga ko mu ngamba zigamije kuzahura ubukungu , u Rwanda rwashyize ingufu mu buhinzi , hategurwa ibihembwe by' ihinga biri imbere , ku buryo abahinzi bahabwa amafumbire n' imbuto kugira ngo hazaboneke umusaruro mwiza , bityo igihugu gikomeze kwihaza mu biribwa kinasagurira amasoko .
Ikindi ni ukwihutisha imishinga yari yaratangiye itanga akazi , cyane iy' ibikorwa remezo , nk' inyubako n' ibindi .
Ati " Hari imishinga y' imihanda , iy' amazi , iy' amashanyarazi , kugira ngo amafaranga agere ku bantu " " " " .
Hari kandi gukomeza gushyira ingufu muri gahunda zo gufasha abatishoboye yaba mu kubaha imirimo , kubaha inkunga ku badashobora gukora n' inguzanyo iciriritse ishobora kwifashishwa mu gukora imirimo ibyara inyungu .
Indi gahunda yihariye igamije gufasha abashoramari n' abikorera mu byiciro bitandukanye bagizweho ingaruka n' iki cyorezo , aho leta yashyizeho gahunda yo gutangiza ikigega kibafasha kubona amafaranga yo gukoresha .
Ati " Ni ikigega cyafasha amabanki gutanga inguzanyo iciriritse yafasha ibyo byiciro byose kugira ngo bigaruke mu kazi byongere bikore , bibyare umusaruro uzagire ingaruka mu kuzamuka k' ubukungu muri rusange .
" Icyo kigega cyaranogejwe , harimo inkunga yihariye ku mahoteli kuko bigaragara ko ubukerarugendo bizamara igihe kugira ngo bwongere buzanzamuke kuko ntibiterwa n' uko ibihe byifashe mu Rwanda ahubwo uko byifashe ku Isi hose .
Dr Ndagijimana yavuze muri icyo kigega hashyizwemo ingamba zihariye zifasha amahoteli kuvugurura amasezerano y' inguzanyo afite mu mabanki akaba igihe kirekire n' inyungu zikagabanuka , ndetse ku buryo mu gihe yatangiye gufungura , abona amafaranga aciriritse kugira ngo imirimo yongere ikore .
Yavuze ko icyo kigega " kizafasha ubucuruzi ubwo aribwo bwose bwagizweho ingaruka , hari ibipimo bizagenderwaho kugira ngo ababirimo babone amafaranga aciriritse ku gihe cyiza noneho bongere bakore bihutishe imirimo " " " " .
Ibigo bito n' ibiciriritse nabyo biri mu bizahabwa inguzanyo n' ingwate kuko ingwate zikunze kuba ikibazo kuri bene ibyo byiciro .
Ni ikigega biteganyijwe ko gishobora kujyamo nka Miliyari 100 Frw avuye muri leta , ariko hagakomeza gushakwa n' abandi bashyiramo amafaranga kugira ngo cyaguke .
Ati " Turateganya ko mu gihe cy' icyumweru kimwe cyaba gitangiye " " " " .
Mu kugabanya icyuho kiri hagati y' ibyoherezwa mu mahanga n' ibitumizwayo , u Rwanda rurateganya gukomeza guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda , abanyarwanda bagakangukira kubigura kugira ngo bisimbure ibyo hanze .
U Rwanda rwahawe inguzanyo iciriritse ya miliyari 93 Frw yo gufasha urwego rw' ingufu
Guverinoma y' u Rwanda na Banki y' Isi byasinye amasezerano y' inkunga y' inyongera ya miliyoni 100 z' amadolari , ni ukuvuga miliyari 93 .
1 Frw yo gushyigikira icyiciro cya gatatu cy' umushinga wo guteza imbere urwego rw' amashanyarazi , Third Rwanda Energy Sector Development Policy Operation ( DPO ) .
Guverinoma y' u Rwanda na Banki y' Isi byasinye amasezerano y' inkunga y' inyongera ya miliyoni 100 z' amadolari , ni ukuvuga miliyari 93 .
1 Frw yo gushyigikira icyiciro cya gatatu cy' umushinga wo guteza imbere urwego rw' amashanyarazi , Third Rwanda Energy Sector Development Policy Operation ( DPO ) .
Iyi nkunga ni inguzanyo iciriritse izafasha Guverinoma y' u Rwanda kuvugurura ingengo y' imari hagamijwe kwitegura no guhangana n' ingaruka zatewe n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus mu rwego rw' ingufu .
Icyiciro cya gatatu cy' umushinga wo guteza imbere urwego rw' amashanyarazi , ni icya nyuma mu mushinga mugari wagombaga gutwara miliyoni 375 z' amadolari , inguzanyo ya mbere yo gutangiza uwo mushinga ikaba yaratanzwe mu Ukuboza 2017 , iya nyuma yatanzwe umwaka ushize .
Uwo mushinga ugomba kurangirana na 2020 , ugamije gufasha mu iterambere ry' urwego rw' amashanyarazi mu Rwanda nkuko biri muri gahunda y' Igihugu y' Iterambere , NST1 , mu ntego yo kugeza amashanyarazi kuri bose bitarenze mu 2024 .
Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr .
Uzziel Ndagijimana , yavuze ko inkunga bahawe izafasha mu guharanira ko serivisi z' amashanyarazi zikomeza gutangwa nta kirogoya .
Yagize ati " Nubwo ingaruka za COVID - 19 byitezwe ko zizarangira , urwego rw' ingufu byitezwe ko ruzahura n' ibibazo nyamara gukomeza gutanga serivisi z' amashanyarazi birakenewe cyane kugira ngo serivisi rusange zikomeze , bigabanye icyuho mu isubira inyuma ry' ubukungu kandi abatishoboye bakomeze kwatabwaho .
Umuyobozi wa Banki y' Isi , Ishami ry' u Rwanda , Yasser El Gammal , yavuze ko yizeye ko inkunga yatanzwe izafasha u Rwanda gusubira vuba mu murongo w' iterambere ry' ubukungu .
Ati " Nizeye ko kubera ubuyobozi bwiza , ukwihangana kw' Abanyarwanda , ingamba zafashwe na Guverinoma , inkunga ya Banki y' Isi n' abandi bafatanyabikorwa mu iterambere izafasha u Rwanda kwigobotora iki cyorezo rusubire mu nzira nziza .
Mu mpera z' uyu mushinga mu Ukuboza 2020 byitezwe ko ingo 61 % mu Rwanda zizaba zigerwaho n' amashanyarazi , bitange icyizere ku kugera ku 100 % mu mwaka wa 2024 .
Uyu mushinga kandi kunoza imicungire y' amashanyarazi hagabanywa ingano itakara , kugabanya igiciro no kongera umusaruro w' ikigo kiyacuruza n' ibindi .
Imikorere y' ikigega kigamije kuzahura ubukungu bw' u Rwanda bwazahajwe na Coronavirus
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda , BNR , yashyizeho umurongo n' uburyo ikigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu bw' u Rwanda kizakora .
Ni ikigega gifite hafi miliyoni 200 z' amadorali , ni ukuvuga hafi miliyari 186 z' amanyarwanda .
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda , BNR , yashyizeho umurongo n' uburyo ikigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu bw' u Rwanda kizakora .
Ni ikigega gifite hafi miliyoni 200 z' amadorali , ni ukuvuga hafi miliyari 186 z' amanyarwanda .
Iki kigega kigamije gutera inkunga ibikorwa by' abikorera byahungabanyijwe n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr Uzziel Ndagijimana , aherutse gutangaza ko ari ikigega kizafasha amabanki gutanga inguzanyo iciriritse ibyo byiciro byose kugira ngo bigaruke mu kazi byongere bikore , bibyare umusaruro uzagire ingaruka mu kuzamuka k' ubukungu muri rusange .
Muri iki kigega hashyizwemo ingamba zihariye zifasha amahoteli kuvugurura amasezerano y' inguzanyo afite mu mabanki akaba igihe kirekire n' inyungu zikagabanuka , ndetse ku buryo mu gihe yatangiye gufungura , abona amafaranga aciriritse kugira ngo imirimo yongere ikore .
Imikorere y' iki kigega ireba amabanki 16 y' ubucuruzi n' ibigo by' imari biciriritse .
Banki Nkuru y' Igihugu niyo izagicunga , gusa amafaranga ku bakiliya azajya atangwa n' amabanki .
Ku ikubitiro leta yemeye gushyiramo miliyari 100 Frw ariko hagakomeza gushakwa abandi bashyiramo amafaranga kugira ngo cyaguke .
Usibye ku mahoteli , kizafasha mu gutanga igishoro ku bucuruzi bwagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus kugira ngo bukomeze gukora no kudahagarika abakozi , hari kandi inguzanyo ku bucuruzi buto n' ubuciriritse nabwo bwibasiwe na COVID - 19 .
Banki Nkuru y' Igihugu izacunga imikorere yacyo , izaguriza amabanki kugira ngo nayo agurize abakiliya bayakeneye .
Gusaba inguzanyo bizakorwa binyuze muri banki zibishinzwe , nazo zizajya zikurikirana ikibazo , nyuma zohereza kuri BNR ibyifuzo by' abasabye gufashwa kugira ngo bisuzumwe biganishe no ku cyemezo cya nyuma .
Nyuma yo kwemezwa , amabanki azatanga amafaranga kuri konte y' uwayasabye hanyuma ibyakozwe bigaragarizwe BNR ari nayo izatuma amafaranga agera kuwasabye .
Umuyobozi w' Urugaga rw' Abikorera mu Rwanda , Robert Bapfakurera , aherutse kuvuga ati " nk' ubukerarugendo , amahoteli , byagize ibibazo bikomeye kuko barafunze burundu , nubwo [ mu Rwanda ] ibibazo [ bya coronavirus ] byarangira ntabwo ibibazo bizaba byarangiye ahandi hose kuko ubukerarugendo bukorana n' amahanga , bakeneye gufashwa cyane .
Raporo y' Ishami ry' Ubukerarugendo mu Rugaga rw' Abikorera , PSF , yagaragazaga ko muri Werurwe bwagize igihombo cya miliyari 34 .
9 Frw , bivuye ku nama zasubitswe n' ibindi bikorwa by' ubukerarugendo byahagaritswe .
Ibi bihombo byaje bisanga urwego rw' ubukerarugendo mu Rwanda rufite inguzanyo za miliyari 87 .
Imibare ya Banki y' Isi yo kuwa 9 Mata igaragaza ko ubukungu bwo muri Afurika yo munsi y' Ubutayu bwa Sahara , bwagizweho ingaruka na Coronavirus ndetse ko buzamanuka ku kigero cya - 2 .
1 % buvuye kuri 2 .
4 % bwariho mu 2019 .
Ikigega Mpuzamahanga cy' Imari ku Isi , IMF , nacyo giherutse gutanga ikigereranyo ko umusaruro mbumbe w' Isi muri uyu mwaka uzamanuka ku mpuzandengo ya - 3 % naho uw' ubukungu bw' ibihugu byateye imbere kurusha ibindi bumanuke ku kigero cya - 6 % .
Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr Ndagijimana Uzziel , ati " Ni ibintu bikomeye bidaheruka mu mateka y' Isi .
Muri Afurika yo munsi y' Ubutayu bwa Sahara , hateganyijwe ko ubukungu buzamanuka - 1 .
6 % [ ‚Ä¶ ] natwe rero birumvikana ko ubukungu bwacu butazagenda uko busanzwe buteganyijwe .
Minisitiri Dr Ndagijimana yavuze ko ubu igipimo cy' ubukungu bw' u Rwanda kigaragaza ko butazazamuka ku kigero cya 8 % nk' uko byari byitezwe , aho ubu imibare yagiye ivugururwa ikava kuri 5 .
1 % , nyuma biramanuka bigera kuri 3 .
5 % " ubu turi hafi kuri 2 % nubwo bitari byarangira neza " " " " .

Ishoramari mvamahanga ku Isi yose rizagabanukaho 40 % mu 2020
Raporo y' Inama ya Loni ishinzwe ubucuruzi n' iterambere ( UNCTAD ) , yagaragaje ko ishoramari mvamahanga ( FDI , Foreign Direct Investment ) , rizagabanukaho 40 % muri uyu mwaka ku isi yose kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Raporo y' Inama ya Loni ishinzwe ubucuruzi n' iterambere ( UNCTAD ) , yagaragaje ko ishoramari mvamahanga ( FDI , Foreign Direct Investment ) , rizagabanukaho 40 % muri uyu mwaka ku isi yose kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Iyi raporo yatangajwe kuri uyu wa Kabiri , yerekana ko ishoramari mvamahanga rizagabanuka rikava kuri miliyari 1540 z' amadolari ryariho mu 2019 rikagera munsi ya miliyari 1000 z' amadolari , bikaba ari ubwa mbere kuva mu 2005 .
Ishoramari mvamahanga byitezwe ko rizagabanuka hagati ya 5 - 10 % mu mwaka utaha hanyuma ryongere kuzamuka mu 2022 .
Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa UNCTAD , Mukhisa Kituyi , yabwiye itangazamakuru ati " Ubukungu bw' Isi yose buri ahantu habi harenze uko byagenze mu 2008 , ubwo habagaho ibibazo by' ubukungu " " " " .
Yavuze ko icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyagize ingaruka mu byo abantu bashyira ku isoko , ibyo abaguzi bakenera ndetse no kuri gahunda z' ishoramari mvamahanga .
Ibihugu bikennye bizagirwaho ingaruka cyane n' igabanuka ry' ishoramari mvamahanga .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe ishoramari muri UNCTAD , James Zhan , yagize ati " Ubukungu buri mu nzira y' amajyambere byitezwe ko buzasubira hasi mu bijyanye n' ishoramari mvamahanga kubera ko buryishingikiriza mu musaruro ndetse no mu byo rikenera " " " " .
RwandAir yatangiye gutwara amafi yo muri Tanzania iyageza mu Burayi
Sosiyete ya RwandAir yatangaje ko indege zayo zatangiye gutwara amafi aturutse i Mwanza muri Tanzania ziyajyanye i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi .
Sosiyete ya RwandAir yatangaje ko indege zayo zatangiye gutwara amafi aturutse i Mwanza muri Tanzania ziyajyanye i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi .
Intego y' izo ngendo ni ukugeza ayo mafi ku isoko ryo mu Burayi nk' uko biri mu itangazo RwandAir yashyize kuri Twitter .
Today we inaugurated our cargo flight from Mwanza to Brussels which will be transporting fish to Europe .

Umwaka ushize muri Werurwe nibwo u Rwanda na Tanzania byemeranyije ubufatanye mu kugeza ibicuruzwa ku masoko akomeye , arimo ayo muri Tanzania ndetse no ku mugabane w' u Burayi .
Ibihugu byombi byemeranyije ishyirwaho ry' ndege z' imizigo zizajya ziva ku kibuga cy' Indege cya Mwanza zijya ku masoko y' i Burayi , bikaba byaragombaga gutangira kuwa 1 Nyakanga 2019 .
Gutwara amafi yo muri Tanzania akagezwa mu Burayi , ni amahirwe ku barobyi n' abacuruzi b' amafi bo muri icyo gihugu bari bamaze igihe bifuza uburyo buborohereye bwo kugeza umusaruro wabo ku masoko yo mu mahanga , bakagorwa n' igiciro cy' urugendo .
Ubusanzwe abacuruzi b' amafi bajyaga babanza kugeza umusaruro wabo ku bibuga by' indege bya Entebbe muri Uganda na Nairobi muri Kenya , kugira ngo indege ziwugeze ku masoko yo hanze , ibintu bavuga ko byabahendaga .
Ihuriro ry' abarobyi muri Tanzania ritangaza ko hari umusaruro w' amafi wangirikaga kubera kubura uko bawugeza ku isoko mpuzamahanga .
Nko muri Werurwe umwaka ushize , hari umusaruro w' amafi ufite agaciro gasaga miliyari eshanu z' amashilingi ya Tanzania bagombaga kugeza ku masoko ya Israel no mu Buyapani , babuze uko bagezayo kubera guhenda k' urugendo .
Uko umusaruro mbumbe w' u Rwanda wiyongereyeho miliyari zirenga 3000Frw mu myaka itanu
Nubwo u Rwanda kimwe n' Isi yose bihanganye n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , mbere yacyo ubukungu bwarwo bwakomeje kwiyongera mu nkingi zose bwubakiyeho , aho ubuhinzi , inganda , serivisi n' ibindi bitahwemye kuzamuka umwaka ku wundi kandi uruhare rwabyo mu musaruro mbumbe w' igihugu rukigaragaza .
Nubwo u Rwanda kimwe n' Isi yose bihanganye n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , mbere yacyo ubukungu bwarwo bwakomeje kwiyongera mu nkingi zose bwubakiyeho , aho ubuhinzi , inganda , serivisi n' ibindi bitahwemye kuzamuka umwaka ku wundi kandi uruhare rwabyo mu musaruro mbumbe w' igihugu rukigaragaza .
Imibare Ikigo cy' Igihugu cy' Ibarurishamibare ( NISR ) , cyatangaje kuwa 24 Werurwe 2020 , igaragaza ko mu 2019 , umusaruro mbumbe w' u Rwanda ( GDP ) , wiyongereye ku rugero rwa 9 .
4 % , ugera kuri miliyari 9105 Frw uvuye kuri miliyari 8189 Frw wariho mu 2018 .
Muri uyu musaruro mbumbe , ubuhinzi bwagize uruhare rwa 24 % inganda zigira uruhare rwa 18 % , Serivisi zingana 49 % mu gihe ibindi bisigaye byagize uruhare ku kigero cya 9 % .
Iri zamuka ry' ubukungu riratanga icyizere ko nta gihindutse ibyo u Rwanda ruteganya ko nibura mu 2035 ruzaba rufite ubukungu buciriritse bishoboka .
Icyo gihe birasaba ko ubukungu bwaba bwihuta ku 10 % , bigatuma umunyarwanda yazaba yinjiza asaga miliyoni 10 Frw ku mwaka .
Rirashimangira kandi imbaraga leta y' u Rwanda ikomeje gushyira mu guteza imbere ubukungu .
Mu 1994 , izamuka ry' ubukungu bw' u Rwanda , ryasubiye inyuma kuri - 41 .
9 % , umusaruro mbumbe w' umuturage wari amadolari 146 ku mwaka .
Nubwo inzira ikiri ndende , aho iterambere ry' ubukungu bw' u Rwanda rigeze harivugira kuko nko mu myaka itanu ishize umusaruro mbumbe wavuye kuri miliyari miliyari 5 956 Frw mu 2015 , ugera kuri miliyari 9105 Frw .
Usubije amaso inyuma , usanga umusaruro mbumbe w' u Rwanda mu myaka itanu ishize ( 2015 - 2019 ) , wariyongereyeho miliyari 3149 Frw .
Iri zamuka rishingiye ahanini kuri gahunda yo guteza imbere ubuhinzi , ishoramari muri serivisi zitandukanye , ubucuruzi , inganda n' ibindi bicumbi by' ubukungu .
Izamuka ry' umusaruro mbumbe mu myaka itanu
Mu 2015 umusaruro mbumbe w' u Rwanda wazamutseho 6 .
9 % , aho wanganaga na miliyari 5 956 Frw zikaba zari zivuye kuri miliyari 4 915Frw mu 2014 .
Mu 2016 umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 6 , 618 Frw , aho wazamutse ku kigero cya 5 .
9 % ugereranyije n' umwaka wabanje .
Mu 2017 umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 7 597 ukaba warazamutse 6 .
1 % , mu 2018 wageze kuri miliyari 8189 Frw uzamutse ku kigero cya 8 .
6 % ugereranyije n' umwaka wabanje wa 2017 .
Ubwo hatangazwa umusaruro mbumbe wa 2018 , Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr Uzziel Ndagijimana , yavuze ko iterambere ry' ubuhinzi , inganda , ibikorerwa mu Rwanda na serivisi byazamuye ubukungu cyane .
Yagize ati " Ngira ngo muzi gahunda ya Made in Rwanda no korohereza ibikorwa bikorerwa mu Rwanda , biragenda rero bitanga umusaruro , umusaruro w' inganda urazamuka cyane " " " " .
Minisitiri Ndagijimana yavuze ko mu bitanga umusaruro harimo ibikorwa by' ubwubatsi byaba imihanda n' inganda .
Icyo gihe ibikorwa by' ubwubatsi byazamutseho 20 % , mu nganda zitunganya ibintu bitandukanye cyazamutseho kuri 13 % , umusaruro w' inganda zitunganya ibiryo ni 10 % , izitunganya imyenda ni 26 % na 38 % ku musaruro w' inganda zikora ibikoresho bikoze mu byuma .
Mu 2019 , umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 9105 Frw uvuye kuri miliyari 8189 Frw wariho mu 2018 .
Bisobanuye ko hiyongereyeho miliyoni 916Frw mu mwaka umwe .
Urwego rwa serivisi rwashinze imizi
Mu 2015 , urwego rwa serivisi rwazamutse ku kigero cya 7 % rugira uruhare mu musaruro mbumbe wose rwa 47 % .
Mu 2016 serivisi zazamutse ku kigero cya 6 % .
Muri uwo mwaka serivisi zishingiye kuri hoteli na restaurant zazamutse ku rugero rwa 11 % bitewe na gahunda yo kwakira inama n' ibikorwa bitandukanye .
Imirimo y' ubwikorezi yazamutse ku rugero rwa 8 % ahanini bitewe n' ubwikorezi bwo mu kirere bwazamutse ku rugero rwa 15 % .
Mu 2017 , serivisi zazamutse ku kigero cya 8 % naho uruhare rwazo mu musaruro mbumbe rugera kuri 46 % .
Mu 2018 umusaruro wa serivisi wazamutse ku rugero rwa 9 % naho mu 2019 uzamuka ku rugero rwa 8 % ndetse zigira uruhare rwa 49 % muri GDP .
Mu 2016 , uwari Minisitiri w' imari n' igenamigambi , Claver Gatete yavuze ko gahunda ya leta ijyanye no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga yagize uruhare runini mu kuzamura umusaruro mbumbe w' igihugu nk' aho ibijyanye na hotel na restaurant zabigizemo uruhare runini .
Guhera muri Nyakanga 2018 kugeza Gashyantare 2019 , u Rwanda rwari rumaze kwinjiza miliyoni 52 z' amadolari ( asaga miliyari 46 Frw ) avuye mu gutegura no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga .
Mu mwaka w' ingengo y' imari ushize ( 2018 / 2019 ) igihugu cyari cyihaye intego yo kwinjiza miliyoni 74 z' amadolari mu bikorwa byo gutegura no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga , avuye kuri miliyoni 42 zinjijwe mu 2017 .
Kugeza ubu muri Kigali hari ibyumba bya hoteli z' inyenyeri ebyiri kugeza kuri eshanu bisaga 5000 , washyiramo ibindi byumba by' inzu zigezweho zishobora gucumbikira abantu Kigali ifite bikagera ku 10 000 .
Ubucuruzi budandaza n' ubugurisha ibintu icyarimwe bw' ibyakorewe mu Rwanda bukomeje kongera umusaruro wa serivisi , aho mu 2019 bwiyongereye ku kigero cya 16 % .
Ubwikorezi bwazamutse ku kigero cya 12 % ahanini bitewe n' ubwikorezi bwo mu kirere bwazamutse ku kigero cya 17 % .
Serivisi z' imari zazamutse ku kigero cya 8 % naho serivisi za hoteli na za restaurant zizamuka ku gipimo cya 10 % .
Inganda zifatiye runini ubukungu
Kuva mu 2015 , urwego rw' inganda rwagize ingufu nyinshi cyane mu bukungu bw' igihugu kuko ari bwo gahunda ya Made in Rwanda , yatangiraga gushyirwa mu bikorwa mu buryo buhamye .
Icyo gihe umusaruro w' inganda wazamutse ku kigero cya 7 % .
Muri buri turere kandi hashyizweho ibyanya byihariye by' inganda , ndetse no mu Mujyi wa Kigali , iki cyanya gishyirwa i Masoro mu Karere ka Gasabo .
Mu 2016 inganda zazamutse ku kigero cya 7 % , gahunda ya Made in Rwanda igira uruhare rukomeye cyane kuko inganda zikora imyenda , inkweto n' ibindi bituruka ku ruhu byiyongereye ku rugero rwa 10 % , izikora ibyo kurya ziyongera ku rugero rwa 8 % , naho inganda zikora ibikoresho by' ubwubatsi harimo isima ziyongeraho 21 % .
Mu 2017 inganda zazamutse ku kigero cya 4 % , mu 2018 zizamuka ku 10 % naho mu 2019 umusaruro uzamuka kuri 16 % .
Mu 2019 , izamuka ry' umusaruro w' inganda ryatewe ahanini n' ibikorwa by' ubwubatsi , inganda zitunganya ibintu bitandukanye n' ubucukuzi bw' amabuye y' agaciro .
Kuri ubu mu Rwanda habarirwa inganda nto n' iziciriritse zirenga 800 zirimo inganda zitari zisanzwe mu Rwanda nk' izikora telefoni , iziteranya imodoka , izikora ibiribwa n' izindi .
Ubuhinzi bukomeje gutera imbere
Imibare ya NISR , yerekana ko mu 2015 , ubuhinzi bwazamutseho 5 % , ndetse bugira uruhare rwa 33 % mu musaruro mbumbe .
Mu 2018 , umusaruro w' ubuhinzi wazamutse ku rugero rwa 6 % , mu 2019 , wazamutse ku kigero cya 5 % , naho umusaruro wabwo ugira uruhare rwa 24 % mu musaruro mbumbe .
Ubuhinzi nka kimwe mu bitunze abanyarwanda benshi , bwakunze guhura n' imbogamizi zirimo kuba bushingiye ku mvura , yaboneka bukagenda neza yabura bukagenda nabi .
Ibi byatumye leta ishyira imbaraga muri gahunda yo kuhira aho kugeza ubu hegitari zirenga ibihumbi 68 zuhirwa .
Gukoresha inyongeramusaruro , guhuza ubutaka no guhinga igihingwa cyatoranyijwe byitaweho cyane .
Leta y' u Rwanda kandi yashyize imbere no gushyiraho inganda zongerera agaciro umusaruro ukomoka ku buhinzi n' ubworozi .
Umuyobozi wa NISR , Yusuf Murangwa avuga ko ' uyu mwaka wagenze neza kuruta uko byari byitezwe ' .
Ati " Ubuhinzi nabwo ntabwo bwakoze nabi 5 % nubwo haba hifuzwa ko biba byiza kurushaho " " " " .
Mu 2019 , ibihingwa ngandurarugo byiyongereye ku kigero cya 4 % , ibihingwa byoherezwa mu mahanga byiyongera 5 % bitewe n' ikawa yiyongereye ku kigero cya 7 % n' icyayi cyiyongereye ku kigero cya 3 % .
Kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus , ubukungu ku Isi hose buzagabanuka , ubw' u Rwanda byitezwe ko buzazamuka ku gipimo cya 2 % mu mwaka wa 2020 buvuye kuri 9 .
4 % bwazamutseho umwaka ushize .
Icyakora kubera ingamba zafashwe mu kuzahura ubukungu , biteganyijwe ko ubukungu bw' u Rwanda mu mwaka wa 2021 buzazamuka ku gipimo cya 6 .
3 % na 8 % mu 2022 .
Amazon igiye kugura imigabane ya miliyari ebyiri z' amadorali muri Airtel
Ikigo gikomeye mu bucuruzi bukorerwa ku Ikoranabuhanga cyo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , Amazon cyatangiye urugendo rukiganisha ku isoko ryagutse ry' u Buhinde , kinyuze mu kugura imigabane y' Ikigo cy' Itumanaho cya Bharti Airtel , kinafite ishami rikorera mu Rwanda .
Ikigo gikomeye mu bucuruzi bukorerwa ku Ikoranabuhanga cyo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , Amazon cyatangiye urugendo rukiganisha ku isoko ryagutse ry' u Buhinde , kinyuze mu kugura imigabane y' Ikigo cy' Itumanaho cya Bharti Airtel , kinafite ishami rikorera mu Rwanda .
Ibiganiro byo kugura imigabane ya Bharti Airtel ntibiragera kure , ariko abasesenguzi bavuga ko bigenze uko impande zombi zibyifuza , byazamura cyane ubukungu bw' ikoranabuhanga ry' u Buhinde .
Biteganyijwe ko ubwumvikane bw' ibi bigo bushobora gutuma imigabane ingana na 5 % ya Bharti Airtel ijya mu maboko ya Amazon Inc .
hashingiwe ku buryo isoko rihagaze muri iyi minsi .
Bharti Airtel iri ku mwanya wa gatatu mu bigo bitanga serivisi z' itumanaho mu Buhinde igaragaza guhangana gukomeye hagati yayo n' ikigo cya mbere cya Reliance Jio .
Abantu batifuje ko imyirondoro yabo ijya ahagaragara babwiye Reuters ko uburyo Reliance Jio yakoresheje kugira ngo ibe iyoboye ibindi bigo by' itumanaho mu Buhinde na Bharti Airtel yabushobora .
Ku ikubitiro Amazon yari yifuje kugura imigabane iri hagati ya 8 - 10 % ya Bharti Airtel .
Gusa ngo kuko ibiganiro bikiri mu itangira [ ‚Ä¶ ] bishoboka ko n' amasezerano yahinduka cyangwa agaseswa .
Amazon iteganya ko yahita ireba ubundi buryo bujyanye no guhererekanya amafaranga bwazajya bufasha abakiliya ba Bharti Airtel kubona ibicuruzwa byayo bibahendukiye .
Umuvugizi wa Amazon yanze kugira icyo avuga kuri aya makuru , kuko ikigo ahagarariye kitatangaza amakuru ajyanye n' ibyo bazakora cyangwa batazakora mu gihe kiri imbere .
Gusa itangazo ryasohowe na Bharti Airtel rivuga ko isanzwe ikorana n' ibigo by' ikoranabuhanga bitandukanye bishaka kugeza ibicuruzwa byabyo na serivisi bitanga ku bakiliya .
Imigabane ya Bharti Airtel ku isoko ry' imari n' imigabane , kuri uyu wa Kane , tariki ya 4 Kamena 2020 yazamutseho 6 % nyuma yo gutangazwa kw' amakuru y' ibiganiro hagati yayo na Amazon .
Mu byumweru bitandatu bishize ikigo cya Jio gihanganye na Bharti cyabonye miliyari 10 z' amadorali kiyakuye mu bashoramari barimo na Facebook .
Alphabet Inc ya Google na yo iri gushaka uburyo bwo gushora imari muri Vodafone Idea ya kabiri mu Buhinde mu gutanga serivisi z' itumanaho .
Amazon iri kwirukira ku isoko ry' ikoranabuhanga mu Buhinde bitewe no kuba riri kwaguka cyane kuko umubare w' abatuye iki gihugu uri kwiyongera , ukaba ugeze kuri miliyari 1 , 3 .
Amazon iteganya gushora miliyari 6 , 5 z' amadorali mu bikorwa byo gucururiza kuri internet , ndetse ngo ikaba izoroherwa no gukoresha internet ya Bharti ku giciro gito mu gihe ibigo byombi bizaba byemeranyije amasezerano byifuza .
Mu Ukuboza 2017 nibwo Bharti Airtel ibarizwamo Airtel Rwanda yaguze imigabane yose ya Sosiyete y' Itumanaho ya Tigo Rwanda ibarizwa muri Millicom International Cellular SA .
Amasezerano y' ubugure yasinyiwe i New Delhi mu Buhinde , yahaye Airtel Rwanda kwegukana 100 % by' imigabane yose ya Tigo Rwanda .
Bharti Airtel ni ikigo gikomeye ku Isi mu bijyanye n' itumanaho gifite abakiliya barenga miliyoni 403 mu bihugu 18 bya Afurika na Aziya gikoreramo .
Icyayi cy' u Rwanda cyinjije asaga miliyari 25 Frw mu mezi atatu ya 2020
Mu mezi atatu abanza ya 2020 , u Rwanda rwohereje mu mahanga icyayi kingana na toni 9 .
3 zifite agaciro k' amafaranga asaga miliyari 25 Frw , yiyongereye ku kigero cya 27 % ugereranyije n' ayinjiye mu gihe nk' iki mu mwaka wari wabanje , naho ingano y' ibyoherejwe yo yiyongera kuri 15 % .
Mu mezi atatu abanza ya 2020 , u Rwanda rwohereje mu mahanga icyayi kingana na toni 9 .
3 zifite agaciro k' amafaranga asaga miliyari 25 Frw , yiyongereye ku kigero cya 27 % ugereranyije n' ayinjiye mu gihe nk' iki mu mwaka wari wabanje , naho ingano y' ibyoherejwe yo yiyongera kuri 15 % .
Imibare itangazwa n' Ikigo cy' Igihugu gishinzwe guteza Imbere Ibyoherezwa mu Mahanga bikomoka ku Buhinzi , NAEB , igaragaza ko hagati ya Mutarama na Werurwe 2020 , icyayi cyoherejwe mu mahanga ari ibiro 9 .
436 bifite agaciro k' amadolari 27 .
861 ni ukuvuga asaga miliyari zisaga 25 .
Imibare yo mu 2019 igaragaza ko mu mezi atanu ya mbere y' uyu mwaka w' ingengo y' imari watangiye muri Nyakanga 2019 , inyungu yavuye mu buhinzi bw' icyayi yari yazamutseho 8 % igera kuri miliyoni $ 36 .
08 , ni ukuvuga asaga miliyari 33 .
Kuva muri Nyakanga kugeza mu Ugushyingo 2019 , umusaruro w' icyayi cy' u Rwanda wazamutseho 12 % naho icyoherejwe mu mahanga cyiyongereyeho 4 % , ugereranyije n' igihe nk' icyo mu mwaka wa 2018 .
Hagati ya Nyakanga na Ugushyingo 2019 habonetse umusaruro wa toni 12 .
017 z' icyayi , ziruta toni 10 .
769 zabonetse mu gihe nk' icyo mu mwaka wa 2018 .
Icyo gihe byagaragazwaga kandi ko icyayi cy' u Rwanda cyatunganyijwe cyiyongereyeho 4 % , kiva kuri toni 12 .
180 zabonetse mu 2018 zigera kuri toni 12 .
617 mu 2019 .
Mu gihe nk' icyo kandi mu 2019 , icyayi cyoherejwe mu mahanga cyinjije $ 36 , 088 , 761 , bingana n' izamuka rya 8 % , zivuye kuri $ 33 , 562 , 294 mu mwaka wabanje .
Imibare ya NAEB igaragaza ko intego ari uko mu mwaka wa 2024 , icyayi cy' u Rwanda kizaba cyinjiriza igihugu miliyoni 209 z' amadolari .
Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr Uzziel Ndagijimana , aherutse gutangaza ko kubera Coronavirus , muri iki gihe ibyoherezwa mu mahanga bishobora kuzagabanuka , ariko ko mu gihe iki cyorezo kizaba cyarangiye , ibintu bishobora kujya mu buryo .
Yavuze ko ku isoko muri iki gihe ibiciro by' ikawa bihagaze neza nubwo ubu atari igihe cy' umusaruro , gusa iby' icyayi byo biri kugenda bigabanuka ku isoko .
Mu kugabanya icyuho kiri hagati y' ibyoherezwa mu mahanga n' ibitumizwayo , u Rwanda rurateganya gukomeza guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda , Abanyarwanda bagakangukira kubigura kugira ngo bisimbure ibyo hanze .
Minisitiri Dr Ndagijimana yavuze ko ubu igipimo cy' ubukungu bw' u Rwanda kigaragaza ko butazazamuka ku kigero cya 8 % nk' uko byari byitezwe , aho ubu imibare yagiye ivugururwa ikava kuri 5 .
1 % , nyuma biramanuka bigera kuri 3 .

Umwuka w' intambara ukomeje gututumba hagati ya Amerika na Iran
Nyuma y' igitero cyagabwe na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu rukerera rwo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , kigahitana Gen Qasem Soleimani , wari usanzwe ayobora umutwe udasanzwe w' ingabo zirinda abategetsi bakomeye muri Iran ; impungenge n' ubwoba bw' intambara bikomeje kwiyongera ku batari bake bakurikiranira hafi politiki ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , ndetse n' abatuye mu burasirazuba bwo hagati .
Nyuma y' igitero cyagabwe na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu rukerera rwo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , kigahitana Gen Qasem Soleimani , wari usanzwe ayobora umutwe udasanzwe w' ingabo zirinda abategetsi bakomeye muri Iran ; impungenge n' ubwoba bw' intambara bikomeje kwiyongera ku batari bake bakurikiranira hafi politiki ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , ndetse n' abatuye mu burasirazuba bwo hagati .
Iki gitero cyategetswe na Perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , Donald Trump , cyanahitanye Abu Mahdi al - Muhandis , wari umuyobozi wungirije w' umutwe bivugwa ko ufashwa na Iran witwa ( Popular Mobilization Forces ) , ibiro by' ubutasi bya Amerika ( CIA ) byemeje ko ariwo wateguye ukanagaba igitero kuri Ambasade ya Amerika mu mujyi wa Bagdad mu minsi ishize .
Gen Qasem Soleimani na Abu Mahdi al - Muhandis barasiwe ku kibuga cy' indege cya Iraq i Bagdad , bari mu modoka hamwe n' abandi bantu batanu .
Umuyobozi w' ikirenga muri Iran , Ayatollah Ali Khamenei , wahise ategeka iminsi itatu y' icyunamo mu gihugu hose , yavuze ko hateganyijwe kwihorera gukomeye ku bishe Gen Qasem Soleimani .
Perezida wa Iran , Hassan Rouhani , na we yashimangiye ko igihugu cye kizakora ibishoboka byose kikihorera , aho yunganiwe na minisitiri w' ububanyi n' amahanga muri Iran , Javad Zarif , wavuze ko igitero cya Amerika ari icy' iterabwoba .
Ati " Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika zizirengera ingaruka z' ubujiji bwazo .
Gen Qasem Soleimani yakundwaga kandi agafatwaga n' abanya - Iran benshi nk' umwe mu bantu bashobora kurinda ubusugire bw' igihugu cyabo .
Ubuhangange bwe kandi bwareberwaga mu ishusho y' uko yafatwaga nka nomero ya kabiri mu bafata ibyemezo muri Iran .
Abasesenguzi bavuga iki kuri uyu mwuka w' intambara ?
Abademokarate benshi bavuga ko icyemezo cya Trump gishobora gutuma intambara yeruye irota , kandi bakamunenga ko yagifashe atabanje kugisha inama Inteko Ishinga Amategeko .
Kuba Soleimani yari umwanzi wa Amerika hari abademokarate babyemeza ariko bakavuga ko kwica umuntu wa kabiri ukomeye muri Iran kandi bigakorwa nta bwumvikane n' Inteko ishinga amategeko ari ikosa rishobora gushyira akarere kose Iran ihereremo mu ntambara .
Joe Biden wabaye Visi perezida wa Amerika ku ngoma ya Barrack Obama , we yeruye avuga ko Trump yakojeje agati mu ntozi .
Andrew Yang uteganya kwiyamamaza ku mwanya w' umukuru w' igihugu , ahagarariye ishyaka ry' abademokarate yagize ati " Uko mbibona turashaka intambara na Iran ariko nsanga byaba byiza turebye kure tukirinda gushyira abaturage bacu batuye muri kariya karere mu kaga ko kwibasirwa n' abanzi bacu .
Elizabeth Warren , na we wifuza kuzahagararira ishyaka ry' abademokarate mu matora , yavuze ko icyemezo cya Trump kitarimo ubushishozi .
Ati " Soleimani yari umwicanyi , wahitanye ubuzima bw' abantu benshi barimo n' amagana y' abanyamerika , ariko iki cyemezo kitarimo ubushishozi cyazamuye umwuka w' intambara hagati yacu na Iran , kandi gishobora gutuma hapfa abantu benshi mu karere ko mu burasirazuba bwo hagati Iran iherereyemo .
Icy' ingenzi cyari gikwiye ni ukwirinda indi ntambara .
Minisitiri w' ububanyi n' amahanga w' u Burusiya , busanzwe ari umuterankunga wa mbere wa Iran , yavuze ko igitero cya Amerika kirongera ibibazo mu burasirazuba bwo hagati .
Ku rundi ruhande ariko aba ' republicains ' bo bavuga ko kwica uwo mugabo byari amahitamo akwiye kuko yari afite amaraso y' abanyamerika mu biganza bye , kandi yari imbogamizi ikomeye ku mutekano w' abanyamerika babarizwa mu karere ko mu burasirazuba bwo hagati n' inyungu zabo .
Lindsey Graham , umusenateri uhagarariye leta ya Carolina y' Epfo yagize ati " Wakoze bwana Perezida kubwo guhagararira Amerika .
Iki gikorwa cya Perezida Trump n' ingabo zacu , ni igisubizo nyacyo ku bushotoranyi bwa Iran bwari burangajwe imbere na Gen Soleimani n' abamushyigikiye .
Yongeyeho ati " Niba Iran ikomeje gutera Amerika n' abadushyigikiye , bagomba kubyishyura ku kiguzi kinini , kirimo no gusenya amariba yabo ya peteroli .
Kuri leta ya Iran , niba mushaka kuguma mu bucuruzi bwa peteroli , mureke Amerika n' abadushyigikiye , kandi muhagarike gutera inkunga imitwe y' iterabwoba hirya no hino ku isi .
Hari amakuru avuga ko iki gitero cyahitanye Gen Soleimani , ingabo za Israel zaba zakigizemo uruhare .
Nta muyobozi n' umwe muri Israel wari wagira icyo avuga kuri iki gitero kuko abaminisitiri bose babujijwe kugira icyo babivugaho kuko bishobora gukururira akaga icyo gihugu .
Umutwe wa Hezbollah ubarizwa muri Liban , ukaba ushyigikiwe na Iran wahamagariye isi yose guhuriza hamwe bagahorera urupfu rwa Gen Soleimani .
Umuyobozi w' uyu mutwe , Sayyed Hassan Nasrallah , yagize ati " Intego ya Leta Zunze Ubummwe za Amerika mu karere ntikwiye kugerwaho binyuze mu cyaha gikomeye cyo kwicwa abajenerali .
Minisitiri w' intebe wa Israel wari mu ruzinduko mu Bugereki , yahise arusubika rutarangiye nyuma yo kumva urupfu rwa Gen Soleimani , mu gihe Naftali Bennett , wari wamusigariyeho yahise atumiza inama y' igitaraganya yigaga ku mutekano i Tel Aviv , ndetse na za ambasade n' ibiro bihagarariye inyungu z' ibindi bihugu bahabwa umuburo wo ku rwego rwo hejuru .
Minisitiri w' ububanyi n' amahanga w' u Bufaransa , Amelie de Montchalin , yavuze ko igihugu cye kizakomeza gukora uko gishoboye mu guteza imbere ituze n' umutekano mu karere k' uburasirazuba bwo hagati nyuma y' ibitero bya Amerika .
Ati " Ibiri kuba nibyo twatinyaga , umwuka mubi hagati ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika uri kwiyongera .
Mu minsi ishize Gen Soleimani yari yaravuze ijambo ryarakaje Amerika , aho yagize ati " Ndakubwiye wowe Trump umukinnyi w' urusimbi , ndakubwiye , umenye ko turi hafi yawe kuruta uko ubikeka .
Uzatangiza intambara , ariko nitwe dufite ubushobozi bwo kuzayisoza .
Ibibazo hagati ya leta ya Washington na Tehran byazamutse nyuma yuko Donald Trump akuye igihugu cye mu masezerano yo muri 2015 arebana no kubuza Iran gucura intwaro za kirimbuzi .
Aya masezerano yabuzaga Iran kwigwizaho ibitwaro bya kirimbuzi mu gihe cy' imyaka 10 , yafatwaga na benshi nk' intambwe ikomeye yatewe na Perezida Barack Obama muri politiki y' ububanyi n' amahanga .
Kuva mu gitondo cyo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , abantu benshi biraye mu mihanda yo mu murwa mukuru Tehran , bigaragambya bamagana urupfu rwa Gen Soleimani .
Ikindi kibazo kimaze kwigaragaza , ni izamuka rikomeye ry' igiciro cy' ibikomoka kuri peteroli hirya no hino ku masoko mpuzamahanga , ibigaragaza ko nubwo intambara y' amasasu itaratangira mu buryo bweruye , ariko iy' ubukungu yo yahise yaduka .
Ikindi kimenyetso cy' umugambi wa Uganda mu gutera icyuhagiro RNC
Mu gihe umubano w' u Rwanda na Uganda utifashe neza , Uganda ikomeje ibikorwa byayo byo gushyigikira imitwe ibangamiye umutekano w' u Rwanda , aho ibinyamakuru bya Kampala bikomeje ubuvugizi ku mitwe y' iterabwoba irimo na RNC .
Mu gihe umubano w' u Rwanda na Uganda utifashe neza , Uganda ikomeje ibikorwa byayo byo gushyigikira imitwe ibangamiye umutekano w' u Rwanda , aho ibinyamakuru bya Kampala bikomeje ubuvugizi ku mitwe y' iterabwoba irimo na RNC .
Kimwe mu bikorwa bishya , ni ikinyamakuru Daily Monitor kuri uyu wa 2 Kanama cyateruye kivuganira abarwanashyaka ba RNC baba mu Bwongereza , ko bashaka gutaha iwabo nubwo bashinjwa ibyaha bikomeye by' iterabwoba , ariko iki kinyamakuru cyagaragaje ko uyu mutwe ugizwe n' impirimbanyi za demokarasi zishaka impinduka .
Ni ibikorwa bidasiba kandi byiyongera ku kuba Perezida Yoweri Museveni aheruka kwiyemerera ko yahuye n' umwe mu barwanashyaka ba RNC , Charlotte Mukankusi ushinzwe dipolomasi muri uwo mutwe .
Iyi mikoranire ya Uganda ishyigikiye abagamije guhungabanya umutekano w' u Rwanda yagarutsweho kenshi , ko Uganda yahaye rugari umutwe wa RNC ari naho ukorera ibikorwa byo gushaka abayoboke mu banyarwanda baba muri icyo gihugu , ku bufatanye n' urwego rwa gisirikare rushinzwe ubutasi , CMI , abatemeranyije n' uwo mugambi bagakorerwa iyicarubozo rikomeye .
Ambasaderi w' u Rwanda muri Uganda , Maj Gen Frank Mugambage , yavuze ko RNC ari umutwe w' iterabwoba , ku buryo ibyo uvuga byose bidakwiye guhabwa agaciro .
Ni mu gihe abawugize bakabaye bakurikiranwa ku bikorwa uyu mutwe wakoze n' indi migambi mibisha ufite ku Rwanda .
Mu banenze iyi mikorere yo gukeza RNC kandi harimo Yolande Makolo , wibajije niba ubu ari uburyo bushya Uganda izanye nyuma y' imigambi iheruka kuyipfubana yo gushyigikira umutwe witwaje intwaro wagabaga ibitero unyuze mu ishyamba rya Nyungwe .

Uganda ikomeje ibikorwa bibangamiye abanyarwanda , byanatumye u Rwanda rubuza abaturage barwo kujya muri icyo gihugu kubera iyicarubozo bakorerwayo , kugeza igihe ikibazo cy' umutekano wabo kizakemukira .
Ku wa 22 CMI yataye muri yombi abakirisitu ba ADEPR Kibuye bagera kuri 40 mu murwa mukuru Kampala , ubu bafunzwe mu buryo butemewe n' amategeko kuko bataragezwa imbere y' inkiko ngo bamenyeshe ibyo baregwa , banisobanure .
Ni abanyarwanda biyongera ku bandi bafungiwe muri icyo gihugu , banangiwe gusurwa n' abahagarariye u Rwanda muri Uganda .
Ni mu gihe Itegeko Nshinga rya Uganda riteganya ko nta muntu ugomba gufungwa igihe kirenze amasaha 48 uhereye igihe yafatiwe , ataragezwa imbere y' urukiko .
Abarwanashyaka ba Parti Socialiste bakomeje gucikamo ibice bapfa uruhare rw' u Bufaransa muri Jenoside
Mu ntangiriro za Gicurasi uyu mwaka , abarwanashyaka 23 ba Parti socialiste ( PS ) mu Bufaransa bahoze muri Guverinoma ya Fran√ßois Mitterand , bandikiye umunyamabanga wa mbere w' iryo shyaka Olivier Faure , bamusaba kwihaniza umukandida wabo mu matora y' abadepite b' u Burayi , washinje Mitterand n' ubutegetsi bwe uruhare muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Gabon iri mu bihugu 44 byashyize umukono ku masezerano ashyiraho isoko rusange ry' ibihugu bihurira mu Muryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe , AU , azwi nka AfCFTA .
Ibihugu 22 bisabwa kuyemeza burundu ngo ashyirwe mu bikorwa byarabonetse ndetse biteganyijwe ko mu kwezi gutaha azatangizwa ku mugaragaro .
Agaruka kuri ayo masezerano , Perezida Kagame yabwiye abanyamakuru ko ibihugu byose bya Afurika bizi akamaro kayo ku buryo n' ibitarayasinya bizabikora .
Ati " N ' ibihugu bitarayemeza burundu si uko bitabona inyungu cyangwa ngo bibone ko ari ngombwa ahubwo biracyafite ingorane mu bijyanye n' amategeko n' ibindi bya tekiniki bagomba kubanza gukemura mbere yo kuyashyira mu bikorwa .
