Bush wa Amerika mu Ugushyingo 2005 .
Rudatsimburwa agaruka ku mateka ya Rusesabagina akavuga ko atari umunyapolitiki , ahubwo yari umuntu wakoreraga h√¥tel akaza kugirwa igitangaza na filimi bityo agatangira kwibaza ko uwo muntu uri muri filime ari we kandi atari we .
Ati " Ni ukwisumbukuruza gusa kandi nta bushobozi afite uretse ko yabonye abantu bamwumva kuko bibaza ko ari wawundi wo muri filime ariko mu banyarwanda nta kintu avuze , ntacyo bamuziho uretse ibyo ahwihwisa mu maradiyo gusa n' ahandi " " " " .
Akomereza kuri Twagiramungu , akavuga ko we yabaye umunyapolitiki kuva kera ariko ubu akaba ari ' umunyapolitiki wasigajwe inyuma n' amateka ' , kuko uko u Rwanda rwateye imbere ntacyo bimubwiye akiri mu bya kera yari yaramenyereye ku ngoma zindi .
Mu nteruro imwe Rudatsimburwa ati " Nta hantu bishobora kubageza kuko nta ruhare bafite no ku banyarwanda " " " " .
Umuzimu wasaritse abarwanya u Rwanda bazawukira ?
Si ubwa mbere abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi bw' u Rwanda , bifatanyije bagashyiraho amahuriro ngo bahuze imbaraga bagere ku mugambi wabo ariko bikarangira bishwanyutse ntacyo bigezeho .
Ingero ni nyinshi cyane .
Ntawe utazi uko RNC ya Kayumba Nyamwasa yashwanyutse .
Uguterana amagambo hagati ya Dr Th√©og√®ne Rudasingwa na Kayumba Nyamwasa , bari bahuriye muri RNC , mbere y' uko bacikamo ibice , byatumye n' abo bizezaga ibitangaza bacika intege .
Aha niho havutsemo amashyaka atemewe mu Rwanda arimo na RRM ya Nsabimana , nayo yacitsemo ibice mbere y' ifatwa rye kubera ubwumvikane buke , gusuzugurana no kutemera uburyo abayobozi bishyira mu myanya .
Hari kandi n' amatiku hagati y' abasivili n' abahoze mu gisirikare .
RRM igizwe n' abantu ahanini bavuye mu Rwanda bahunze ibyaha bakoze cyangwa andi makosa .
Twagiramungu ubwe nawe yashinze ihuriro ry' amashyaka atavuga rumwe na Leta y' u Rwanda ( CPC ) , ryari rigizwe na FDLR , UDR , RDI , CNR , na PS Imberakuri , igice cya gatatu .
Abarigize baje kunaniranwa nawe bamushinja igitugu .
Muri rusange iyo ugiye kwitegereza umuzimu wasaritse aya mashyaka , ni ugupingana no kuryana , buri wese arwanira kuba ku isonga no guhabwa ibyubahiro by' umukuru w' ishyaka cyangwa uzayobora igihugu igihe bageze ku butegetsi .
Rudatsimburwa yongeraho izindi mpamvu abashinga aya mahuriro ntacyo bageraho ari uko ikibagenza ari inyungu zabo bwite , kwitwaza iturufu y' amoko n' intege nke basanganywe .
Ati " Ubundi mu mvugo zabo usanga nka Rusesabagina afite akantu ko kuzana iby' amoko , RNC usanga ikibazo bafite ari umuyobozi mukuru .
Ni uguhuza gusa ariko ubona ko bafite intege ziri hasi cyane , bakibaza ko guhuza imbaraga byatuma bazamura urwego rw' imbaraga zabo ariko akenshi ubona ko kuba ari abantu bifitiye gahunda zabo bwite , birangira akenshi bashwanye kuko hari aho batazahuza " " " " .
Rudatsimburwa akomeza agira ati " Ntibafite ingengabitekerezo ifatika yatuma babona n' imfashanyo , birangirira aho .
Mu by' ukuri ( Twagiramungu ) , aba ashaka kwihuza n' abandi kuko nta bushobozi na buke afite , niwe wenyine wibaza ko izina gusa rikurura ariko hashize imyaka 25 uriya muntu ntabwo azwi , ntawe yakurura , nta na benewabo yakurura .
Avuga ko FPR Inkotanyi yashobotse bitewe no guhuza mu bitekerezo byari bifitiye akamaro abanyarwanda bose yaba abari impunzi n' abandi bari mu gihugu babaho mu buzima bw' ingoma ya Habyarimana .
Ati " Niyo mpamvu FPR yakuruye abantu n' ubushobozi bw' abo bantu .
Ikindi harimo n' abantu bafite ubunararibonye bw' uko niba byanze muri politiki hari uko babikora bakurikije ubushobozi bwo gushoza intambara .
Abandi ntabyo bafite , akenshi banafashwa n' abantu bashaka kugirira u Rwanda nabi ariko nabo kubera aho u Rwanda rugeze nta ngaruka yindi bifite uretse gukerereza iterambere ryabo " " " " .
U Budage ntibwakwicarana n' abahoze ari aba - Nazi
Twagiramungu n' abandi bafatanyije kurwanya ubutegetsi bw' u Rwanda , ntibasiba kumvikana bavuga ko bazagaruka mu Rwanda habaye ibiganiro .
Rudatsimburwa asanga ntaho ibi biganiro byahera kuko u Rwanda rudaheza kandi ruhora rushishikariza impunzi n' abari mu mahanga gutaha , bityo n' abo bashaka ibiganiro bakwiye gutaha niba hari icyo bahindura ku cyerekezo cy' u Rwanda , bakagikora .
Icyakora avuga ko harimo n' abantu kuganira na bo byagereranywa no kuvuga uti ' u Budage bw' iki gihe bukwiye kwicarana n' abahoze ari aba - Nazi cya gihe cya Hitler ' kuko abuzukuru babo babisabye .
Abo Twagiramungu yifatanyije nabo harimo abashyiriweho impapuro mpuzamahanga zibata muri yombi , Rudatsimburwa avuga ko nta kabuza uyu musaza agomba gufatwa nk' umuterabwoba kuko kuba yifatanyije nabo bivuze ko yemera ibyo bakora .
Kugeza ubu ikibazwa ni ikidasanzwe ubufatanye bwa MRCD na RDI Rwanda Rwiza buzanye ku buryo bidatinze abantu batazumva iri huriro ryatewe n' umuzimu wasaritse abarwanya u Rwanda , nabo bagacikamo ibice .
Bigenda bite iyo umudepite ageze mu Nteko ntatange ibitekerezo ?
Iyo havuzwe Umudepite nta kindi cyumvikana mu matwi ya benshi , uretse uwo umuturage aba yaritoreye ngo amuhagararire mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko atanga ibitekerezo by' impinduka zikenewe , ni nayo mpamvu babita intumwa za rubanda .
Iyo havuzwe Umudepite nta kindi cyumvikana mu matwi ya benshi , uretse uwo umuturage aba yaritoreye ngo amuhagararire mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko atanga ibitekerezo by' impinduka zikenewe , ni nayo mpamvu babita intumwa za rubanda .
Mu nshingano z' intumwa za rubanda harimo gutora amategeko abareye abaturage , kugenzura ibikorwa bya guverinoma , kwemeza abayobozi runaka , hari n' ibihugu baba bafite inshingano zo gutora abakuru b' igihugu .
Nubwo baba baratowe n' abaturage ngo babahagararire , mu bihugu bimwe birimo n' u Rwanda , usanga hari abaturage bavuga ko baheruka babatora ntibazongere kubaca iryera cyangwa bagatora amategeko atabanogeye .
Tariki 19 Nzeri 2018 ubwo yakiraga indahiro z' Abadepite , Perezida Paul Kagame , yavuze ko bagomba kujya begera abaturage , bakabikora nk' uko babigenza iyo babashakamo amajwi .
Ati " Igihe mwese mwamaze mwiyamamaza hirya no hino mu gihugu , mwabonanye n' Abanyarwanda , uko mwabagezeho mubashakaho amajwi ariko bizakomeza kubageraho mubasanga , mufatanya gukemura ibibazo bafite .
Mu nteko habamo imirimo myinshi irimo kwiga imishinga y' amategeko , kuyisuzuma , kuyitangaho ibitekerezo n' ibindi .
Akenshi abaturage bamenya ubushobozi bw' umudepite batoye bitewe n' uburyo abavuganira , ibitekerezo atanga ku ngingo zitandukanye zizanwa mu Nteko , kubasura n' ibindi .
Hari ibihugu umudepite ugeze mu nteko ntiyongere kumvikana ku ngingo zibangamiye abaturage agaragazwa , byaba na ngombwa akaba yahagarikwa .
Nko mu 2018 muri Kenya , ikinyamakuru The Standard cyasohoye urutonde rw' abadepite batajya bavuga mu Nteko .
Havugwaga ko hari Abadepite bicara mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko , ntibabe batekereza umushinga wafasha abaturage ahubwo icyo bakora , bikaba gusa gushyigikira imishinga yavuzwe n' abandi .
Iki kibazo cyazamuwe na bamwe mu badepite muri iki gihugu , batangiye bijujuta bavuga ko hari bagenzi babo bahitagamo kwisohokera , mu gihe abandi babaga bageze ku ngingo zikomeye zo gutorerwamo amategeko .
Depite Justin Bedan Njoka Muturi yabwiye abanyamakuru ati " Ntabwo nishimye kuko hari abadepite bagenzi bacu usanga birirwa bavuga ko bishimira ibyo bagezeho mu nteko , mu gihe mu by' ukuri ntacyo bigeze bakora .
Yavuze ko hari bamwe usanga batagaragara mu gihe barimo gushaka gushyiraho itegeko runaka , nyamara nyuma ryajya gutorwa ugasanga batangiye kwijujuta kandi batarigeze bagaragara mbere ngo baritangeho ibitekerezo .
Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Kenya yavuze ko 70 % by' abayigize wasangaga nta jambo bafata ngo batange ibitekerezo , bamwe muri bakaba baravugaga ko babiterwa n' uko babaga bakiri bashya mu nshingano .
Mu Rwanda bihagaze gute ?
Kugeza ubu Inteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Rwanda igizwe n' Imitwe ibiri , Umutwe w' Abadepite na Sena .
Kuva tariki 19 Nzeri 2018 umutwe w' abadepite wabonye abadepite bashya 80 bari muri manda izageza mu 2023 , naho kuva mu Ukwakira 2019 hatowe abasenateri , kugeza ubu bose hamwe ni 26 .
Nubwo bitoroshye kumenya imikorere ya buri mudepite , iyo uganiriye na bamwe muri aba bakubwira ko nubwo hari bamwe batavuga , ngo ni uburenganzira bwabo cyane ko nta tegeko rihari ribategeka kuvuga .
Depite , Dr Frank Habineza , usanzwe ari n' Umuyobozi w' Ishyaka Riharanira Demokarasi no kurengera ibidukikije ( DGPR ) , yabwiye IGIHE ati " Abadepite bose bafite uburenganzira bungana imbere y' amategeko , nta mudepite kandi ubuzwa kugira igitekerezo atanga , buri wese afite uburenganzira bw' iminota ingana , burya umuntu kutavuga ni umutimanama we .
Dr Habineza avuga ko ubwabo nk' abadepite badashobora kwicara ngo banenge umudepite runaka utajya utanga ibitekerezo , keretse wenda bikorewe mu mutwe wa politike aturukamo .
Ati " Ibyo byakorwa n' amashyaka kuko buri shyaka rigira umuhwituzi .
Nk' ubu twe nubwo turi babiri mu nteko ariko dufite umuhwituzi ari we njye , ubu mfite uburenganzira bwo gukurikirana umudepite wo mu ishyaka ryanjye iyo nta gitekerezo atanga cyangwa ntacyo avuga , ndamubaza nti ese wowe ko mbona utavuga wabaye iki ?
n' ahandi ubwo ni uko babikora .
Dr Habineza avuga ko ku giti cye intego yajyanye mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko , ni uko buri gihe aba yiteguye kugira icyo yavuga gifasha umuturage .
Ati " Nta tegeko ryacaho ntarivuzeho kandi na mugenzi wanjye uba muri PAC agomba kureba uko amafaranga akoreshwa neza .
Kuva mu 2008 , Depite Nyirahirwa Veneranda ari mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Rwanda .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko abantu bashobora kwibeshya ko hari abadepite batavuga kandi iyo bari muri komisiyo batanga ibitekerezo .
Ati " Burya hari ibintu abantu batazi , mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko akazi gakorwa mu byiciro bitandukanye , hari imirimo ikorerwa muri komisiyo abadepite bakajya impaka ku mategeko , nyuma akazashyikirizwa inteko rusange , aha ni naho abaturage bose baba babyumva kuri radiyo .
" Hari abantu benshi usanga bazi ko dutangira akazi saa cyenda mu gihe harimo inteko rusange ariko siko biri .
Tuba twatangiriye muri komisiyo saa tatu ikageza saa sita , nyuma saa cyenda tukajya mu nteko rusange .
Nyirahirwa yavuze ko muri ayo matsinda , hari abantu usanga batanga ibitekerezo , ntibabitange mu nteko rusange .
Ati " Hari abadepite usanga bavuga cyane mu mirimo ya komisiyo , mu nteko rusange burya hageramo ibyasuzumiwe muri za komisiyo ugasanga mu nteko rusange ntavuze , ariko hari n' abandi bavuga hose .
Icyakora , yemeza ko hashobora kuba n' utatanga ibitekerezo aho hombi kuko iyo bageze mu nteko , nta muntu babwira ngo azagende avuge cyane .
Ati " Nta muntu uza kuguha amabwiriza ngo vuga , wanamara rwose imyaka itanu utavuze kandi nta wazabikubaza .
Depite , Sheikh Harerimana Musa Fazil , Visi Perezida ushinzwe Imari n' Abakozi mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Rwanda umutwe w' abadepite , yabwiye IGIHE ko kugeza ubu nta tegeko rihana umudepite utatanze ibitekerezo , bityo ko utabikoze nta tegeko aba yishe .
Agira ati " Nta cyaha gihari iyo utavuze kuko inteko ikorera mu mategeko , iyaba hari itegeko rivuga ngo niba utavuze umwaka wose bigenda gutya , icyo gihe twaryubahiriza ariko noneho ubwo nta tegeko rihari , ubwo nabyo biremewe , ikitabujijwe n' amategeko kiba cyemewe .
Yavuze ko gahunda nyinshi mu nteko zibera muri za komisiyo , ku buryo hari abadepite benshi baba baratanze ibitekerezo , byagera mu nteko rusange akumva nta mpamvu yo kongera kuvuga .
Sheikh Harerimana yavuze ko bari kwiga ku buryo n' ibiganiro byabeye muri za Komisiyo byajya bica kuri radiyo kugira ngo abaturage babashe gukurikirana ibikorwa by' Inteko n' imikorere y' abadepite batoye .
Ati " Twamaze kuganira n' ubuyobozi bwa RBA ngo turebe ukuntu n' impaka zabereye muri Komisiyo , rimwe na rimwe zajya zinyura kuri radiyo Rwanda Inteko , ibyo turimo kubiganira bizadutwara amafaranga kandi ntaraboneka ariko niwo murongo dushaka kuzakoreramo .
Muri Uganda mu 2016 hasohotse urutonde rw' abadepite batajya bagaragara mu batanga ibitekerezo ku ngingo zireba abaturage , nyamara ari bo bahagarariye .
Mu badepite 427 bagize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Uganda , 82 ngo nta jambo na rimwe bari bakavuze , 51 bari baravuze ijambo rimwe .
Mu 2011 , mu Bwongereza ibinyamakuru byasohoye urutonde rw' abadepite b' abanebwe .
Icyo gihe bashingiraga ku mubare w' inama abadepite bakoranaga n' abaturage bo mu duce bahagarariye .
Baje gusanga Depite Sir Stuart Bell , yari amaze imyaka 14 mu Nteko , nta na rimwe arajya kugirana ibiganiro n' abaturage bamutoye ngo yumve ibibazo byabo .
Sir Stuart Bell yaje kwitaba Imana mu 2012 afite imyaka 74 .
Baringa ku cyiswe " balkanisation " y' u Rwanda kuri RDC
Ijambo " balkanisation " rimaze kuba intero n' inyikirizo mu mvugo y' abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , kuva Perezida F√©lix Tshisekedi yatorerwa kuyobora iki gihugu .
Ijambo " balkanisation " rimaze kuba intero n' inyikirizo mu mvugo y' abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , kuva Perezida F√©lix Tshisekedi yatorerwa kuyobora iki gihugu .
Aba batifuza ko amahoro agaruka muri RDC , bakomeje guhimba ikinyoma ko u Rwanda rushaka kwigarura Uburasirazuba bwayo , bagamije kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda n' Abanye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda .
Ibivugwa bisa no kureba filimi mbarankuru y' intambara zabaye mu kinyejana cya 20 mu Burayi bw' Amajyepfo , mu gace kiswe ' les Balkans ' , ubu kigizwe n' ibihugu nka Bulgarie , Croatie , u Bugiriki , Roumanie , Slov√©nie , Albanie , Bosnie - Herz√©govine , Kosovo , Mac√©doine y' Amajyaruguru , Mont√©n√©gro , Serbie na Turquie ; byari byarigaruriwe n' Ubwami bw' Abami bwa Ottoman , bukabiremamo uduhugu twinshi .
Igitandukanye muri uyu mwaka wa 2020 , ni uko ibi bivugirwa mu mihanda ya Kinshasa , aho ababiyoboye badakomoka muri Hongrie cyangwa Turikiya , bahora baririmba bati " balkanisation ntikabe kuri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Mu Karere k' Ibiyaga Bigari , ijambo ' balkanisation ' ryatangiye kuhumvikana mu mpera y' imyaka ya 1990 , ubwo u Rwanda na Uganda byateraga icyahoze cyitwa Za√Øre .
Abazayirwa bari bafite ubwoba ko abaturanyi babo babiri bagiye kwisubiza ibice bahoranye mbere y' uko Abanyaburayi bigabagabanya Afurika , ariko ntibyigeze biba .
Iyi mitekerereze yongeye kumvikana nyuma y' aho Joseph Kabila agiriye ku butegetsi mu 2001 .
Abamurwanya bavugaga ko afite inkomoko mu Rwanda kandi akaba afite uruhare mu mugambi mpuzamahanga wo gucamo ibice RDC , ibice byayo by' Uburasirazuba bikize ku mabuye y' agaciro bikomekwa ku Rwanda .
Kujya ku butegetsi kwa F√©lix Tshisekedi bigaragara ko ntacyo byahinduye .
Ubu iyo ntero n' inyikirizo biri kuzamurwa n' Ihuriro ry' Amashyaka atavuga rumwe n' Ubutegetsi ya Lamuka ririmo na Martin Fayulu watsinzwe mu matora y' umukuru w' igihugu aheruka .
Ibyavuye mu matora yari ahanganiyemo na F√©lix Tshisekedi byagaragaje ko yabaye uwa kabiri ariko Inama nkuru ya Kiliziya Gatolika muri RDC yo yavuze ko ariwe watsinze .
Yaba Lamuka na Kiliziya ntibigeze bemera ko Fayulu yatsinzwe .
Kubiba urwango
Ku ruhande rwe nka Perezida watowe , F√©lix Tshisekedi , yahisemo kuzahura umubano w' igihugu cye n' u Rwanda , mbere yo kohereza umubare w' ingabo za Congo mu Burasirazuba bw' igihugu ngo zijye kurwanya imitwe yitwaje intwaro yahagize akarima kayo .
Ubu Ingabo za Congo ( FARDC ) zimaze kwigarurira ibice byinshi byari byarayogojwe n' iyo mitwe ; ku buryo n' iyo gahunda yo kwigarurira ibice bya RDC iyo iza kuba ihari , icyizere cyayo ubu kiri kubarirwa ku busa .
Abarwanya ubutegetsi mu RDC bahisemo kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda n' Abanye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda kugira ngo bace intege umubano mwiza uri kubagarirwa hagati y' u Rwanda na RDC .
Ariko n' ubundi abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi nta nyungu bafite mu kuba amahoro yagaruka muri RDC .
Mu myaka 25 ishize , ikibazo cy' umutekano muke mu Burasirazuba bwa RDC cyafashije abari abami b' intambara kwigwizaho imitungo no kwinjira mu bikorwa bya politiki cyangwa igisirikare .
Urugero rwa hafi ni umutwe wa ADF - Nalu ukomoka muri Uganda , wigize nka ba kavukire , ukaba uterwa inkunga n' uwahoze ari umunyapolitiki ku butegetsi bwa Kabila , Mbusa Nyamwisi , ubu wituriye muri Uganda .
Uyu Mbusa Nyamwisi yanahoze ari mu ihuriro Lamuka , nyuma aza kwitandukanya naryo .
Mu gihe RDC iri kugerageza kwivana mu ntambara imaze imyaka irenga 20 , cyane cyane hashingiwe ku mibanire myiza n' abaturanyi bo mu Burasirazuba , abarwanya ubutegetsi bakomeje kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda , ariko si n' Abanyarwanda , ahubwo ni abo bita ko bakomoka mu bwoko bw' Abatutsi n' Abanye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda mu rwego rwo guca intege umubano mwiza hagati y' u Rwanda na RDC .
Igitangaje ni uko imvugo ya " balkanisation " ari ikirego kidafite ishingiro .
Mu gihe Umuhuzabikorwa w' Ihuriro ry' abatavuga rumwe n' Ubutegetsi , Lamuka , wanahoze ari Minisitiri w' Intebe , Adolphe Muzito , yagaragaje mu buryo bweruye ko ashaka gutera u Rwanda byanashoboka bakarwomeka kuri RDC ; uyu ni na we ushinja u Rwanda kugambirira kwigarurira ibice by' igihugu cye .
Nubwo bashinje Joseph Kabila gufatanya n' u Rwanda muri uwo mugambi akiri ku butegetsi , ubu bakaba bageze kuri F√©lix Tshisekedi , ubwabo bigeze gukorana n' u Rwanda mu bihe byatambutse .
Ibi bigaragaza ikinyoma gikomeye kandi cyumvikana .
Byongeye kandi muri gahunda y' ubuhahirane busesuye mu Muryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe n' ubusabe bwa RDC bwo kwinjira mu Muryango wa Afurika y' Uburasirazuba ( EAC ) , bigaragara ko kwigarurira ubutaka bw' ikindi gihugu byaba ari amafuti .
Aho gutanga ibisubizo by' ibibazo nyabyo Abanye - Congo bafite ubu nk' ubushomeri , kutagira inganda zihagije no kwangiza ibikorwa remezo , kwangirika kw' ibikorwaremezo n' ibindi bishobora gusunikira urubyiruko rudafite akazi kwishora mu byaha cyangwa kwinjira mu mitwe yitwaje intwaro , [ ‚Ä¶ ] abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi muri RD Congo bahisemo gushyushya imitwe y' abaturage babo bakoresheje
imitekerereze ishaje .
Gukoma mu nkokora u Rwanda cyangwa ikindi gihugu cyo mu Karere ntibyongera umusaruro ; ntibirema imirimo kandi ntibinazana ubukungu .
Abavuga " balkanisation " ntibigeze bakandagiza ikirenge ku mupaka uhuza u Rwanda na RDC , umwe mu inyurwaho na benshi ku Isi ; ntibigeze byibura banumva ubuhamya bw' abagore bahakorera ubucuruzi , bahambukira inshuro nyinshi ku munsi bashaka imibereho .
Ubukungu nyabwo bwa RDC ni abaturage bayo .
Muri Afurika yose , umutungo kamere ubyarira inyungu ibigo mpuzamahanga biwubyaza umusaruro n' abayobozi bamwe na bamwe bahabwa utuvungukira n' icyizere cyo kubarindira ubutegetsi bwabo .
Ku ngoma ya F√©lix Tshisekedi , RDC ifite amahirwe yo guhinduka igihugu kirimo amahoro kandi gitera imbere ; ariko kugira ngo ibyo bigerweho birasaba ko bigirwamo uruhare n' impande zitandukanye zigize ubukungu nyabwo bwa RDC .
Gushaka kwihorera ku Rwanda barugira umwanzi bahuriyeho ni igitekerezo gifutamye cyabafasha kwihuza ariko ntibirambe .
Iyi nkuru yanyuze mu kinyamakuru Jeuneafrique , ni ibitekerezo bwite by' umwanditsi Gatete Nyiringabo , umunyamategeko akaba n' inzobere mu burenganzira bwa muntu .
Minisitiri Mbabazi yatangije imurikabitabo rya 2020 , akomoza ku nyungu ziri mu bwanditsi
Minisitiri y' Urubyiruko n' Umuco , Rosemary Mbabazi , yatangije imurikabitabo ry' Igihugu mu buryo bw' ikoranabuhanga rizakorerwa ku mbuga za internet , asaba Abanyarwanda kugira umuco wo gusoma no kwandika kuko ariwo nkingi ikomeye y' iterambere ry' igihugu .
Minisitiri y' Urubyiruko n' Umuco , Rosemary Mbabazi , yatangije imurikabitabo ry' Igihugu mu buryo bw' ikoranabuhanga rizakorerwa ku mbuga za internet , asaba Abanyarwanda kugira umuco wo gusoma no kwandika kuko ariwo nkingi ikomeye y' iterambere ry' igihugu .
Iri murikabitabo ryateguwe na Minisiteri y' Urubyiruko n' Umuco ndetse n' Ikigo cy' Igihugu gishinzwe Ishyinguranyandiko na Serivisi z' Inkoranyabitabo , RALSA .
Muri uyu mwaka rifite insanganyamatsiko igira iti " Twandike ibitabo , bimenywe , bigurishwe mu Isi y' ikoranabuhanga " " " " .
Minisitiri Mbabazi yagize ati " Gusoma no kwandika ni inkingi ikomeye y' iterambere ry' igihugu cyacu , niyo mpamvu leta y' u Rwanda ishyira imbaraga mu gukundisha abanyarwanda uwo muco , hategurwa ibikorwa bitandukanye harimo ubukangurambaga bwo gusoma no kumurika ibitabo .
" Igikorwa cyo kumurika ibitabo ni igikorwa ngarukamwaka guhera mu 2017 kandi uko gikozwe hari intambwe iterwa mu ruganda rw' ibitabo , aho usanga abitabira kumurika bagenda biyongera .
Yavuze ko ibitabo byandikwa bikwiriye kuba bijyanye n' igihe kandi bifite ireme ku buryo bigira icyo byungura ababisoma .
Yavuze ko iri murikabitabo ari iry' abanyarwanda bose , ko bakwiye kuryitabira kugira ngo umuco wo gusoma no kwandika bawugire uwabo .
Yagize ati " Igitabo ntigisanza kandi n' ubumenyi ntibusaza , ni uburyo bwiza bwo kugeza ubumenyi ku bariho n' abazaza tubagezaho ubumenyi n' ibitekeerzo byubaka .
Iri murikabitabo ry' igihugu 2020 riri mu buryo bw' ikoranabuhanga rizakorwa kuva tariki 15 Kamena kugeza tariki 15 Kanama uyu mwaka .
Iri murikabitabo ry' Igihugu mu buryo bw' ikoranabuhanga rizakorerwa ku mbuga za Internet zitandukanye .
Ushobora kurigeraho unyuza aha .
Imurikabitabo ni igikorwa ngarukamwaka gitoza umuco wo gusoma no kwandika by' umwihariko mu bana .
Dutembere kuri Stade ya mbere yubatswe mu Rwanda yakiniweho n' Umwami Rudahigwa
Stade ya Rwinkwavu ni yo yubatswe bwa mbere mu Rwanda , iherereye mu Murenge wa Rwinkwavu mu Karere ka Kayonza , yubatswe iruhande rw' umuhanda .
Hirya yayo gato hahoze hacukurwa amabuye y' agaciro ndetse amateka yerekana ko ari ho hambere yacukuwe mu Rwanda n' Ababiligi .
Stade ya Rwinkwavu ni yo yubatswe bwa mbere mu Rwanda , iherereye mu Murenge wa Rwinkwavu mu Karere ka Kayonza , yubatswe iruhande rw' umuhanda .
Hirya yayo gato hahoze hacukurwa amabuye y' agaciro ndetse amateka yerekana ko ari ho hambere yacukuwe mu Rwanda n' Ababiligi .
Ni stade abenshi bitirira Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa [ Charles Leon Pierre ] watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 1931 kugeza 1959 , bivugwa ko yakundaga kureba aho bakinira umupira w' amaguru cyane ko nawe yajyaga acishamo akawukina .
Umunyamakuru wa IGIHE yatembereye kuri iyi stade aganira n' abakuru barimo Musafiri Kabemba watangiranye n' ubucukuzi bw' amabuye y' agaciro mu Rwanda , uyu kandi yari ahari ubwo iyi stade yatangiraga kubakwa .
Kabemba Musafiri ufite imyaka 102 yabwiye IGIHE ko igitekerezo cyo kubaka iyi stade cyagizwe n' umuzungu w' umubiligi nyuma yaho benshi mu basore bakoreshwaga mu bucukuzi bw' amabuye y' agaciro i Rwinkwavu , mu masaha y' ikigoroba basoje akazi batagiraga ikindi kintu kibahuriza hamwe .
Amateka agaragaza ko ubucukuzi bw' amabuye y' agaciro mu Rwanda bwatangiye mu 1930 - 1931 ubwo gasegereti yavumburwaga mu birombe bya Rwinkwavu na Rutongo .
Ababiligi ngo bazanye abakongomani 300 barimo na Musafiri kugira ngo bafatanye n' abandi basore b' abanyarwanda kuyacukura .
Uko Stade ya Rwinkwavu yubatswe
Kabemba Musafiri avuga ko iyi stade ijya kubakwa yari ahari ariko ko atibuka neza umwaka , gusa ngo byaturutse ku muzungu w' umubiligi wari umuyobozi mukuru w' abacukura amabuye y' agaciro ndetse akanaba inshuti y' Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa .
Uyu muzungu yazanye umukino w' umupira w' amaguru nk' uburyo buzajya bufasha abacukuzi b' amabuye y' agaciro kwidagadura mu gihe bavuye muri iyo mirimo .
Ati " [ Stade ] yayishinze hafi mu 1940 , yashinzwe n' umuzungu w' umubiligi wakundaga gukina umupira w' amaguru , Umwami Rudahigwa yarahazaga cyane nawe akishimira kubona uwo mukino , bigera aho bayishyiraho igipangu kiyizengurutse hose , twayikiniragaho nimugoroba no kucyumweru , ni nabwo Umwami yakundaga kuhaza .
" Yari stade nziza cyane ifite igipangu , hari ikipe y' abacukura amabuye y' agaciro hakaba n' ikipe y' abazungu , hari n' andi makipe yadusuraga ku cyumweru aturutse ahandi hantu hose bacukuraga amabuye , amakipe yacu yose yabaga afite abajyanama .
Uko abakinnyi bahembwaga
Kabemba Musafiri yavuze ko abakinnyi batahabwaga amafaranga ahubwo bahabwaga inka zabaga zatanzwe n' Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa .
Ati " Abakinnyi beza bahabwaga inka hamwe n' abatsinze ibitego , babanzaga kubatekera neza bakahaba ibiryo byinshi birimo inyama ubundi bakajya mu kibuga bamara gutsinda nanone bakababagira inka , undi witwaye neza nawe akagabirwa inka akayitahana " " " " .
Umwami Rudahigwa yacishagamo agakina umupira
Kabemba Musafiri yavuze ko Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa yari umwe mu bakundaga gukina no kureba uko bakina umupira w' amaguru , ngo rimwe na rimwe nawe yajyaga acishamo akawukina nubwo bitari cyane .
Ati " Hari ubwo yazaga inaha akizihirwa nawe agakina , yajyaga mu ikipe y' abacukuraga amabuye hamwe n' abandi batware , abazungu b' ababiligi nabo bakajya mu ikipe yabo ubundi bagakina gusa ntabwo byabagaho kenshi .
Kabemba yavuze ko guhera mu 1960 kuzamura imipira yaberaga kuri iki kibuga yatangiye kugabanyuka ndetse abaturage batangira gusenya urupangu bakitwarira amabuye kugira ngo bayubakishe .
Abaturage barifuza ko iyi Stade yavugururwa
Bamwe mu baturage bo mu Murenge wa Rwinkwavu bavuze ko bifuza kubona iyi stade yavuguruwe ikajya iberaho imikino ikomeye , abandi basabye ko hashyirwa ibimenyetso byerekana ko ariyo stade yubatswe bwa mbere mu Rwanda .
Bankundiye Alphonsine yagize ati " Turifuza ko hashyirwa ikimenyetso cyerekana ko ari yo stade ya mbere yubatswe mu Rwanda , binabaye byiza bayivugurura natwe tukajya tuharebera imipira ikomeye .
Buregeya Emmanuel we yagize ati " Leta ikwiriye kubungabunga iyi stade n' inzu ziri hano zubatswe icyo gihe zabagamo abazungu b' ababiligi , byose bikwiriye kwitabwaho ku buryo bishyirwa mu mateka y' igihugu cyacu .
Umuyobozi w' Ikigo cy' Igihugu cy' ingoro ndangamurage z' u Rwanda , Amb Robert Masozera , yabwiye IGIHE ko bari kubarura ahantu hatandukanye hirya no hino mu gihugu hari ibyiza nyaburanga ku buryo nyuma hazakurikiraho kubibyaza umusaruro .
Ati " Rwinkwavu hari mu hantu twitayeho kimwe n' ahandi hirya no hino mu gihugu , tumaze kubona ahantu harenga 600 mu Rwanda hose kandi ntiturarangiza gukora urutonde , aho tumaze gukorera ubushakashatsi no kwandika ni 145 , iriya stade ntabwo irazamo turacyareba niba akarere kabyifuza kuko tugendera ku byifuzo by' Akarere .
Yavuze ko nyuma yo kuhabarura aribwo hazakurikira icyiciro cyo gushaka uburyo hakwitabwaho hakavugururwa hakabyazwa umusaruro .
Kugeza ubu kuri iyi stade hakinirwaho ikipe ikina mu cyiciro cya kabiri y' Akagera , ariko hakunda no kubera inama zihuriza hamwe abaturage benshi .
RDC : Leta irashaka kugura inzu ya Papa Wemba ikagirwa inzu ndangamuco
Guverinoma ya Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo yatangaje ko iri kwiga uburyo yagura inzu yahoze ari iy' umuhanzi w' icyamamare Jules Shungu Wembadio uzwi nka Papa Wemba , igahindurwa inzu ndangamuco .
Guverinoma ya Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo yatangaje ko iri kwiga uburyo yagura inzu yahoze ari iy' umuhanzi w' icyamamare Jules Shungu Wembadio uzwi nka Papa Wemba , igahindurwa inzu ndangamuco .

Mu nama y' abaminisitiri , Perezida F√©lix Tshisekedi yasabye Minisiteri y' umuco n' ubugeni kureba niba Leta yagura inzu yahoze ari iya Papa Wemba , ikagirwa inzu ndangamuco izaba irimo na studio itunganya umuziki .
Itangazo rigira riti " Umukuru w' Igihugu nyuma yo kubona ko uwo muhanzi w' icyamamare , yamenyekanishije cyane umuziki wa Congo , yasabye Guverinoma kugurira Leta inzu ye yashyizwe ku isoko , igasanwa ku buryo bubereye inzu ndangamuco .

' Sinzatesha agaciro uwakansubije ' , igitabo kivuga amateka y' Abanyarwandakazi n' uburyo basubiranye ijambo
Umwanditsi Hategekimana Richard , Umuyobozi Mukuru w' Urugaga rw' Abanditsi mu Rwanda agiye kumurika igitabo gishya yise ' Sinzatesha Agaciro Uwakansubije ' kijya mu mizi amateka y' abagore mu Rwanda .
Umwanditsi Hategekimana Richard , Umuyobozi Mukuru w' Urugaga rw' Abanditsi mu Rwanda agiye kumurika igitabo gishya yise ' Sinzatesha Agaciro Uwakansubije ' kijya mu mizi amateka y' abagore mu Rwanda .
Gikubiyemo amateka y' abagore mu Rwanda rwa mbere y' ubukoloni , guteshwa agaciro mu bukoloni na nyuma y' aho ndetse n' uburyo bongeye gusubizwa agaciro nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Iki gitabo cy' amapaji asaga 250 kizamurikwa ku mugaragaro kuwa Gatanu tariki 15 Ugushyingo 2019 muri Kigali Convention Centre .
Hetegekimana usanzwe yandika ibitabo bitandukanye , yavuze ko iki gitabo kigaragaza neza uburyo mbere y' umwaduko w' abazungu abanyarwandakazi bagiraga ijambo mu miyoborere n' ubuzima bw' igihugu , bikavaho mu gihe cy' ubukooloni , muri Repubulika ya mbere n' iya kabiri , bakongera kwisanga mu buzima bw' igihugu ubwo Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yahagarikwaga n' Ingabo za FPR Inkotanyi zari
ziyobowe na Perezida Paul Kagame .
Muri iki gitabo atangamo ingero z' uburyo abagore bagize uruhare mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu n' umusanzu bakomeje gutanga nyuma ya Jenoside ngo u Rwanda rwongere kuba igihugu cyubashywe .
Aganira na IGIHE , Hategekimana yavuze ko yanditse icyo gitabo , kugira ngo yibutse abagore ko ubwisanzure n' ijambo bafite hari aho byaturutse , bityo ko bakwiriye kurinda icyo gihango bafitanye na Perezida Paul Kagame .
Ati " Mbere y' ubukoloni , Abanyarwandakazi bari bafite agaciro , bagagaragara mu buzima bw' igihugu ariko kuva mu bukoloni kugeza mu 1994 agaciro kabo barakambuwe .
Imiyoborere myiza ya Perezda Paul Kagame n' umuryango FPR Inkotanyi yasubije agaciro Abanyarwandakazi , bafata iya mbere mu kugirana igihango na Perezida wa Repubulika , biyemeza ko agaciro yabahaye batazigera bakamutesha .
Yakomeje agira ati " Ni igitabo kigaragaza amateka y' umugore , kikamwereka aho ari , aho ava n' aho yerekeza kikanamwibutsa igihango afitanye na Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame .
Muri iki gitabo , ijambo ry' ibanze ryasinywe na Madamu Ingabire Marie Immacul√©e uyobora Umuryango Transparency International Rwanda .
Hategekimana avuga ko yabikoze kugira ngo igitabo cye koko kigire umwihariko no kugaragaza uruhare rw' abagore mu iterambere .
Igitabo ' Sinzatesha Agaciro Uwakansubije ' kibaye icya gatatu cya Hategekimana Richard , cyabanzirijwe n' ibirimo " Intwari Mpinduramatwara Paul Kagame " " " " n' ikindi cyitwa " Urubyiruko dufitanye igihango " " " " .
Amafoto mpangano y' abami batwaye u Rwanda imyaka 870 n' abagabekazi babo
Hashize imyaka 929 ( 1091 - 2020 ) u Rwanda rubaye igihugu gihamye gituwe na bene Kanyarwanda .
Amateka y' igihugu cyacu muri iki kinyagihumbi gishize ni maremare bitavugwa , dore ko rwayobowe n' abami 28 bafatanyije n' abagabekazi 27 kuva mu 1091 kugera mu 1961 mu gihe cy' akaga kiswe ' revolisiyo ' , ubwo ingoma ya cyami yasimburwaga na Repubulika .
Hashize imyaka 929 ( 1091 - 2020 ) u Rwanda rubaye igihugu gihamye gituwe na bene Kanyarwanda .
Amateka y' igihugu cyacu muri iki kinyagihumbi gishize ni maremare bitavugwa , dore ko rwayobowe n' abami 28 bafatanyije n' abagabekazi 27 kuva mu 1091 kugera mu 1961 mu gihe cy' akaga kiswe ' revolisiyo ' , ubwo ingoma ya cyami yasimburwaga na Repubulika .
Hifashishijwe ibisigo by' Abasizi bisingiza Abami n' ingoma zabo ndetse n' Abacurabwenge bari abarinzi b' amateka n' intekerezo z' igihugu , hiyongereyeho n' Abiru bari abanyamabanga n' abagaragu b' ingoma , hakusanyijwe amateka y' u Rwanda kuva mu ntango yarwo ubwo Gihanga I Ngomijana yashyiragaho imfatiro z' igihugu kugera ubwo Ingoma cya cyami yasimburwaga na Repubulika .
Mu bakoreye mu ngata Gihanga I Ngomijana harimo ubuvivi bwe Ndoba watwaye u Rwanda ahasaga mu wa 1213 kugera 1246 arangwa n' ibitekerezo bihanitse mu bumenyi mu by' ibidukikije , inyamaswa n' urusobe rw' ibinyabuzima .
Muri make Ndoba yari afite ubuhanga karemano muri siyansi , dore ko ari nawe dukesha ibirangamuryango nko kuba Abasinga barangwa na Sakabaka , Abashambo bakarangwa n' Intare , Abenengwe bakarangwa n' Ingwe mu gihe Abega barangwa n' Ibikeri , byose ni we tubikesha .
Hari kandi na Ruganzu Bwimba watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 1312 kugera mu 1345 wabaye imbimbuzi mu ndwanyi zaranze amateka y' u Rwanda mu guhirimbanira ubuhangange bw' igihugu .
Niwe wagabye igitero cya mbere atera Gisaka yashakaga gusibanganya u Rwanda we arayitanga arayitera .
Ni we dukesha kurwanira ishyaka igihugu , cyane cyane mu guhangana n' abagomera umurage wa Gihanga w' igihugu gisangiwe .
Nta n' uwarenza ingohe Cyilima Rugwe , watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 1345 kugera mu 1378 , umutekerereza w' ubutabera bwunga mu mateka y' u Rwanda .
Ni we washyizeho Inkiko z' Umuryango , iz' Abunzi n' iza Gacaca agena n' uko ibihano bizajya bitangwa ku bagomye .
Yashakaga ko u Rwanda ruba igihugu kizira icyaha , abyubakira ku guhana igihango nk' uburyo bwo gukumira icyaha kitaraba .
Nta n' uwakwibagirwa Ruganzu II Ndoli , watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 1510 kugera mu 1543 wari indwanyi karundura , wadukanye amatwara yo guhangana n' amahanga adakunda u Rwanda akayagusha ruhabo , akarwagura kurusha abandi bami bose dore ko yarwometseho ibihugu icyenda .
Hari inzobere kandi muri dipolomasi Mutara Semugeshi , watwaye u Rwanda mu 1543 kugera mu 1576 , ni we mwami dukesha politiki ya mbere y' ububanyi n' amahanga , yubatse kandi imiyoborere ihamye mu kwegereza ubuyobozi abaturage aho yashyizeho inzego zisaga 75 nk' Intebe y' Abasizi , Abatware b' Ubutaka , Abatware b' Inyambo , Intebe y' Abahaditsi ( abavuzi b' amatungo - v√©t√©rinaire ) , Intebe y' Abahoryo (
Agronome ) , Intebe y' Abamotsi ( abari bashinzwe itangazamakuru ry' ibwami ) n' izindi .
Ni we washyizeho uburyo bw' imisimburanire y' Abami ku ngoma bijyanye n' inshingano zabo nk' aho Umwami Mutara yabaga ashinzwe kwagura ubworozi bw' inka yakurikirwaga na Kigeli wari umwami w' intambara , Mibambwe wari ushinzwe uburumbuke , Yuhi wari umwami usigasira amahoro bityo bityo .
Ntitwakwibagirwa n' abandi nka Cyilima Rujugira ( 1675 ‚Äì 1708 ) , wadukanye intero y' u Rwanda rutera rudaterwa , Yuhi Gahindiro ( 1746 - 1802 ) wazanye gahunda z' ubugiraneza nka Girinka na Kigeli Rwabugili ( 1859 - 1895 ) wacecekesheje ibihugu byashakaga kwiyomora ku Rwanda .
Mu mateka y' Isi n' ibihangange byayibayemo nk' Abami b' u Rwanda , benshi baburiwe irengero , amasura yabo aribagirana kuko nta buryo bwariho bwo gufata amafoto no kuyashyingura ariko ibikorwa byabo bikaba bikibukwa kuko basize imusozi amavugwa y' ibikorwa bihanitse .
Umushakashatsi ku mateka y' u Rwanda , Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , yahereye aho maze akusanya ibitekerezo by' ubuzima bwaranze aba bakurambere , yifashisha abahanga mu gushushanya bahanga amafoto y' abami b' u Rwanda , cyane umwami wa mbere wafotowe yari Kigeli Rwabugili mu 1894 , abandi bamubanjirije ntawe uzi neza uko basaga .
Aya mafoto mpangano y' Abami b' u Rwanda n' Abagabekazi babo , yakozwe n' umunyabugeni Mugisha Paul wize ku Nyundo , yashyizwe hanze bwa mbere mu gitabo " Intwari z' Imbanza , zubatse u Rwanda rugahamya igitinyiro " " " " cyasohotse muri Gicurasi 2018 .
Uko ubumenyi n' ikoranabuhanga bigenda bikwira ku Isi yose rero , abahanga bagiye bitabaza inyurabwenge maze bakazimbura amasura y' abo bantu babayeho mu myaka ibihumbi kugira ngo bajye bayifashisha mu kubavuga ibigwi no kubagiraho icyitegererezo , ariko batari za baringa cyangwa umuntu udashobora kubonwa .
Ni muri urwo rwego hariho amafoto ya Yesu , Mariya , Yozefu , intumwa za Yesu 12 , Musa wavanye Abayisiraheli mu Misiri n' abandi .
Nsanzabera avuga ko " Abo bagize ibikorwa bakora ku Isi n' ubu bikiri intangarirwa , kandi amafoto yabo mpangano akaba yaramamaye mu buryo buhanitse ndetse ntashidikanyweho ko aribo koko .
Nk' abakoze ishusho ya Yezu , icyo bakoze ni ukureba ku bikorwa bye , amateka yamuranze n' imyitwarire ye ku Isi , barema amafoto mpangano ye kugira ngo buri wese ajye abasha kumubona mu buryo bugenekereje .
Mu gushushanya amafoto mpangano agenekereje y' abami b' u Rwanda , hagendewe ku bushakashatsi bushingiye ku bikorwa byabaranze , uruhererekane - mvugo rw' ibyabaye ku ngoma zabo , imishyingiranire y' umuryango w' abami b' u Rwanda n' indi miryango migari y' Abanyarwanda , igenantekerezo ( Philosophie ) n' imyitwarire yaranze Abami b' u Rwanda ndetse n' ikigero cy' imyaka y' ubukure mu iyimikwa ryabo .
Nsanzabera ati " Ese niba umwami runaka yarakoze ibikorwa bikomeye mu kubaka u Rwanda , aho ntiyasaga atya ?
Iyo ni imwe mu ngingo yitaweho cyane mu kugenekereza amafoto y' abami b' u Rwanda .
Kuko kenshi imirimo y' umuntu isa n' isura ye , ikanahamya umutima wamuranze mu bihe byose .
Aya mafoto mpangano yanashingiye ku kigero cy' ubukure cy' abami n' abagabekazi .
Hari aho atandukanye mu kigero cy' ubukure bitewe n' uko hari abagiye bimikwa bafite imyaka ibiri , abari abasore b' ibihame , abahawe ingoma bakiri ingimbi n' abayihawe bakuze cyane .
Ni nako byagenze ku Bagabekazi kuko hari abagiye bapfakara bakiri bato , umwami agatanga , bakiri ibirongore , abandi ugasanga bari bakiri abagore b' amariza n' ibindi .
Intego ya Nsanzabera ni uko ababyifuza bakoresha amafoto mpangano mu nyandiko na filime zirebana n' amateka y' u Rwanda mu kwerekana amashusho y' abami n' abagabekazi .
Aya mafoto ni uburiza bw' andi yaranze u Rwanda mu bihe bitandukanye , azasohoka mu bindi bitabo .
Umusozi wa Kigali wasabirwagaho kugira Umutima w' u Rwanda
Abanyarwanda ba kera bahoranye umuhango mwiza wo gusaba Imana kugira Umutima w' u Rwanda .
Bakawusabira ku musozi wa Kigali bafataga nk' igicumbi cy' Umutima w' u Rwanda .
Ese Abanyarwanda b' ubu bawusabira he ?
Cyangwa se ntawo bagikeneye ?
None se iyo Imbuto Foundation igarutse ku bidindiza " Ndi Umunyarwanda " " " " , aho si ibyo iba ishaka kumenya ?
Reka twumve icyo Abacukumbuzi b' ireme ry' Umuco n' Amateka by' u Rwanda babivugaho mu bushakashatsi bwabo .
Abanyarwanda ba kera bahoranye umuhango mwiza wo gusaba Imana kugira Umutima w' u Rwanda .
Bakawusabira ku musozi wa Kigali bafataga nk' igicumbi cy' Umutima w' u Rwanda .
Ese Abanyarwanda b' ubu bawusabira he ?
Cyangwa se ntawo bagikeneye ?
None se iyo Imbuto Foundation igarutse ku bidindiza " Ndi Umunyarwanda " " " " , aho si ibyo iba ishaka kumenya ?
Reka twumve icyo Abacukumbuzi b' ireme ry' Umuco n' Amateka by' u Rwanda babivugaho mu bushakashatsi bwabo .
Umusozi wa Kigali n' Igenamigambi ry' ingoma inye ( Ubu twagereranya na Vision 2020 cyangwa 2050 ) .
Kumenya icyerekezo cy' u Rwanda mu myaka ijana ni byo bitwereka neza icyo ubusugire n' ubwigenge by' u Rwanda gakondo byari bisobanuye , bityo na none tukabasha no gusobanukirwa neza n' icyari ku mutima ( Philosophie ) w' abakurambere baremye u Rwanda bakarwubaka , bakarurwanira ndetse benshi bakanarupfira .
Aha tugiye kubona ko ubusugire n' imibereho myiza y' Abanyawanda ku ngoma eshatu bwategurwaga n' Abami bitwa Mutara na Cyilima mbereho nk' imyaka ijana .
Nk' uko musanzwe mubizi , mu mazina y' Abami atanu yasimburanaga mu bihe bine yakurikiranaga atya : Mutara , Kigeli , Mibambwe , Yuhi na Cyilima .
Aha biragaragara neza ko hagati ya Mutara na Cyilima hacagamo Ingoma eshatu mbere y' uko Cyilima atangiza ikindi cyiciro cy' Abami .
Inshingano z' abami Kigeli na Mibambwe zabaga ari ukwagura u Rwanda kuko ku ngoma eshatu zabaga zarabanje Inka n' Abantu byabaga byaragwiriye bityo hakaba haragombaga kuboneka uruhumekero habayeho kwagura ubutaka bw' igihugu .
Yuhi yari ashinzwe imihango y' i Bwami cyane cyane Umuriro waho utarazimaga ukaba wararangaga ubusugire bw' igihugu .
Aha murumva ko Yuhi yari ashinzwe gutunganya ibijyanye n' ubusugire bw' igihugu n' ibijyanye n' imiyoborere myiza kimwe n' Iyobokamana kugira ngo abandi bami bane babone urufatiro rukomeye bazubakiraho .
Ubwo hari aho bitaniye cyane n' ibikorwa ubu mu igenamigambi rirerire ?
Yaba Yuhi , Kigeli na Mibambwe uko ari batatu babanzirizwaga kandi bagaherukwa na Mutara cyangwa na Cyilima .
Musenyeri Kagame yaragaragaje ko mu Rwanda Ingoma eshatu zamaraga imyaka 100 kuko buri yose yari imyaka yegereye 33 .
Mbese ni ukuvugako kuva Mutara cyangwa Cyilima batanze kugera hongera kwima undi Mutara cyangwa undi Cyilima ; muri rusange habaga hashize imyaka 100 .
Umuhango wo kwaka Umutima w' Ingoma
Mutara na Cyilima bari Abami b' Inka kandi bagombaga kugira umuhango ukomeye wo mu Bwiru bakoraga ujyanye n' icyerekezo cy' u Rwanda mu ngoma eshatu zigiye gukurikiraho .
Niwo mu Bwiru bita " Inzira y' Ishora " " " " .
Hari umuhango baheragaho wo kuvugurura Ingoma z' ibwami nka Kalinga , Cyimumugizi , Kiragutse na Mpatsibihugu .
Barebaga niba mu myaka hafi ijana ishize nta kibazo izo ngoma zagize kugira ngo bibaye ngombwa babe basisazura cyangwa se ngo bazisimbuze izindi .
Iyo basangaga izo ngoma zikiri nzima cyangwa bagasanga zigomba gusimbuzwa ; byanze bikunze bagombaga kuziha icyo bitaga " kuziha imitima mishya " " " " .
Iyo mihango yo kubonera Ingoma z' ingabe imitima , imwe bayikoreraga ahitwa i Karama ku murwa wa Kigali hariya ku musozi wa Mont Kigali aho bavuga ko mu mirwa yose y' Abami umurwa wa Kigali ari wo wari Imfura y' imirwa yose y' Abami .
Aho i Karama bahajyaga baje kuhatora imitima y' Ingoma z' ingabe arizo Cyiragutse , Cyimumugizi , Mpatsibihugu na Kalinga .
Mu gihe ingoma Kalinga yari Ingabe y' ubwami bw' u Rwanda , ziriya zindi uko ari eshatu zo bigaragara ko zari ingabe za buri mwami muri bariya Bami batatu bari hagati ya Mutara na Cyilima .
Bishoboka ko Cyiragutse ari ingabe ya Mibambwe maze Mpatsibihugu ikaba iya Kigeli bitewe n' uko bose bari bashinzwe kwagura u Rwanda nk' uko amazina y' izo ngoma abigaragaza .
Cyimumugizi ikaba ingabe ya Yuhi kuko ariwe wari ushinzwe imihango y' ubwami bw' u Rwanda nk' uko na none izina ryayo ribigaragaza .
Ibi rero ubona bimeze nka bya bindi by' Umwami Salomo wo muri Bibiliya igihe yajyaga gutambira ku musozi wa Gabaon nk' uko tubisoma mu 2 Abami 3 : 1 - 14 .
Ubwo Salomo yariho atamba Imana yaramubonekeye imubwira kuyisaba icyo ashaka maze Salomo ayisaba ubwenge kugira ngo agire ubushishozi bwo kuyobora ishyanga rya Israel .
Uriya muhango wa Salomo wo gusaba Imana ubwenge ( Umutima ) bari ku musozi muremure nk' uwa Kigali urasa cyane n' ibyo Abiru b' i Rwanda bakoraga bafatanije n' Umwami nk' uko tugiye kubibona .
Iyo rero Abiru n' abandi banyamihango bageraga ku murwa wa Kigali babaga bazanye : Umutsobe w' isugi , Umukobwa w' isugi n' Umwenenyabirungu w' isugi , bakazana amata , inzoga n' imbuto bagatereka aho .
Hanyuma rero bendaga ya mata na za nzoga bagakozamo icyuhagiro icyarimwe bakuhagira igiti cy' umurama ( ngo gitere uburame ) babaga bazanye maze Umutsobe mukuru agapfukama agasenga avuga aya magambo :
Gahorane Imana Kigali .
Tuje kwenda imitima y' ingoma Ngo Umwami mu Rwanda agire umutima Ingoma mu Rwanda zigire umutima Abagabo mu Rwanda bagire umutima Abagore mu Rwanda bagire umutima Inka mu Rwanda zigire umutima U Rwanda rwose rugire umutima .
Aha murabona ko niba Ingoma y' Ingabe y' u Rwanda ari yo Kalinga iyo ibonye Umutima ugereranya Ubwenge n' Ubushishozi , Umwami wayimye nawe aba abonye umutima .
Na none Ingoma z' Abami ari zo Cyimumugizi , Kiragutse na Mpatsibihugu iyo zibonye umutima , ni ubutegetsi bw' imyaka ijana bw' Abami Kigeli , Mibambwe na Yuhi burangwa n' umutima .
Uwo mutima rero ni wo ugera mu baturage no mu nka .
Ibyo birangira ari u Rwanda rwose rubonye umutima kugira ngo rubone kuba umurame .
Ibyo bimeze nk' uko Umwami Salomo yasabye ubwenge Imana ikamushima ikamubwira ko izamuha n' ibyo atasabye nko kurama , ubukire , amahoro no kunesha abanzi bitewe n' uko yahisemo neza .
Ibyo Imana yamusezeranyije byose bimeze nk' ibyo Abanyarwanda bizeraga kubona bamaze kubona Umutima w' Ingoma .
Dore uko uduce tw' ubwiru dukurikira tubivuga :
Uri umurame umwami abe umurame Ingoma mu Rwanda zibe umurame Abagabo b' i Rwanda babe umurame Abagore b' iRwanda babe umurame Inka mu Rwanda zibe umurame U Rwanda rwose rube umurame
Nyuma rero yo kubona umutima no kubona uburame ; ibyo ntabwo byari bihagije kuko u Rwanda rwose rwagombaga kuzira ubusembwa , kuvogerwa no guhumana ari byo bishushanywa na ba bantu b' amasugi bazanye .
Ubusanzwe umuntu w' isugi ni umuntu ugifite ababyeyi bombi cyangwa umukobwa utarasambanyijwe .
Muri ya masengesho y' Umutsobe mukuru yakomezaga agira ati :
Aya ni amasugi umwami abe isugi Ingoma i Rwanda zibe amasugi Abagabo i Rwanda babe amasugi Abagore mu Rwanda babe amasugi Inka i Rwanda zibe amasugi U Rwanda rwose ruhorane amasugi
Usibye imihango yo mu bwiru yo gusabira u Rwanda rwose umutima , uburame n' ubusugire , mu magambo amwe n' ayo tubonye hejuru , na none icyerekezo cyari ukugira ubuhoro ( amahoro ) mu Rwanda rw' Umwami .
Umwami w' i Rwanda agira ubuhoro Ingoma z' i Rwanda zigira ubuhoro , Abagabo b' i Rwanda bagira ubuhoro Abagore b' i Rwanda bagira ubuhoro Inka z' i Rwanda zigira ubuhoro U Rwanda rwose rugira ubuhoro
Nyuma y' ibyo byose u Rwanda rukagira uburumbuke bw' amata , ubuki n' inturire .
Ibyo nabyo babivugaga mu mugambo ahwanye n' ayo hejuru bati
Ng' aya amata n' ubuki Kugira ngo Umwami agire amata n' ubuki Ingoma mu Rwanda zigire amata nubuki Abagabo bagire amata n' ubuki Abagore bagire amata n' ubuki Inka mu Rwanda zigire amata n' ubuki .
Nyuma y' ibi , hazaga amasengesho yo gucyamura ( gukebura ) amahanga yose adatura umwami w' u Rwanda .
Dore amagambo bavugaga muri ubwo Bwiru :
Twacyamura u Burundi ku ngoma Twacyamura u Bushubi ku ngoma Twacyamura u Bunyabungo ku ngoma Amahanga yose adatura umwami w' u Rwanda Twayacyamura
Ibi twabigereranya na diporomasi y' ubu iba igamije gutuma amahanga yandi ayoboka iby' igihugu cyawe .
Amahame remezo y' u Rwanda gakondo
Iyi mihango yakorwaga n' Abami bitwa Mutara na Cyilima hari ibintu idusobanurira neza bigatuma tumenya Ihame - ngengabitekerezo ryubatse u Rwanda rikaruha Indangagaciro .
Ihame - ngengabitekerezo ni ryo soko y' ibikorwa n' imyitwarire by' umuntu cyangwa by' ikigo biturukamo .
Ni yo mpamvu nta muntu , nta kigo , nta shyaka nta n' ishyanga byabaho bidafite Ihame - ngenga - bitekerezo ababigize bagenderaho .
Ku gihugu Ihame - ngengabitekerezo ni ryo rigena kandi rikagenga Indangagaciro na Kirazira by' igihugu !
None abakurambere baturaze u Rwanda barwubatse babikuye ku rihe hame - ngengabitekerezo ukurikije ibyo tumaze kubona ?
Ihame - ngengabitekerezo rya mbere ryagenaga kandi rikagenga ibyo mu Rwanda byose ; ni iritumenyesha icyo u " Rwanda rwose " " " " ari cyo : " u Rwanda rwose " " " " ntabwo ari ubutaka bwose bw' aho twita mu Rwanda gusa ; ahubwo ni ahantu hari : Ingoma - Umwami - Abagabo - Abagore - Inka .
Ibi rero ni nabyo byerekana ibyo twabonye by' Ibanga ry' Umwami n' Ingoma , n' Ibanga ry' Inka n' Ingabo .
Aha icya mbere kigomba kumvikana mu Ihame ngenga - bitekerezo ry' abahanze u Rwanda , ni uko ahantu hose ku isi hari kuba haboneka Umwami wimye Ingoma - ngabe yahawe umutima , hakaboneka Abagabo n' Abagore ndetse n' Inka , habashaga kuboneka u " Rwanda rwose .
" " " " Kimwe n' uko ibyo byose uwari kubivana ku butaka bw' u Rwanda haba hatakaje kuba " u Rwanda rwose .
Impamvu ni ko ikihagira u Rwanda rwose ari izi ndangagaciro z' Abanyarwanda zihari tuzi ko izo ndangagaciro zari zubakiye ku Mana , Inka n' Ingoma .
Nk' uko Umwami yabaga ahatswe n' Ingoma maze Ingabo ( Abaturage ) nazo zikaba zihatswe n' Umwami ; ni nako u Rwanda rwose rwabaga ruhatswe n' Imana bitewe n' uko Ingoma yimye u Rwanda ari Imana yayihaye umutima .
Nk' uko Inka ihaka isabwa kubyara icyo ihatse ; ni nako Imana ihatse u Rwanda na yo isabwa guhora irubyara ( irugoboka ) .
Burya mu Kinyarwanda ijambo " gusenga " " " " risobanuye gukesha byose uguhatse !
Ni yo mpamvu usanga n' isengesho gakondo ryo gusabira u Rwanda na ryo ari ibyo ryabaga ryerekejeho .
Nimwongere murebe amagambo arigize :
Seka seka gasani k' i Rwanda Rusekere rugubwe neza Rusenderezemo amahoro n' amahe Rutsindire ubukenya n' ubugingo buke Rutsindire ubusame n' ubusharire Rutsindire icyago n' icyagane Rutsindire nyamunsi n' intumwa yayo Rutsindire umwanzi wo mu kirambi N ' umurozi uvuka ishyanga Garika ibiganza utugabire Rugaba , Rugabo , Rwagisha Maze twishyuke mu Rwanda umu .
Ihame - ngengabitekerezo ry' abahanze u Rwanda ni ukugira Ishyanga aho Umwami yima Ingoma - ngabe yahawe umutima ( ubushishozi ) n' Imana , maze ingoma ( reigns ) zikagira umutima ( ubushishozi ) bigatuma Ingabo z' Umwami ( Abagabo n' Abagore ) nabo bagira umutima uzagera no ku nka na zo zikagira umutima ( wo gukamwa no konsa izazo ) .
Murabona neza ko uru ari uruhererekane rw' Umutima uva ku MANA ukagera mu Mwami unyuze mu NGOMA - NGABE maze ukarangiriza mu NKA unyuze mu ngabo ( Abagabo n' Abagore ) .
Uru ruhererekane kandi ni rwo rwahoze rukoze " umutima w' u Rwanda rwose " " " " .
Byongeye kandi u Rwanda rwose iyo rwabaga rubonye umutima ; ni byo na none byateraga igihugu kugira uburame , ubusugire , ubuhoro n' uburumbuke ndetse no kugarura amahanga adatura u Rwanda .
Ibi rero abakurambere bacu bakoraga kera ngo bahorane Umutima w' u Rwanda ( w' Ubunyarwanda ) n' ubu mpamya ko bikenewe .
Kubura uwo umutima w' u Rwanda , w' ubunyarwanda ni byo byatumye abanyarwanda bishora mu mahano ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Ngo na Ruganzu Ndoli amaze kubohora u Rwanda amacakubiri yatumye rugirwa ingaruzwamuheto imyaka irenga icumi , yatangiye yigisha umutima w' u Rwanda .
Arwanya ba mutima - nda , mutima - rwana , mutima - muke , agakunda cyane mitimi - igwanye ( ihuje ) .
Ese ubu abo ba mutima - nda sibo batumye u Rwanda rutabohoka burundu ?
Imana tugira ni uko " imiyaga isubiza inyuma indege itwaye abanyarwanda itayibuza kugera iyo ijya " " " " nk' uko Nyakubahwa Perezida wa Repubulika aherutse kubyibutsa Abanyarwanda bo mu Rwanda rutugendamo !
Naho ibidindiza Ndi Umunyarwanda byo ubanza dukwiye kubirebera mu mizi yabyo mikuru twitabaje amahame - remezo yagengaga ishyaka ry' u Rwanda n' Abanyarwanda .

Hagiye kuba amarushanwa y' igisoro , umwe mu mikino nyarwanda imaze igihe
Mu rwego rwo guteza imbere imikino gakondo n' umuco nyarwanda , hagiye kuba amarushanwa yo gukina igisoro agamije kumenyekanisha no gukundisha abanyarwanda uwo mukino .
Mu rwego rwo guteza imbere imikino gakondo n' umuco nyarwanda , hagiye kuba amarushanwa yo gukina igisoro agamije kumenyekanisha no gukundisha abanyarwanda uwo mukino .
Igisoro ni umwe mu mikino gakondo yatangiye kumenyekana mu Rwanda mu mwaka wa 1510 ku ngoma y' Umwami Ruganzu II Ndoli .
Ni umukino ukinanwa ubuhanga bwinshi hifashishijwe insoro ( zimeze nk' utubumbe duto ) bagenda betereka mu twobo twabugenewe .
Ni umukino amateka agaragaza ko na Ruganzu Ndoli yawukinnye kuko hirya no hino mu gihugu hari ibimenyetso byamwitiriwe nko ku bitare bya Mpushi muri Kamonyi ahari igisoro , ikibumbiro , amajanja y' imbwa ze n' intebe yicaragaho .
Umuyobozi wa sosiyete Umutsakura yateguye ayo marushanwa , Nshimyumuremyi Justin yabwiye IGIHE ko amarushanwa yatangiye mu Ukwakira uyu mwaka , umukino wa nyuma ukazaba kuwa Gatanu tariki 22 Ugushyingo muri Olympique Hotel ku Kimironko .
Ababugu ( abakina igisoro ) babiri nibo bazaba bahatanira umwanya wa mbere .
Nshimyumuremyi yavuze ko igisoro ari umwe mu mikino y' umwihariko w' abanyarwanda , nyamara udahabwa agaciro kuko ufatwa nk' usuzuguritse .
Ati " impamvu yo gukora aya marushanwa ni ukuwusigasira .
Usanga indi mikino yarahawe agaciro ariko igisoro basa nk' aho bagisize inyuma kandi ari umwihariko wacu abanyarwanda .
Aya marushanwa ni uburyo bwo kugira ngo igisoro cyongere kimenyekane , cyongere gikinwe ndetse mu bihe bizaza nkuko abakina Football ibagirira umumaro n' abakina igisoro boye kujya bitwa inkorabusa cyangwa se abanebwe .
Yongeyeho ko " Hambere igisoro cyari gifatiye abanyarwanda runini .
Bagikoreshaga mu mibare .
Kubera ko bari bataragira irindi terambere rihambaye , iyo bakinaga barabaraga bati ndazana butatu nkurase burindwi , nongere nzane bune murase 12 [ ‚Ä¶ ] kumenya iyo mibare rero bigaragaza ubuhanga bari bafite .
Uretse kumenyekanisha uwo mukino , Nshimyumuremyi yavuze ko bashaka no kugikundisha abakiri bato kugira ngo bazagisigasire .
Kwinjira muri uyu mukino wa nyuma bizaba ari ubuntu .
Uzaba uwa mbere azahembwa ibihumbi 75 Frw , uwa kabiri ahembwe ibihumbi 50 naho uwa gatatu ahembwe ibihumbi 30 Frw .
Biteganyijwe ko hazanakorwa ibindi bikorwa by' umuco birimo indirimbo gakondo , imivugo n' ibisigo , ibyivugo n' ibindi .
Abategura aya marushanwa bavuze ko icyifuzo ari uko aya marushanwa yajya ategurwa nibura gatatu mu mwaka ubushobozi buramutse bubonetse .
Padiri Amerika agiye kumurika igitabo gitanga umucyo ku mpaka z' urudaca zishingiye kuri Bibiliya
Padiri Amerika Victor , uyobora Paruwasi ya Nyabinyenga muri Diyosezi Gatolika ya Kabgayi agiye kumurika igitabo yise ' Nzi uwo Nemeye ' gishishikariza abakiristu mu madini yose kumenya imvano y' ibyo bemera aho kuba imbata z' idini .
Padiri Amerika Victor , uyobora Paruwasi ya Nyabinyenga muri Diyosezi Gatolika ya Kabgayi agiye kumurika igitabo yise ' Nzi uwo Nemeye ' gishishikariza abakiristu mu madini yose kumenya imvano y' ibyo bemera aho kuba imbata z' idini .
Muri iki gitabo , Padiri Amerika yashyizemo ibice bitandukanye bishingiye ku bushakashatsi na Bibiliya , bigaragaza ukuri kw' imyererere abantu bajya bibazaho .
Avugamo inzira ikwiriye abanyamadini kuri ubu basa n' abarajwe ishinga no kurwana intambara zishingiye ku myemerere , ugasanga barwanira abayoboke kurusha uko bwaranira kwigisha ukuri kw' ijambo ry' Imana .
Agaruka no ku bibazo bigaragara mu muryango ariko bitavugwaho rumwe , nk' ibijyanye no kwihorera , gusenda abagore , kuboneza urubyaro n' ibindi .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na IGIHE , Padiri Amerika yavuze ko yagize igitekerezo cyo kwandika iki gitabo nyuma yo kwegerwa na bamwe mu bakiristu ayoboye akumva ibibazo bakunze kumubaza bigaragaza ko hari ibyo badasobanukiwe .
Yabihereye kandi mu gace paruwasi ayobora iherereyemo kabonekamo amadini menshi ariko ugasanga ashishikajwe no gushaka abayoboke asebya andi aho kwigisha ukuri kw' ijambo ry' Imana kuboneka muri Bibiliya .
Ati " Muri iki gihe abantu benshi baremera , dufite amadini atandukanye dusengeramo ugasanga umuntu yabaye uw' idini kuruta kuba uw' ukuri , agatsimbarara kuri bya bindi bemera ariko atanabisobanukiwe .
Yakomeje agira ati " Igitabo cyanjye ntabwo ari igitabo cy' idini , ni igitabo nanditse nk' umuntu uri mu buzima bw' iyobokamana ariko cyakwifashishwa n' abantu bose .
Padiri Amerika nko ku kijyanye no kuboneza urubyaro , agaragaza ko hari abagendera ku mugambo aboneka muri Bibiliya avuga ngo " Mubyare mwororoke mungane n' umusenyi wo ku Nyanja " " " " .
Yavuze ko nubwo Bibiliya ivuga ityo , Aburahamu ufatwa nka sekuruza w' abemera bose yabyaye abana umunani gusa mu gihe cye bishingiye ku bushobozi n' inshingano yari afite .
Ibyo bijyanye n' andi magambo yo muri Bibiliya , mu ibaruwa ya kabiri Pawulo intumwa yandikiye abanyakolenti , 12 : 14 handitse ngo " si abana bateganyiriza ababyeyi ahubwo ni ababyeyi bateganyiriza abana babo .
Padiri Amerika agaragaza ko iyo ngingo yereka umubyeyi ko kubyara ari uburenganzira n' inshingano .
Ati " Byara uwo ushoboye kurera , utazaba interagahinda akurushye , arushye n' igihugu .
Muri iki gitabo kandi umwanditsi agaruka ku buhanuzi bweze muri iki gihe cyane cyane ubujyanye n' igihe isi izarangirira .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko ntawe ukwiriye guhanura iby' irangira ry' isi atarayishyizeho , ko bikwiriye guharirwa Imana ari nayo yaremye .
Yifuza ko uzasoma iki gitabo asobanukirwa n' imyemerere ye ndetse n' itandukaniro n' iy' abandi ariko byose bikaba ibiganisha ku kubana neza n' abandi aho gushwana .
Ati " Tureke kuba abantu b' idini , ntabwo idini ari ishyaka .
Ishyaka rya mbere ni ukurwanirira kubana neza n' abandi , kugira ngo mugenzi wawe akugirireho umugisha nawe umugirireho umugisha .
Musenyeri wa Diyosezi ya Kabgayi , Smaragde Mbonyintege ni we wanditse ijambo ry' ikaze ry' iki gitabo .
Mbonyintege mu ijambo ry' ikaze , yavuze ko iki gitabo kije gukemura impaka z' urudaca ku myumvire ya Bibiliya mu matorerro atandukanye .
Ati " Impaka z' urudaca ku myumvire ya Bibiliya duhuriyeho n' andi matorero ndetse no ku Masakramentu bamwe mu banyamatorero bakunze kugoreka imyumvire , umwanditsi yabiboneye ibisubizo ku buryo bwumvikana .
Yongeyeho ati " Iki gitabo ndagishimira ko kitagamije kwinjira mu mpaka n' abagoreka ibyo twigisha , ahubwo gufasha mbere na mbere abakristu bacu gusobanukirwa mu mpaka z' ababarundaho ibisobanuro biyobya .
Iki gitabo kizamurikwa kuri uyu wa Gatanu i Kigali kuri Hotel St Famille , guhera saa kumi n' igice z' umugoroba .
Uruzinduko rw' amasaha arindwi Bush yakoreye mu Rwanda , rugasiga ishusho nshya y' umubano mu ishoramari
Ku wa kabiri tariki 19 Gashyantare 2008 , uwari Perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika George W .
Bush yagiriye uruzinduko rw' amasaha arindwi mu Rwanda , rusiga ibihugu byombi bisinye amasezerano y' ishoramari n' icyerekezo cy' umubano mushya .
Ku wa kabiri tariki 19 Gashyantare 2008 , uwari Perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika George W .
Bush yagiriye uruzinduko rw' amasaha arindwi mu Rwanda , rusiga ibihugu byombi bisinye amasezerano y' ishoramari n' icyerekezo cy' umubano mushya .
Yaje mu Rwanda asoza uruzinduko rw' iminsi yari amaze muri Afurika mu bihugu birimo B√©nin , Tanzania , Ghana na Liberia .
Bush yaje mu Rwanda ibibazo byasizwe na Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi bikiri byinshi , abapfakazi ba Jenoside , impfubyi , ibikorwa remezo bidahagije na gahunda z' imibereho myiza y' abaturage bikiri hasi .
Icyakora yaje u Rwanda rutangiye kwigaragaza , aho 95 % by' abana bagejeje igihe cyo kujya kwiga mu mashuri abanza bajyagayo na hejuru ya 90 % y' abana bavuka bahabwa inkingo .
Yageze ku Kibuga Mpuzamahanga cy' Indege cya Kigali mu gitondo , impande nyinshi z' umujyi umutekano wakajijwe .
Bush yazanye n' umufasha we Laura Bush , bahitira ku rwibutso rwa Jenoside rwa Kigali kunamira inzirakarengane zazize Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi no gusobanurirwa byimbitse itegurwa n' ishyirwa mu bikorwa ry' iyo Jenoside ikomeye yakozwe mu kinyejana cya 20 .
Amaze gusura urwibutso no gushyira indabyo ku mva ziruhukiyemo imibiri isaga ibihumbi 250 , Bush yavuze ko ibyabaye mu Rwanda bidakwiriye kugira ahandi biba .
Yagize ati " Aha ni ahantu hatitiza ibyiyumviro byawe .
Byanyibukije ko tudakwiriye gutuma ibintu nk' ibi biba kandi ko abaturage b' u Rwanda bakeneye ubufasha ngo biyunge , batere imbere nyuma y' ibi bihe by' ubwicanyi .
Turasabira umugisha uva ku Mana abagifite ibikomere n' abamaze igihe bakeneye ubufasha ndetse n' abana ubuzima bwabo bwashegeshwe n' ibihe banyuzemo .
Yongeyeho ati " Turashimira ubuyobozi kuba bwarashyizeho ahantu nk' aha hibutsa abantu ko ikibi ntaho cyagiye mu Isi kandi ko kigomba kurwanywa .
Avuye ku rwibutso rwa Jenoside , Bush yakomereje muri Village Urugwiro kuganira na Perezida Kagame no gusinya amasezerano y' ishoramari hagati y' ibihugu byombi .
Mu 2007 , u Rwanda rwohereje muri Amerika ibicuruzwa bifite agaciro ka miliyoni 13 z' amadolari ya Amerika , ruvanayo ibicuruzwa bifite agaciro ka miliyoni $ 16 .
Amasezerano amaze gusinywa , abakuru b' ibihugu byombi bagiranye ikiganiro n' abanyamakuru , Perezida Kagame avuga ko ayo masezerano ari ubutumire ku bashoramari bo muri Amerika kuza mu Rwanda .
Ati " Ni ubutumire ku bashoramari kandi tubabwira ko nibaramuka baje hano ishoramari ryabo rizarindwa neza ku buryo bazabona umusaruro w' ibyo batanze .
Yongeye kubisubiramo nyuma ubwo batahaga Ibiro bishya bya Ambasade ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , avuga ko gutaha inyubako nshya za ambasade bikwiriye kuba nka rukuruzi ikururira abashoramari bo muri Amerika kuza gushora mu Rwanda .
Ibirori byakomereje ku Kacyiru ku Biro bishya bya Ambasade ya Amerika mu Rwanda , bishimira imyaka ibiri yari ishize byubakwa .
Ni ibiro Perezida Bush yitiriye Martin Luther King waharaniye ubwigenge bw' abirabura muri Amerika .
Muri ibyo birori byitabiriwe n' abantu babarirwa mu magana , Michael Arieti wari Ambasaderi wa Amerika mu Rwanda yavuze ko uwo munsi ari uw' amateka mu mubano w' u Rwanda na Amerika .
Yatangiye yibutsa ko mu 2004 aribwo Leta y' u Rwanda yemeye kugurisha ikibanza ngo kigurwe na Amerika cyubakweho ambasade .
Yavuze ko imirimo yo kubaka iyo ambasade yakozwe n' abakozi 750 , barimo abasaga 650 b' Abanyarwanda .
Bush wari umaze amasaha make mu Rwanda , yahawe umwanya avuga ko bitumvikana uburyo igihugu cyanyuze mu bibazo nk' ibyo yari amaze kubona ku rwibutso , cyabashije kwiyubaka kikaba gitanga icyizere .
Yavuze ko ejo heza h' u Rwanda hashoboka cyane ashingiye ku muhate n' urukundo yabonanye Perezida Kagame .
Ati " Ntabwo byumvikana uburyo icyizere cyagaruka nyuma yo guca mu bihe nka biriya .
Abanyamerika turi kumwe namwe mu rugamba rwo guharanira ejo heza .
Nishimira kuganira n' abayobozi bakomeye bita ku baturage babo .
Nkunda umuhate n' urukundo ari nabyo Perezida wanyu afite .
Yita bikomeye ku bibazo by' abaturage be .
Yavuze ko kuba hatashywe inyubako nshya za ambasade , ari umukoro ku Banyamerika wo gukomeza umutima wo gufasha no gushyigikira iterambere ry' u Rwanda .
Ahagana saa cyenda , Bush na Laura bagiye muri Lyc√©e de Kigali kuganira n' abanyeshuri baho ibijyanye no kwirinda SIDA , ahava ahawe inkoni ya Kinyarwanda nk' impano .
Ubwo yageraga ku kibuga cy' indege atashye , yaganiriye gato n' abasirikare bari baravuye mu butumwa bw' amahoro mu Ntara ya Darfur muri Sudani , dore ko igihugu cye cyari kimaze iminsi gitanga amahugurwa ku ngabo zigiye kujya mu butumwa bw' amahoro .
Bivugwa ko mu ruzinduko rwa Bush , we na Perezida Kagame baganiriye ku mutekano wo mu Karere cyane cyane muri Kenya aho imvururu zakurikiye amatora yo mu Ukuboza 2007 zari zimaze guhitana abantu basaga igihumbi .
No mu kiganiro n' abanyamakuru , Bush yabikomojeho , avuga ko hatagizwe igikorwa ibiri kuba muri Kenya biganisha ku byabaye mu Rwanda mu 1994 .
Bush ni we Perezida wa Amerika uheruka gusura u Rwanda , akaba uwa kabiri nyuma ya Bill Clinton wahaje mu 1998 Jenoside imaze imyaka ine ihagaritswe .
Uruzinduko rwe rwongereye ishoramari n' ubucuruzi hagati y' ibihugu byombi kuko mu 2018 , ibyo u Rwanda rwohereza muri Amerika byari bigeze kuri miliyoni $ 67 .
4 , bivuye kuri miliyoni $ 13 mu 2007 ibyo ruvanayo biba miliyoni 425 .
3 bivuye kuri miliyoni $ 16 mu 2007 .
Ibigwi n' ibirindiro by' umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , mu gitero cy' Imigogo ( Igice cya mbere )
Abatekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda n' abayatekererezwa , bakunze gutangarira ibikorwa by' umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , wazengereje amahanga , akayagusha ruhabo , kugeza ubwo ashaririwe no kumva izina " Rwanda " mu matwi yabo .
Abatekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda n' abayatekererezwa , bakunze gutangarira ibikorwa by' umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , wazengereje amahanga , akayagusha ruhabo , kugeza ubwo ashaririwe no kumva izina " Rwanda " mu matwi yabo .
Muri iki gice cy' uruhererekane rw' inkuru twise " Ibigwi n' ibirindiro " Aho tuzajya tubakusanyiriza amateka y' ibihangange byabaye mu rwa Gasabo bifite ibikorwa bikomeye , tugiye kubavunguriraho gato ku bigwi n' ibirindiro by' umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , dore ko utabikuyeho akamanyu nibura gato gato , utashobora kubiva imuzi ngo ubigere imuzingo .
Nk' uko tubikesha igitabo " Intwari z' imbanza , zubatse u Rwanda rugahaya igitinyiro " cyanditswe n' Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere ku Muco , ubusizi n' amateka , tugiye kubatekerereza bimwe mu bigwi n' ibirindiro by' umwami Kigeli Rwabugili , aho tubimburiye ku bigwi bye mu gitero cy' imigogo , na n' ubu kikirahirwa n' amahanga , by' umwihariko abakigabweho
b' Abanyankore b' Abahinda .
Mu gitero cyiswe icy' Imigogo Rwabugili yagabye muri Nkore , cyabaye mu gihe Abanyaburayi bari batangiye gusesekara muri Afurika y' Iburasirazuba ngo bayikoronize , icyo gihe agace k' igihugu cya Uganda Nkore yabarizwagamo kari karatangiye kugendagendwamo n' Abongereza barimo kwiga inzira bazanyuramo batangira kuhakoroniza no kuhasakaza ibikorwa byabo .
Mu Rwanda ho bari bakihasunasuna byo kuhatinya kubera amateka yaho y' abayobozi n' abaturage b' indwanyi .
Impano za mbere Abongereza bahaye Abanyankore ni imbunda n' amasasu yo kwirwanaho bahashya umwanzi ubashotoye .
Zimwe mu mbunda Abanyankore bari bafite ni izo bitaga ' Makoba ' .
Izo mbunda babahaye zigera ku 300 nizo zabashutse batangira kwigerezaho ngo bagiye gutera u Rwanda rwabazengereje imyaka myinshi , dore ko hari ikindi gitero Rwabugili yari aherutse kubagabaho mu myaka ibiri yari ishize , ni ukuvuga mu wa 1892 .
Bitewe nuko ibice byo mu Burasirazuba bw' u Rwanda byari byaramaze kwigarurirwa burundu n' u Rwanda , icyari kiraje ishinga Rwabugili , ni ibihugu byo mu Burengerazuba bw' u Rwanda byari bitarigarurirwa ibindi byigaruriwe n' ababanjirije Rwabugili , byaratangiye kwigomeka .
Abanyankore bari batangiye kwiga uburyo bagaba ibitero by' ubushotoranyi ku Rwanda , bikaba n' uburyo bwo kubihimuraho kuko bari barabumvishije mu gitero cyaherukaga .
Ubushotoranyi bwakozwe na Ntare IV Rugingiza rwa Migereka umwami wa Nkore watwaraga icyo gihe , aho yambutse umupaka aza kunyaga Inyambo z' i Rwanda , agatwika ingoro ya Rwabugili yari i Rutaraka muri Nyagatare .
Icyo gihe Rwabugili yari yaragabye ibitero mu Burengerazuba bw' u Rwanda ku Ijwi ryari ryarigometse , arabimenya ko umwami wa Nkore Ntare Rugingiza rwa Migereka yamuteye akanyaga Inka ze zari Rutaraka muri Nyagatare .
Umugenga wazo Kinyamakara cya Ndezi ari na we wayoboraga ingoro ya Rwabugili yari i Rutaraka mu Ndorwa , yari mu ruzinduko , nuko banyaga inka za Rwabugili n' umwe mu baja be barimo Nyiranziza muka Mpore ya Semandira .
Umutasi wabanje gutatira Ntare yari umuhungu we Muhanika wa Ntare .
Amakuru y' icyo gitero cy' Abanyankore , Rwabugili yayabariwe n' umuhima Bukomangando wabaciye mu rihumye akabonera akito kuri ibyo bitero ko kwihakirwa kuri Rwabugili , kuko yari amuziho ubuhangange n' ubudatsindwa .
Rwabugili uburakari buramusaba yibaza uko ari bubigenze abifatira ingamba , kuko ntabwo yagombaga kugaruka igitero cyo ku Ijwi atagisoje .
Yaje gutegura igitero cyagabwe ku Banyankore muri Gashyantare umwaka wa 1894 , cyiswe " Igitero cy' Imigogo " " " " kuko cyitabiriwe n' Imitwe ibiri y' Ingabo z' Abanyankore zitwa : " " " " Ingogo n' imigogo " " " " .
Umwami Kigeli Rwabugili wari i Bunyabungo n' Ingabo ze , yabanje kohereza yo Nyamuhenda wa Kajeje , n' umutwe yari ayoboye witwaga " Ibisumizi " " " " .
Mu gushyika aho urugerero rw' Abanyankore rwari rukambitse i Kagitumba , Nyamuhenda wa Kajeje yasanze atari ukunyaga Inka gusa , ahubwo biteguye no kurwana .
Nyamuhenda n' Ibisumizi , bakabona Abanyankore barimo bohereza mu kirere ibintu biturika byaka umuriro bikabayobera kuko batari bagasobanukirwa n' imikorere y' imbunda zari zadutse vuba muri Afurika .
Bitewe nuko gusubira inyuma ku rugamba no kuruhunga bitari mu ndangagaciro z' Abanyarwanda , biyemeje kururwana , nubwo babonaga harimo udushya twinshi turimo n' imbunda zitari zimenyerewe muri aka karere .
Icyo gitero Abanyankore bagabye mu Rwanda , nicyo kiswe mu mateka y' u Rwanda na Nkore " Ehururu ya Rwanda " " " " .
Urugamba rwaremeye mu Kibande cya Ruhumba rwa Kiyojo .
Nyamuhenda n' Ibisumizi yari ayoboye , Abanyankore bahabarasira kubamara kuko bo bari bakirwanisha imiheto n' imyambi , abandi bafite imyuko iruka umuriro !
Nyamuhenda abonye ko Ingabo zigiye kumushirana , aravunura ahagarika urugamba ajya guhamagaza indi mitwe y' ingabo .
Nuko atanga ubutumwa ibukuru aho Rwabugili yari , amutangariza amacumu y' urugamba .
Rwabugili yazibiranyijwe n' uburakari butagira ingano , bitewe n' agasuzuguro kangana gutyo Abanyankore basuzuguye u Rwanda none bakaba bagiye no gutsindwa urugamba rwo kubarwanya , bitarigeze bibaho mu mateka y' abami b' u Rwanda .
Rwabugili yafashe imitwe y' Ingabo yose yari ku Ijwi n' i Bunyabungo yageraga kuri 30 , ahamagaza n' indi yari inyanyangiye ku ngerero zitandukanye hirya no hino mu gihugu yose igera kuri 50 , baravunura batera Nkore .
Bageze i Rutaraka ku ngoro ya Rwabugili , basanga harabaye amatongo , bahicara umwanya munini biga imigendekere y' urugamba bagiyemo .
Abanyankore babonye Ingabo z' uruvunganzoka z' Abanyarwanda , zitangiye kubanyanyagiramo , batangira gushya ubwoba , ariko birema agatima ku bwo kwiringira imbunda bari bafite kandi bibwiraga ko Abanyarwanda bari bataragera ku ikoranabuhanga nk' iryo .
Abanyankore batangira kurasa mu kirere no gukanga kwinshi , ariko Abanyarwanda barimo kubiga no kwitegereza ibyo barimo .
Rwabugili akitegereza iyo myuko yohereza imiriro mu kirere , niko kubaza Nyamuhenda wa Kajeje , ati " Ko ndeba bariya Banyankore bohereza imiriro mu kirere , kandi nkaba mbona igera ku butaka yazimye , babicishije iki ?
Nyamuhenda wa Kajeje , amutekerereza uburyo bagiye bakabahagarara imbere bahanganye nk' abagiye kurasana nk' uko bisanzwe mu mirwanire ya gakondo , noneho batangira kubarasa mu mutwe no mu gituza abantu batangira kwikubita hasi n' intwaro zabo , ari nako urushunzi rw' amaraso rwisuka ku butaka , bapfa umusubizo .
Mu gice gikurikira , tuzabaramburira imigendekere y' urwo rugamba rwongereye ibigwi bya Rwabugili n' igitinyiro cy' u Rwanda kirushaho kwiyongera ‚Ä¶ .
Nzaharanira kutaruta ubutumwa kuko buruta intumwa !
Isezerano rya Bamporiki nyuma yo kugirwa Minisitiri
Ku wa Mbere tariki 4 Ugushyingo 2019 nibwo Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame yashyize mu murimo mishya bamwe mu bayobozi banyuranye .
Bamporiki Edouard yagizwe Umunyamabanga wa leta muri Minisiteri y' Urubyiruko n' Umuco .
Ku wa Mbere tariki 4 Ugushyingo 2019 nibwo Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame yashyize mu murimo mishya bamwe mu bayobozi banyuranye .
Bamporiki Edouard yagizwe Umunyamabanga wa leta muri Minisiteri y' Urubyiruko n' Umuco .
Nyuma yo guhabwa uyu mwanya Bamporiki Edouard yashimiye Perezida Kagame amwizeza ko atazamutenguha ndetse azasohoza ubutumwa amutumye .
Abinyujije ku rukuta rwe rwa Twitter , Bamporiki yagize ati " Witaba kare ugatumwa kure , Watumwa n' Umukuru ugashima ushingura ugana iyo utumwe .
Ubutumwa mumpaye Nyakubahwa Mutoza w' Ikirenga Paul Kagame nzabusohoza bwemye , nzaharanira kutaruta ubutumwa kuko buruta intumwa .
Nzaba Mudahusha ku ruhembe muntumye kurasaniraho .
U Rwanda nirweme .
Ubu butumwa buri mu Kinyarwanda cyiza , bwumvikanisha uburyo uyu mugabo wari usanzwe ari umukuru w' Itorero ry' Igihugu yishimiye inshingano nshya yahawe .
Usibye kuzishimira , ikindi Bamporiki yavuzemo ni uko atazigera ashaka kuruta ubutumwa ahawe kuko buruta intumwa .
Aha akaba yumvikanishaga ko atazitwaza umwanya abonye ngo akomere kuruta inshingano ze .
Bamporiki yamenyekanye nk' umukinnyi wa filime , ikinamico akaba n' umwanditsi w' ibitabo , imivugo n' ibisigo , azwi cyane mu ikinamico urunana aho akina yitwa Tadeyo cyangwa se Kideyo , aho akina ari se wa Budensiyana na Solina , inshuti ya Bushombe na Sitefano b' i Nyarurembo .
Yavutse tariki 24 Ukuboza 1983 , i Nyamasheke mu Ntara y' Iburengerazuba , ari naho yaje kwiga amashuri abanza ndetse n' ayisumbuye , nyuma yiga amategeko mpuzamahanga muri Kaminuza yigenga ya Kigali ULK .
Yakuze akunda cyane kwandika imivugo , bituma yitabira amarushanwa atandukanye mu bigo by' amashuri .
Afite imyaka 11 gusa y' amavuko , yakoze umuvugo witwa " Iyo badatsembwa tuba dutwenga " " " " ari nawo watumye amenyekana nk' umusizi akiri umwana .
Amaze kuba umusore yagiye abona umwanya wo kuvuga imivugo mu birori bitandukanye byo ku rwego rw' igihugu , nko ku munsi mukuru w' Intwari n' indi minsi mikuru itandukanye .
Bamporiki wari usanzwe yumva ikinamico " Urunana " " " " akiri muto , akifuza kuba umwe mu bakinnyi bayo , mu 2003 yashakishije aho umushinga uyitegura ukorera , arahamenya maze agezeyo arabinginga ngo bareke ajye akinamo .
Aza kubyemererwa maze ahabwa umwanya yitwa Tadeyo .
N ' ubwo abantu bagiye bumva Tadeyo akina ari umusaza ndetse ufite abana bakuru n' abuzukuru , yari muto kuko icyo gihe yari afite imyaka 20 y' amavuko , bamwe mu bakinaga byumvikana ko ababereye umubyeyi baramurutaga .
Mu bindi bijyanye n' ubuhanzi , Bamporiki yakunze kugaragara muri filime zitandukanye ndetse ahabwa ibikombe n' ibihembo muri sinema , haba mu z' abandi yagiye akinamo ndetse no mu zo yagiye yandika akanazikinamo .
Muri z' abandi yagaragayemo harimo iyitwa ' Munyurangabo ' y ' uwitwa Isaac Chung ukomoka muri Amerika , iyitwa ' Rwanda take two ' ya Pia nawe wo muri Amerika , n' iyitwa ' Imitoma ' ya Kwezi John .
Mu mafilime yanditse ku giti cye akanakinamo harimo iyitwa ' Ukuri kuri he ' ndetse na ' Long Coat ' ( Ikote rirerire ) .
Mu 2006 yitabiriye Iserukiramuco ry' amafilime rya Cannes mu Bufaransa , mu 2010 yitabira iryabereye i Rotterdam mu Buholandi , mu 2011 yitabira iryabereye muri Turikiya ryitwa " Crimes and punishment " " " " .
Mu 2008 yabonye igihembo yakuye i New York muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , akaba yarahembewe kwandika filime nziza ( Best Script ) abikesheje filime " Long Coat " " " " , yagaragayemo abahanzi b' Abanyarwanda nka Nirere Shanel , Mani Martin n' umukinnyi Jimmy Gatete .
Mu 2011 yabonye igihembo cy' umukinnyi mwiza ( Best Actor ) mu iserukiramuco rya Heart Land .
Nyuma y' ubuhanzi mu byiciro bitandukanye , Bamporiki mu 2013 yatorewe kuba intumwa ya rubanda , aba Umudepite mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Rwanda .
Ku itariki ya 30 Kanama 2017 , Bamporiki yahawe imirimo mishya agirwa Umuyobozi w' Itorero ry' Igihugu .
Bamporiki ni umugabo wubatse , wambikanye impeta y' urudashira na Uwingabire Claudine tariki ya 18 Ukuboza 2010 .
Bamporiki yize amasomo atandukanye , arimo ajyanye na sinema yize i Burayi ahitwa Plague , aza no kwiga muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ibijyanye no kubaka amahoro no kurwanya amakimbirane .
Mu masomo asanzwe yize muri Kaminuza yigenga ya Kigali ULK aho yakuye impamyabumenyi y' icyiciro cya gatatu mu mategeko mpuzamahanga .
Ubutumwa bwa Bamporiki Edouard nyuma yo guhabwa umwanya mushya
Witaba kare ugatumwa kure , Watumwa n' Umukuru ugashima ushingura ugana iyo utumwe .
Ubutumwa mumpaye Nyakubahwa Mutoza w' Ikirenga @ PaulKagame nzabusohoza bwemye , nzaharanira kutaruta ubutumwa kuko buruta intumwa .
Nzaba Mudahusha kuruhembe muntumye kurasaniraho .
