Inkomoko gakondo y' ibicumbi by' imiryango migari y' Abanyarwanda ( Igice cya mbere )
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza ikibazo kijyanye n' ibicumbi bikuru by' imiryango bakomokamo nka gakondo y' ubutaka bwatuweho n' abakurambere mbere y' uko bororoka bagakwirakwira hirya no hino ku butaka bw' u Rwanda , ari nako babuhangaho ibihugu byaje kungwa bikabyara igihugu kimwe aricyo u Rwanda .
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza ikibazo kijyanye n' ibicumbi bikuru by' imiryango bakomokamo nka gakondo y' ubutaka bwatuweho n' abakurambere mbere y' uko bororoka bagakwirakwira hirya no hino ku butaka bw' u Rwanda , ari nako babuhangaho ibihugu byaje kungwa bikabyara igihugu kimwe aricyo u Rwanda .
Nk' uko tubikesha igitabo " Iyororoka ry' Abanyarwanda , Inkomoko y' imiryango migari " dukesha Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere mu muco , ubusizi n' amateka y' u Rwanda , tugiye kubatekerere za gakondo nkuru z' ibicumbi bikuru by' imiryango migari y' Abanyarwanda .
Abanyarwanda bibumbiye mu Bicumbi bikuru by' imiryango , imiryango migari ndetse n' inzu z' imiryango .
Ibicumbi bikuru by' imiryango , nibyo byabyaye imiryango migari , naho imiryango migari ibyara inzu z' imiryango .
Muri aya mateka tukaba tugiye kwanzikira kuri gakondo z' ibicumbi bikuru by' imiryango y' Abanyarwanda aribyo : Abasinga , Abazigaba n' Abanyiginya .
Gakondo z' igicumbi gikuru cy' imiryango y' Abasinga
Abatekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda , bagaragaza neza ko Abasinga batuye bwa mbere ku butaka bw' u Rwanda , bafite inkomoko ku Bahima babarizwa ku butaka bw' igihugu cya Uganda , aribo bakunze kwita " Abahima b' Abanyankole " " " " .
Mu iyaduka ryabo , baje bafite intego yo guhamya ubuhangange bwo gutura ku butaka bwari butwikiriwe n' amashyamba ya kimeza , babuhangaho ibihugu , bituma bakura izina ryabo mu rurimi rw' igisekuruza cyabo rw' urunyankore , bakurijeho kwitwa " Abasinga " " " " aribyo mu Kinyarwanda bisobanuye : ' ' Abatsinze " .
Mu gutura kuri ubu butaka bw' u Rwanda , Abasinga binjiriye bwa mbere mu Majyaruguru y' u Rwanda bakomereza mu Burengerazuba bagana mu Majyepfo , bakurikiranye ubutohe bw' umwegega w' Ikiyaga cya Kivu n' amashyamba y' Ibirunga n' aya kimeza nka Gishwati , Nyungwe , Mukura na Cyamudongo .
Ayo mashyamba bayahereyeho bahiga , kugeza ubwo bayatutira , bayahangaho ibihugu .
Kubera ko ntawe bacuranwaga ngo abakome imbere kuri ubu butaka , barisanzuye baratura kugeza n' ubwo basakaje ingoma zabo mu Rwanda rw' u Burengerazuba , mu Rwanda rw' Amajyepfo no mu Rwanda rwo Hagati ndetse bambuka na Nyabarongo basatira u Rwanda rw' i Burasirazuba .
Gakondo yabo ari nayo gicumbi gikuru batuyemo , kuri ubu ni mu Mirenge ya : Kigeyo , Mushonyi , Musasa , Ruhango , Gihango , Kivumu na Boneza yo mu Karere ka Rutsiro n' Umurenge wa Nyamyumba wo mu Karere ka Rubavu
Gakondo z' igicumbi gikuru cy' imiryango y' Abazigaba
Abatekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda , bagaragaza neza ko Abazigaba batuye mu ba mbere kuri ubu butaka bw' u Rwanda bakurikiye bene wabo b' Abasinga , bafite ikomoko ku Bahima babarizwa ku butaka bw' igihugu cya Uganda , aribo bakunze kwita " Abahima b' Abanyankole " " " " .
Mu iyaduka ryabo , badukiriye igice cy' i Burasirazuba bw' u Rwanda bogoze ibiyaga bigari bihabarizwa , aba ariho batema amashyamba ya Cyimeza barayakonda , barayatutira bayahangamo ibihugu bishyira kera .
Batuye ako gace babungira ubutohe gakomora ku ruzi rw' Akagera n' ibiyaga bihaboneka nka Nasho , Hago , Ihema n' ibindi .
Nuko batangira kwagura ibihugu byabo bagana mu Rwanda rwo hagati no mu Majyepfo y' Iburasirazuba .
Gakondo y' imbanza y' igicumbi gikuru cy' imiryango y' Abazigaba ni mu mirenge ya : Mwili na Murundi yo mu Karere ka Kayonza , ukongeraho Umurenge wa Rwimbogo yo muri Gatsibo .
Gakondo z' igicumbi gikuru cy' imiryango y' Abanyiginya
Abatekereze b' amateka y' Igicumbi cy' imiryango migari cy' Abanyiginya , bavuga ko cyaba gikomoka mu Majyaruguru y' Iburasirazuba bwa Afurika mu gihugu cya Ethiopia .
Inkomoko yabo ikaba ari iyo mu muryango w' Abagala bakunze kwita n' Abaromo , wari ukomeye muri icyo gihugu kandi wari nawo mugabwangoma mu myaka ya 300 nyuma ya Yezu Kirisitu .
Abanyiginya basesekaye mu Karere ka Afurika y' Iburasirazuba no mu Rwanda , ahasaga muwa 700 , ubwo bari mu iyimukayimuka nk' abandi bose ry' abatuye muri Afurika , bashaka ubwinyagamburiro bw' imiryango yabo n' amatungo yabo .
Nyuma y' igihe kitari gito , bafashe urugendo rwo mu muhora uhuza Afurika y' Amajyaruguru y' Iburasirazuba n' iy' Amajyepfo , bagaca mu bihugu bya Somaliya , Kenya na Uganda , niko gusesekara kuri ubu butaka bw' u Rwanda .
Barasukiye mu Burasirazuba bw' u Rwanda mu Murenge wa Gatsibo wo mu Karere ka Gatsibo , basanga Abazigaba barahakabye barema ingoma y' u Rweya rw' u Mubali , yari ikomatanyije Imirenge y' Akarere ka Gatsibo , n' imirenge imwe n' imwe iri mu Majyaruguru y' Akarere ka Kayonza .
Abahasesekaye muri ibyo bihe , nibo bavuyemo Abasekuruza b' Imbanza ba Kazi wabyaye Gihanga cyahanze ingoma y' u Rwanda .
Mu gusesekara mu Rweya rw' Abazigaba , bahaserukanye , ibigwi n' imihigo y' ibyo bazanye muri aka karere , nk' uko babivuze mu izina ryabo ubwo Abazigaba babazaga izina ryabo .
Nk' aho bakavuze iry' igisekuruza cyabo cy' Abagala cyangwa se Abaromo , badukana izina rishya ryibigwi n' ibirindiro by' ahazaza habo , ry' Abanyiginya rishatse kuvuga " Abantu barambye ku butunzi n' ubupfura " " " " .
Nyuma y' imyaka isaga 300 , Abanyiginya bamaze mu busembere bacumbikiwe n' Abazigaba , nibwo umucyo w' ubuhangange wabamurikiye bahanga igihugu cyabo kitwaga Gasabo , cyinjira mu ruhando rw' ibindi bihugu bigera kuri 24 byari bisanganyije ubu butaka bw' u Rwanda , baba babaye igihugu cya 25 , gihangwa na Gihanga Ngomijana , umukurambere w' Abangiyinya bahanze ingoma y' u Rwanda .
I Gasabo niho Abanyiginya n' imiryango ibakomokaho baguriye ubutaka bwabo bahanga ibindi bihugu ku bisigara by' ubutaka Abasinga n' Abazigaba bari baranennye .
Ibihugu byahanzwe na bene Gihanga , muri byo dusangamo Ndorwa y' Abashambo , Kibali y' Abega , u Bugara bw' Abacyaba n' u Bugesera bw' Abahondogo .
Amateka y' impitabie ku gihugu cy' u Rwanda , adutekerereza ko gakondo nkuru y' igicumbi gikuru cy' Abanyiginya n' imiryango migari ibakomokaho , ari mu Mirenge ya Nduba , Bumbogo , Rutunga , Gikomero , Ndera na Rusororo yo mu Karere ka Gasabo , ukongeraho n' Umurenge wa Fumbwe wo mu Karere ka Rwamagana .
Nyuma yo kubagezaho Gakondo nkuru z' ibicumbi by' imiryango y' Abanyarwanda , mu bice bikurikiraho , tuzabagezaho za Gakondo nkuru z' imiryango migari y' Abanyarwanda , uko ari 24 .

Iki gitabo yacyise ' 100 mistakes i don' t regret ' cyangwa se mu rurimi rw' Ikinyarwanda ' Amakosa 100 nticuza ' .
Rubaduka Frank yanditse igitabo kigaragaza amakosa yakoze mu buzima ariko aticuza .
Iki gitabo yacyise ' 100 mistakes i don' t regret ' cyangwa se mu rurimi rw' Ikinyarwanda ' Amakosa 100 nticuza ' .
Uyu musore watangije irushanwa rya Miss Career Africa agiye gushyira hanze iki gitabo yageneye urubyiruko n' undi wese ushaka gutsinda ubwoba agakurikira amahitamo y' umutima we .
Iki gitabo yacyanditse mu gihe cy' imyaka ibiri .
Kizacururizwa ku rubuga rwa Amazon .
Uyu musore yahisemo gukurikira ibyo akunda nyuma y' uko atanze igitabo gisoza kaminuza kikangwa bitewe n' uko yari yatinze , kuko hari hashize icyumweru abandi batanze ibyabo .
Gutinda gutanga igitabo gisoza kaminuza yabitewe n' uko yari yahugiye ku bikorwa bya sosiyete ye .
Yahisemo guhagarika amasomo , ahubwo yita ku bikorwa bya sosiyete ye kuko ariho yari yerekeje umutima .
Umuryango we ntiwishimye iyo nzira kuko washakaga ko yiga akaminuza akajya gusaba akazi ahandi ku buryo wazajya umubona mu biro ari umuntu ukomeye .
Hashize igihe gito ahagaritse kwiga , yatsindiye inkunga y' amadorali ibihumbi 150 yahawe n' Abanya - Australia .
Rubaduka witegura kwizihiza isabukuru y' imyaka 27 y' amavuko , yahise ashinga sosiyete eshanu mu bihe bitandukanye buri imwe ishamikiye ku yindi .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko yahisemo gutanga ubutumwa muri iki gitabo kubera ko abenshi bakunze guhisha inzira banyuzemo kandi zabera urugero rwiza benshi .
Ati " Abantu benshi iyo batangiye gutera imbere hari ukuntu bahisha amakosa n' ibindi bintu bagiye bahura nabyo .
Ariko kuko njye nagiranye igihango n' Imana ko ningira aho ngera nta mpamyabumenyi mfite nzabwira urubyiruko rugenzi rwanjye ko umuntu adakeneye impamyabumenyi n' ibitangaza kugira ngo abe igitangaza mu Isi .
Yavuze ko byarangiye uwari umuterankunga we muri Kaminuza anyuzwe n' intego ye amutera inkunga y' umushinga wa mbere yakoze hashize umwaka umwe abona undi muterankunga .
Iki gitabo acyitezeho guhindura imyumvire y' abandi n' iy' ababyeyi babuza abana babo gukurikira amahitamo yabo .
Aniteze ko umuntu wakuriye mu buzima bubi uzasoma iki gitabo azahita ahagarika kumva ko akeneye umuntu uvuga rikijyana kugira ngo agera ku cyo yiyemeje .

Village Urugwiro , inyubako y' amateka akomeye mu Rwanda
Village Urugwiro , ni inyubako yubashywe kuva icyubakwa kugeza n' ubu .
Benshi tuyirebera kure kubera icyubahiro tuyigomba nk' ibiro bicurirwamo icyerecyezo gitumye u Rwanda ruba ubukombe , ikaba isoko y' amahoro aduhesha ibikombe mu mahanga .
Village Urugwiro , ni inyubako yubashywe kuva icyubakwa kugeza n' ubu .
Benshi tuyirebera kure kubera icyubahiro tuyigomba nk' ibiro bicurirwamo icyerecyezo gitumye u Rwanda ruba ubukombe , ikaba isoko y' amahoro aduhesha ibikombe mu mahanga .
Ni inyubako y' amateka kuko abagera kuri 50 % by' Abanyarwanda bariho bavutse iriho , iganje ku Kacyiru , mu Karere ka Gasabo mu Mujyi wa Kigali aho imaze imyaka 44 .
Yubatswe mu 1975 n' Umuryango wahuzaga Ibihugu bya Afurika cyane cyane ibyakolonijwe n' u Bufaransa n' ibikoresha Igifaransa , Organization Commune Africaine et Malgache ( OCAM ) .
Uwo muryango kuri ubu wazimye , u Rwanda rwawinjiyemo mu 1965 .
Mu 1975 , nibwo rwari kwakira inama yawo yagombaga kwitabirwa n' abakuru b' ibihugu bagera kuri 15 .
Byari ihurizo rikomeye ku gihugu nk' u Rwanda cyari gifite hoteli nke zitwa ko zikomeye nka Mille Collines na Diplomate zari zigezweho icyo gihe ariko zifite ubushobozi bwo kwakira abashyitsi baringaniye .
Muri icyo gihe u Rwanda rwiteguraga kwakira inama , inyubako za mbere za Village Urugwiro zubatswe ku mafaranga ya OCAM nkuko Rucagu Boniface , umwe mu bagize Urwego Ngishwanama rw' Inararibonye yabibwiye IGIHE .
Inama ya OCAM irangiye , inyubako za Village Urugwiro zeguriwe Leta y' u Rwanda nayo izihinduramo hoteli yakiraga abifite muri ibyo bihe .
Nubwo Village Urugwiro yabaye hoteli , mu gihe u Rwanda rwabaga rwakiriye inama zikomeye yakomezaga kwifashishwa mu kwakira abashyitsi ba Leta .
Urugero ni tariki 21 na 22 Gicurasi 1979 ubwo u Rwanda rwakiraga inama ya Gatandatu ihuza u Bufaransa na Afurika yanitabiriwe na Perezida wari uyoboye u Bufaransa icyo gihe , Val√©ry Marie Ren√© Georges Giscard d' Estaing .
Mbere y' uko iyo nama iba , u Bufaransa bwari bwatanze amafaranga yo kwagura Village Urugwiro no kuyivugurura kugira ngo ijye ku rwego rwo kwakira inama ikomeye nk' iyo , nkuko biri mu nyandiko z' ibanga za Ambasade ya Amerika mu Rwanda muri icyo gihe , zashyizwe hanze na WikiLeaks .
Uwo mwaka ni nabwo hubatswe hoteli Novotel Umubano ( Marasa Umubano Hotel kuri ubu ) nabwo ku mafaranga yatanzwe n' u Bufaransa .
Rucagu avuga ko nyuma yo kwagura Village Urugwiro , yasigaye igizwe n' inyubako ( appartments ) zisaga 20 zirimo amacumbi agezweho , ibyumba by' inama n' ibindi .
Amacumbi y' abadepite , ibiro bidahoraho bya Perezida
Juv√©nal Habyarimana amaze gufata ubutegetsi mu 1973 , yahise asesa Inteko Ishinga Amategeko .
Yongeye kuyisubizaho mu 1981 , abadepite ba mbere 70 b' inzibacyuho batangira imirimo mu 1982 .
Kubera ubuke bw' amacumbi muri Kigali , Leta yemereye buri mudepite icumbi muri Village Urugwiro dore ko abenshi babaga baturuka mu bice bya kure badashobora gukora bataha iwabo .
Mu 1983 habaye amatora y' abadepite , Rucagu Boniface aba umwe muri bo ubwo yatangiraga imirimo mu 1984 na we ahabwa icumbi muri Village Urugwiro .
Umudepite yahabwaga icumbi gusa , ibyo kurya akimenya .
Rucagu avuga ko mu badepite 70 , abasaga 40 babaga muri Village Urugwiro kuko babaga baturuka mu bice bya kure .
Uwabaga yifitiye inzu i Kigali , yayibagamo Leta ikamugenera amafaranga y' icumbi .
Rucagu ati " Uwabaga yifitiye inzu ye bamuhaga amafaranga ariko babanje kubyanga bavuga bati kuki mushaka kurara mu nzu zanyu kandi twarabageneye iza Leta , baraburana ariko byaje gukemuka nyuma .
Icyo gihe abadepite babamo , inzu zasagukaga zakomezaga kuba ibyumba bya hoteli bisanzwe , abashaka kubiraramo bakaza kwishyura .
Nubwo hari hoteli n' amacumbi y' abadepite , Perezida Habyarimana na we yahashyize ibiro ariko akajya abizamo rimwe na rimwe kuko ibiro nyamukuru byari mu mujyi rwagati , ahubatse Ibiro by' Umujyi wa Kigali ubu .
Rucagu ati " Iruhande rw' izo nzu haruguru y' ahahoze reception niho hari Ibiro by' Umukuru w' Igihugu .
Muri izo nzu zose ahagana ku rwinjiriro yari yarafashemo inzu y' ibiro bye , izindi zose zikomeza kuba hoteli .
Yari ibiro bya kabiri yazagamo nka rimwe cyangwa kabiri mu kwezi .
Buri nyubako ( apartment ) muri izo zari zigize Hotel Village Urugwiro yabaga ifite icyiciro runaka ibarizwamo .
Rucagu wahabaye mu gihe cy' imyaka 10 ari umudepite , avuga ko buri nyubako yabaga ifite ibyumba bitatu , ni ukuvuga A , B na C .
Icyumba A , cyabaga gifite ibyangombwa nkenerwa byose birimo uruganiriro , uburiri , ubwiherero , igikoni , harimo frigo n' ibindi , kikaba kigenewe Umukuru w' Igihugu mu gihe habaye inama cyangwa undi muntu wo ku rwego rwo hejuru wakirayemo .
Hafi y' icyo cyumba nyamukuru , habaga ikindi bise B , kikararamo umuganga w' umuntu mukuru waraye muri A .
Ni ukuvuga ko niba haraye Perezida , muri B hararaga umuganga we naho muri C hakarara abarinzi be .
Mu gihe habaga habaye inama zikomeye , abadepite bari barahawe amacumbi muri Village Urugwiro basabwaga kuvamo bakazagaruka inama yarangiye .
Rucagu ati " Batumenyeshaga mbere y' ukwezi , tukavamo bakahakoropa , bakahasukura bakavanamo umwanda wose , tukazagaruka baragiye .
Ubwo mu mirimo y' Inteko twariyeranjaga .
Village Urugwiro yakomeje kuba hoteli kugeza mu 1994 muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Jenoside imaze guhagarikwa , muri Nyakanga uwo mwaka Leta y' Ubumwe imaze kurahira Village Urugwiro aho kuba ibiro bidahoraho by' Umukuru w' Igihugu , yahindutse Ibiro byuzuye by' iminsi yose by' Umukuru w' Igihugu kugeza ubu .

Abakobwa bifuza guhatanira ikamba rya Miss Rwanda 2020 batangiye kwiyandikisha binyuze ku rubuga rw' irushanwa , mu mabwiriza basabwe kuba bujuje harimo impinduka kuko Ikinyarwanda cyashyizwe mu ndimi zemerewe gukoreshwa .

Ikinyarwanda ni cyo cy' ingenzi , izindi ndimi zizakoreshwa ku mahitamo y' uhatana .
Prince Kid yavuze ko mu gutanga amanota hazitabwa cyane kubyo umukobwa avuga , ubwiza ndetse n' umuco .
Ubusanzwe umukobwa yasabwaga kuba azi Ikinyarwanda n' urundi rurimi rumwe rw' amahanga , uburyo abahatana bitwaraga mu ndimi z' amahanga byatumye benshi bibaza impamvu abategura Miss Rwanda bazibandaho nyamara hashobora gukoreshwa ururimi kavukire , aha bagaraazaga ko icyingenzi ari ikiri mu muntu atari ururimi akivugamo .

Inkomoko y' amazina y' uduce tumwe two muri Kigali nka Nyarugenge , Kacyiru n' utundi
Ikigo cy' Ingoro z' Igihugu z' Umurage w' u Rwanda ( INMR ) cyatangaje ko amwe mu mazina yahawe uduce tumwe na tumwe two muri Kigali akoreshwa kugeza ubu , yagiye atangwa hashingiwe ku ihangwa ry' igihugu , ibikorwa by' iyubaka gihugu ( Ubuhinzi , ubworozi , intambara ) , ibikorwa byahabereye bigasiga umugani .
Ikigo cy' Ingoro z' Igihugu z' Umurage w' u Rwanda ( INMR ) cyatangaje ko amwe mu mazina yahawe uduce tumwe na tumwe two muri Kigali akoreshwa kugeza ubu , yagiye atangwa hashingiwe ku ihangwa ry' igihugu , ibikorwa by' iyubaka gihugu ( Ubuhinzi , ubworozi , intambara ) , ibikorwa byahabereye bigasiga umugani .
Icyo kigo kivuga ko hari amazina yatanzwe hagendewe ku bwoko bw' igiti biri cyangwa byiganje ahantu runaka .
Izina " " " " Nyarugenge " " " " rituruka ku giti cyitwa Imigenge ( Acacia hochii ) .
Ariryo ubu ryitwa Akarere ka Nyarugenge .
Abahanga mu mateka bavuga ko hari ahandi nka ' Kimironko ' hiswe hatyo hagendewe ku ishyamba ry' ibiti byitwa ' Imironko ' ryatewe na Cyilima Rujugira , kugira ngo ajye aritemamo ibiti byo kuramvura imiheto yo guhangana n' amahanga adakunda u Rwanda .
Kimihurura habaga ibyatsi bivura byitwa ' imihurura ' n ' ahandi .
Ikigo cy' Ingoro z' Igihugu z' Umurage w' u Rwanda ( INMR ) kivuga ko hari amazina yaturutse ku bantu bakomeye babaga ahantu runaka .
Nka " Kacyiru " " " " bivugwa ko ryatanzwe hagendewe ku mugabo witwaga Cyiru ; wari umutware na " Rwabutabura " " " " ryatanzwe riturutse ku witwaga Rwabutabura wari utuye ahitwa iryo zina muri iki gihe , ubu ni mu Karere ka Nyarugenge .
Umushakashatsi ku muco n' amateka Nsanzabera Jean De Dieu avuga ko ' Kacyiru ( agasozi k' icyiru ) ' byitiriwe agasozi katangiweho ' Ibyiru ' byinshi , bikomotse ku manza zacirwaga Abanyabwanacyambwe banze kuyoboka ingoma ya Mukobanya , nyuma yo kuhigarurira ahasaga mu wa 1378 ubwo yicaga Nkuba ya Nyabakonjo umwami w' u Bwanacyambwe .
' Gacuriro ' hiswe hatyo kubera uruganda rucura amacumu yo kwagura u Rwanda rwubatswe na Kigeli Mukobanya .
Andi mazina yatanzwe afatiwe ku bikorwa byo kubaka u Rwanda nk' ubworozi bw' inka .
" Kicukiro " " " " risobanuye umusozi amacukiro ( ibirundo by' amase y' inka ) .
Mu bihe byo hambere , Kicukiro izwi nka kamwe mu turere tw' umujyi wa Kigali kororerwagaho inka nyinshi .
Niho hari hubatse ibiraro by' inka za Kigeli Mukobanya n' umuhungu we Mibambwe Sekarongoro Mutabazi .
Hari ahazwi nka ' Kabusunzu ' hiswe hatyo kubera umupfumu w' umuhanga wari waraturutse i Karagwe witwa ' Gasunzu ' nyuma aho atuye bahita ' Kagasunzu ' nyuma umunyamakuru wo kuri Radiyo Rwanda yagiye gutara amakuru avugira kuri Radiyo ko ari ' Kabusunzu ' rihama rityo .
Hazwi nk' i Nyamirambo hiswe hatyo biturutse ku mirambo myinshi yahabonetse ubwo abanyoro bateraga u Rwanda .
Amateka nk' ayo aboneka mu nzu ndangamateka yitiriwe Richard Kandt ( Kandt House Museum ) .
Mu busanzwe hari ahandi mu Rwanda hagiye hitwa amazina hagendewe ku bikorwa bitandukanye byagiye bihabera .
Hari nko ku Kivumu cya Mpushi , ahacirwaga abarwaye ibinyoro , ku cya Semakamba habereye urubanza rwa Semakamba n' Umwami Kigeli Rwabugiri n' ahandi .
Kigali yagizwe umurwa mukuru w' u Rwanda bwa mbere ku bwa Kigeli Mukobanya ahasaga 1378 .
Umurwa mukuru w' Umwami wari mu Mudugudu wa Vugavuge mu Kagali ka Gasabo mu Murenge wa Rutunga h' ubu .
Kurasaga , imyotso , kurumika , kugombora : Uburyo gakondo bwamamaye mu kuvura indwara z' amayobera
Kurumika no kurasaga , imyotso no kugombora , ni imigenzo nyarwanda yakorwaga mu buvuzi gakondo no kurinda ibyago Abanyarwanda , bityo uwabikoraga akaba afite imyerere y' uko iyo bikozwe byanze bikunze birinda kandi bikanavura .
Kurumika no kurasaga , imyotso no kugombora , ni imigenzo nyarwanda yakorwaga mu buvuzi gakondo no kurinda ibyago Abanyarwanda , bityo uwabikoraga akaba afite imyerere y' uko iyo bikozwe byanze bikunze birinda kandi bikanavura .
Gusa kuri ubu Abanyarwanda benshi ntibabyemera , ndetse bavuga ko ari imihango ya gipagani , n' ubwo hari abaganga bemeza ko iyo migenzo yabaga ari ingirakamaro .
Nk' uko tubikesha igitabo " Umuco mu Buvanganzo " cyanditswe n' Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , Inzobere ku muco , amateka n' ubuvanganzo nyarwanda , tugiye kubataturira imwe mu mihango n' imigenzo yakorwaga mu kuvura no kurinda indwara mu muco w' Abanyarwanda .
Kurasaga ( Guca indasago , gukeba gahoro gahoro ku mubiri ) umuntu byaterwaga n' uko bashaka nko kumushyiramo imiti yo kumuvura ikintu arwaye , cyangwa kumutsirika bavuga ngo batazamuroga , bakarasaga rero bagashyiramo iyo miti .
Hari n' aho bikengeraga ko umwana wavutse azahura n' akaga , nako bakagatsirika bakoresheje kumuca indasago , ukazasanga koko bibaye impamo , ibyago baketse , akabicika .
Hari kandi n' indasago bacaga ku mugore ugiye gushaka cyangwa umugabo , bagashyiramo imiti ituma bahamya umubano uzira kidobya .
Niyo mpamvu uzasanga abantu bakuru benshi bafite indasago ku mubiri , ku gikanu , mu gatuza , ku bibero ku gahanga , mu biganza n' ahandi .
Umumaro w' indasago ahanini , wari uwo gutsirika ushyiramo umuti aho barasaze , bakungikanya n' imitongero runaka yo kuvura , imitongero igakurwa n' indi maze umuntu akaba mutaraga .
Kurumika ho bacaga indasago nko mu gikanu cyangwa mu mugongo , bagashyiraho ikintu bita ingunga .
Ingunga kari agacuma bakebye katagira ijosi .
Kurumika babikoraga bashaka gusohora amaraso mabi ari mu mubiri .
Hari nk' ubwo imitsi yipfundikaga ikabuza umuntu kuba yagenda , ugasanga aho yipfunditse habaye nk' umukara , uwo byabayeho agakunda kugira ibinya bimufata bya hato na hato .
Barasagaga ya maraso agasohoka , nyuma bagasigamo imiti yo kugira ngo homoke hasubirane , ariko na none igakiza ubwo burwayi ntibuzagaruke .
Hari n' aho barumikaga bakoresheje ihembe rikiyomeka ku mubiri rikajya rikurura amaraso , ryamara kuzura bakarikuraho bakayamena bakongera bagasubizaho .
Kurasaga no kurumika , bifite itandukaniro benshi badakunze kumenya .
Kurasaga byakorerwaga ku ruhu inyuma , basharuragaho gato , hakava amaraso makeya .
Naho kurumika , byakorwaga binjiye mu mubiri imbere ku buryo bashyikira umutsi ujyana amaraso mu mubiri , akaba ariwo bakomeretsa amaraso bashaka kumena akava .
Ubuvuzi gakondo bwo kotsa ( imyotso ) amateka atugaragariza ko bwaba bukomoka mu Gisaka , aho bwadutse ku ngoma y' umwami waho Kimenyi II Shumbusho , watway I Gisaka ahasaga mu wa 1312 .
Muri icyo kibariro , mu Gisaka hadutse indwara y' amaso yafataga abana bakiri bato bakundaga kuvukana bitewe n' uburwayi bwafataga Ababyeyi batwite , urukingo rukaba gufata abo bana bakabotsa ku gahanga no mu misaya , bagahita bakira .
Noneho biba nk' umugenzo wo muri ako gace , abantu babona ari byiza , uvutse wese kabone n' ubwo yaba atarwaye amaso bakamwotsa .
Gushyira imyotso ku gahanga no mu misaya , nibwo buvuzi gakondo bw' Abanyarwanda bifashishaga bavura icyorezo cy' uburwayi bw' amaso , haba ku bana no ku bantu bakuru
Uwo mugenzo wo guca imyotso ku bana b' Abanyagisaka , wageze aho uba ikirango mwihariko wabo , uhinduka umugenzo wo guca imanzi z' ubwiza ku mwana uwo ariwe wese uvukiye mu Gisaka , ku buryo byabaye n' ikimenyetso cyakoreshwaga mu ntambara y' I Gisaka n' u Rwanda kugira ngo Abanyagisaka babashe gutandukanya abaturage babo n' Abanyarwanda .
Ubuvuzi gakondo bw' Abanyarwanda bugombora uwakomwe ( uwarumwe ) n' inzoka , akabasha kuyirokoka , ni bumwe mu buvuzi gakondo bumaze igihe kirekire mu Rwanda , kuko bwahanganywe n' u Rwanda rukiri amashyamba y' inzitane adapfa kwisukirwa .
Kugombora , hakoreshwaga uburyo bwo gushyira umuti witwa : ' ' Umukubayoka " ahakomwe ( aharumwe ) n' inzoka , cyangwa se bagashyira ifu y' inzoka y' inkazi babaga baraseye ( nk' impiri , uruziramire n' izindi ) mu gikomere cy' aharumwe n' inzoka .
Kugombora byaherekezwaga n' imitongero ivugwa muri ubu buryo :
Ndakugombora impiri , ndakugombora idubi , Ndakugombora insana n' inkomyi , Habyimbirwa imbwa , habyimbirwa impyisi , Ubwo bugomboro nabugomboje Ruganzu , Bwagomboye Rwabugili na Rudahigwa .
Ndakugombora byunga na barihuta , N ' inyenzi na buhoma !
Murahura , ntikurya !
urajye kuvoma , Ntikurya !
urajya ku ryama ! ntikurya !
Murahura , ikaraba , ikarabirana , ikabura ubwenge , Ikabura ubwinyo , ikaba imbwa biseseme !
Ubuvuzi gakondo bw' Abanyarwanda bushingiye ku kurumika , kotsa , guca indasago no kugombora , bwari bwuje igenantekerezo zisobetse rwose , ku buryo ritabashaga kugerurwa n' abahisi .
Ku buryo na n' ubu hari aho bugikoreshwa mu kuvura indwara zimwe na zimwe .
1884 - 1885 : Uko byagenze ubwo Afurika yagabanwaga bugati n' Abanyaburayi
Nyuma y' imyaka 300 yo gusahura Afurika abaturage bayo bajyanwa ku ngufu mu mirimo y' agahato n' ubucakara muri Amerika , mu 1884 Abanyaburayi bahinduye umuvuno noneho bajya umugambi wo kugira Afurika iyabo .
Nyuma y' imyaka 300 yo gusahura Afurika abaturage bayo bajyanwa ku ngufu mu mirimo y' agahato n' ubucakara muri Amerika , mu 1884 Abanyaburayi bahinduye umuvuno noneho bajya umugambi wo kugira Afurika iyabo .
Ni umushinga wakoranywe ubugome nk' uwa mbere kuko ubuzima bw' umunyafurika icyo gihe ntacyo bwari buvuze , icyari kibaraje ishinga ni ugukungahaza ibihugu byabo basahura mutungo kamere wa Afurika .
Mu 1884 Abanyaburayi birengagije miliyoni z' abanyafurika bapfiriye mu buretwa no mu nzira bajyanywe mu bucakara muri Amerika , bongera kureba ibiri mu nyungu zabo ku Mugabane wari usanzwe uri ukwawo .
Ku gicamunsi cyo kuwa Gatandatu tariki 15 Ugushyingo 1884 , i Berlin mu ngoro y' ubwami bw' u Budage izwi nka Wilhelmstrasse hateraniye inama mpuzamahanga .
Iyo nama yari yatumijwe n' uwari Chancelier w' u Budage , Otto von Bismarck .
Intego nyamukuru y' iyi nama yigaragazaga ucyinjira mu cyumba kuko hari hamanitse ikarita y' Afurika ifite uburebure bwa metero eshanu igaragaza ibiyaga by' uwo mugabane , imigezi , imisozi , amazina make y' ahantu hamwe na hamwe n' utudomo tw' umweru hamwe na hamwe h' ingenzi .
Imbere y' ameza y' uruziga hari hicaye abayobozi b' ibihugu 13 by' i Burayi .
Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika nazo zari zatumiwe ariko zanga kwitabira kuko nta nyungu nyinshi zabonaga muri Afurika .
Iyo nama yamaze amezi atatu kuko yarangiye tariki 26 Gashyantare 1885 , ibihugu byose bimaze kwemeranya uko bizigabanya Afurika , by' umwihariko ibyifataga nk' ibikomeye birimo u Budage , u Bufaransa , u Bwongereza , u Buholandi , u Bubiligi , Portugal na Espagne .
Mu kugabana bari bafite amakaramu y' ibiti , buri umwe aca imiringo aho ashaka gufata , bakabanza kubiganiraho , babyemeza ubwo bagakomereza ku wundi .
Iyo nama yamaze iminsi 104 uvanyemo akaruhuko gato bafashe ngo bajye kwizihiza iminsi mikuru ya Noheli n' Ubunani .
Nyuma y' inama , ibihugu byose bya Afurika uvanyemo Liberia na Ethiopia y' ubu , byaragabanywe kandi birakolonizwa .
Nubwo ibyagabanwaga ari ubukungu bwa Afurika , nta munyafurika wigeze atumirwa muri iyo nama cyangwa ngo hagire ubahagararira .
N ' umuyobozi wa Zanzibar washatse kwitumira ngo ayijyemo yakumiriwe kure n' Abongereza .
Inzobere mu mateka ya Afurika , Umunyanijeriya Prof Olyaemi Akinwumi yavuze ko kugabanya Afurika byakozwe hatitawe ku mateka cyangwa imibereho y' abatuye uwo mugabane ari nazo ngorane igihura nazo .
Ati " Benshi muri Afurika twemera ko inkomoko y' amakimbirane akigaragara kuri uyu mugabane , yatangiriye mu nama y' i Berlin .
Akinwumi avuga ko nk' ubwoko bwabaga bubumbiye hamwe , bwajyaga kwisanga bwashyizwe mu bihugu bitandukanye , ibihugu bimwe bikagabanyirizwa ubuso n' ibindi .
Mu mabwiriza ibihugu byaganiye i Berlin byahawe , harimo ko niba igihugu cyageze ku butaka runaka bwa Afurika , buzitwa ubwacyo ari uko kibimenyesheje bigenzi byacyo i Burayi kandi kuri ubwo butaka hakoherezwayo ingabo nke .
Intego yo kujya muri Afurika kwari ukuhazana ibyo bise ' iterambere ' , kuhasakaza ubukirisitu no guteza imbere ubucuruzi ' bwabo ' .
Kugira ngo igihugu cyemererwe ko ubutaka cyafashe ari ubwacyo , cyagombaga gisinyana n' abategetsi gakondo baho inyandiko yemera ko bemeye abakoloni ariko bakazahabwa uburinzi n' icyo gihugu cyabakolonije .
Ibyo ntibyari bigoye dore ko abategetsi benshi muri Afurika batari bazi kwandika cyangwa gusoma .
Mu gihe cyo kugabana Afurika , uduce duke tw' uwo mugabane nitwo twari twaragezwemo n' Abanyaburayi .
Abenshi bari baragiye bakambika ku nkengero z' uwo mugabane ku bice bikora ku nyanja .
Mu 1900 nibwo batangiye kwinjira imbere muri Afurika bashakisha ibyo kwifashisha mu nganda zabo nk' amabuye y' agaciro , Caoutchouc yakoreshwaga mu nganda zikora ibinyabiziga mu Burayi n' ibindi .
U Bubiligi nibwo bwabyungukiyemo cyane kuko umwami Leopold II yahawe ububasha bwo kugenzura ubutaka bwa Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , gusa ategekwa kuhubaka ku buryo haba ahantu h' ubucuruzi hagati y' Abanyaburayi bose muri Afurika , mbese buri gihugu cy' i Burayi gishaka kuhisanzura kikabikora .
Mu bindi yasabwe ni ugukwirakwiza ubukiristu mu bice byose bigize Congo .
Nubwo Leopold II yari yemeye ko Congo izabyazwa umusaruro n' abanyaburayi bose , siko byagenze kuko amasezerano yo gucukura no gutwara umutungo kamere wa Congo amenshi yasinyishwaga sosiyete zo mu Bubiligi .
Mu 1908 byaje kumenyekana ko ku mabwiriza ya Leopold II , abaturage ba Congo bategekwaga kujya gushaka ingano runaka ya Caoutchouc bashyira abatware b' Ababiligi , batabikora bagacibwa amaboko cyangwa ibirenge .
Leopold II yaje kwamburwa Congo iherezwa Guverinoma y' u Bubiligi .
Kuva mu 1885 kugeza mu 1908 , miliyoni z' abanye - Congo zari zimaze gupfa zishwe , ziciwe amaboko , zikubiswe kubera " " " " ibikorwa by' agakiza " " " " L√©opold II yari yavuze ko abazaniye , nyamara byahe byokajya .
Kugeza mu 1914 , nibura 90 % by' ibihugu bya Afurika byari mu maboko y' ibihugu birindwi by' i Burayi .
Afurika yasanze guhindura imipaka byateza ibindi bibazo bidashira
Imipaka yashyizweho n' abakoloni niyo ikigenderwaho n' uyu munsi .
Mu mabwiriza ibihugu byari byahawe , ni uko abaturage bakolonijwe n' igihugu runaka , babaga batemerewe guhahirana n' abo badahuje igihugu kibakolonije .
Akinwumi avuga ko kubera ko abenshi mu bagiye bacibwaho imipaka babaga ari abaturage bo mu bwoko bumwe , kubategeka kudahahirana kuko baciriweho imipaka byateje amakimbirane akigaragara n' ubu .
Ati " Iriya nama yangije byinshi cyane muri Afurika .
Hari ibihugu bikigerwaho n' ingaruka zayo uyu munsi .
Mu myaka ya 1960 , abayobozi b' ibihugu bya Afurika byari bikibona ubwigenge bashatse guhindura imipaka yashyiriweho mu nama y' i Berlin ariko basanga byateza ibibazo byinshi kurusha ibyo byakemura .
Umushakashatsi ku mateka y' ubukoloni muri Afurika , akaba n' umwarimu muri Kaminuza ya Erfurt , Michael Pesek , yagize ati " Abayobozi benshi ahagana mu 1960 , bavugaga ko baramutse bayihinduye byaba ari ukwiteza ibibazo byinshi .
Inzobere zivuga ko icyo gihe nibura amakimbirane yari ashingiye hagati mu baturage atari hagati y' ibihugu .
Guhindura imipaka byari kwiyongeraho andi makimbirane hagati y' ibihugu , ibintu bikazamba kurushaho .
Mu mwaka wa 2010 ubwo hizihizwaga imyaka 125 ishize inama y' i Berlin irangiye , abari bahagarariye ibihugu bya Afurika muri uwo munsi wizihirijwe Berlin bavuze ko Afurika ikeneye impozamarira y' ibyangijwe n' ubukoloni ndetse bavuga ko ibyakozwe ari ibyaha byibasiye inyokomuntu .
Nubwo basabye impozamarira , nta na kimwe cyakozwe .
Pesek yemeza ko bidatunguranye kuba ntacyo Afurika yahawe .
Ati " Hari ibindi byagiye bivugwa byo guha impozamarira Afurika kubw ' ubucakara ndetse n' impozamarira kubwa Jenoside yakorewe Abayahudi .
Nyamara ntawe ujya ukomoza ku myaka isaga ijana abanyaburayi bamaze muri Afurika bayikoloniza .
Ghana nicyo gihugu cya Afurika cyabashije kwigobotora bwa mbere ingoyi cyashyizweho n' inama y' i Berlin , kibona ubwigenge .
Mu 2000 hafi ibihugu byose byahoze bikolonijwe muri Afurika byari bimaze kubona ubwigenge .
Ikibazo nuko byinshi mu bihugu byakolonije Afurika , na nyuma y' ubwigenge byakomeje kugira akaboko mu miyoborere ya Afurika ndetse rimwe na rimwe ushaka kubibangamira akigizwayo .
Mu kwezi gsuhize inama y' abaminisitiri mu Bufaransa , yemeje umushinga w' itegeko rihindura amasezerano bwagiranye n' ibihugu umunani byo mu burengerazuba bwa Afurika ku ikoreshwa rya CFA .
Igihugu gikoresha iryo faranga cyasabwagwa kubika kimwe cya kabiri cy' amafaranga n' amadevize yacyo muri Banki Nkuru y' u Bufaransa .
Mutaganzwa agiye gusohora igitabo kivuga ku mpanuro z' ingenzi Perezida Kagame yagiye atanga
" Tujye twirinda kumera nk' isenene aho uwazifashe yazishyize kandi mu kanya zitegereje gukarangirwa hamwe " " " " ni impanuro Perezida Kagame yatanze tariki 5 Ugushyingo 2016 ubwo hizihizwaga imyaka 20 yari ishize umuryango Unity Club ushinzwe .
" Tujye twirinda kumera nk' isenene aho uwazifashe yazishyize kandi mu kanya zitegereje gukarangirwa hamwe " " " " ni impanuro Perezida Kagame yatanze tariki 5 Ugushyingo 2016 ubwo hizihizwaga imyaka 20 yari ishize umuryango Unity Club ushinzwe .
Izo mpanuro ni zimwe mu zikubiye mu gitabo gishya " Isoko tuvomaho Impanuro " Mutaganzwa Charles agiye gusohora , kigaruka mu buryo buvunaguye ku mbwiraruhame za Perezida Kagame , zagize uruhare mu kubaka igihugu nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi muri Mata 1994 .
Ni igitabo gikubiyemo uduce tw' impanuro Perezida Kagame yagiye atanga mu bihe bitandukanye .
Ni igitabo kirimo izo mpanuro gusa , nta bindi bitekerezo by' umwanditsi byiyongeraho .
Mutaganzwa avuga ko impanuro za Perezida Kagame zagize uruhare rukomeye mu kongera kubaka igihugu haba mu bumwe n' ubwiyunge , iterambere , kwihesha agaciro , kurinda igihugu n' ibindi .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko yatangiye kwandika icyo gitabo , yifuza ko izo mpanuro zikomeza kuba umusemburo w' impinduka nziza mu Rwanda ku bariho ubu n' abazaza nyuma .
Yagize ati " Narebye inama yatanze tukazishingiraho twubaka igihugu nyuma ya Jenoside n' uburyo yabanishije Abanyarwanda , mbona atari byiza ko twajya dukurikira imbwiraruhame ze bisanzwe ngo azivuge zigende zitambuke gusa [ ‚Ä¶ ] Ndavuga nti nubwo nta kwandika impanuro zose yavuze , ariko najya ntoranya amagambo y' ingenzi yagirira abantu akamaro ku buryo abantu basigarana impanuro ze biyubaka ubwabo
banubaka igihugu mu gihe kizaza .
Mutaganzwa yavuze ko impanuro za Perezida Kagame zifitemo ubushobozi bwo gufasha ushaka kubaka igihugu cyangwa umuryango muri rusange ndetse n' umuntu ku giti cye , by' umwihariko urubyiruko .
Ati " Ushaka kubaka igihugu mu buryo bwose cyangwa kwiyubaka ubwawe , iki gitabo cyagufasha ugendeye ku mpanuro za Perezida wa Repubulika .
Urubyiruko nirwo Rwanda rw' ejo , rushingiye rero kuri izi mpanuro za nyakubahwa Perezida wa Repubulika , rwaba ari u Rwanda rumeze nkuko turwifuza .
Iki gitabo kigabanyijemo ibice 12 bivuga ko ngingo zitandukanye Perezida Kagame yagiye agarukaho mu mbwirarwaruhame ze nko kwihesha agaciro icyo ari cyo , kurinda igihugu , guteza imbere igihugu bishingiye kuri ba nyiracyo , inyungo n' isomo ryo guca mu ngorane n' ibindi .
Mutaganzwa yavuze ko igitabo cye " Isoko tuvomaho Impanuro " " " " kizasohoka mu minsi ya vuba ari nabwo kizatangira kuboneka mu maguriro y' ibitabo hirya no hino mu gihugu .
Ububiko bw' amateka : Umudugudu wa Nyirabwana wahoze ari igicumbi cy' ingoma y' u Bwanacyambwe
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza uko ubutaka bw' u Rwanda bwo mu bice bimwe na bimwe bwari buteye bukiri amashyamba , butaraba igihugu gituwe kandi gihingwa , abandi bagakomeza kwibaza cyane ku bugenge n' ubuhanga bukabije buvugwa ku bami bagenganga ibihugu bw' ibikorwa by' ubuhangange bagezeho kandi nta bikoresho bihambaye bari bafite .
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza uko ubutaka bw' u Rwanda bwo mu bice bimwe na bimwe bwari buteye bukiri amashyamba , butaraba igihugu gituwe kandi gihingwa , abandi bagakomeza kwibaza cyane ku bugenge n' ubuhanga bukabije buvugwa ku bami bagenganga ibihugu bw' ibikorwa by' ubuhangange bagezeho kandi nta bikoresho bihambaye bari bafite .
Muri iki gice , tugiye kubatekerereza bimwe mu bimenyetso ndangamateka , bigaragaza imiterere y' imwe mu misozi y' u Rwanda rwo hambere , rutaraturwa ngo rube insinsiro zisakayemo abantu .
Nkuko tubikesha igitabo " Imizi y' u Rwanda " n' igitabo " Intwari z' imbanza , zubatse u Rwanda rugahamya igitinyiro " , byombi dukesha umwanditsi n' umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , tugiye gutekerereza hamwe amateka y' umudugudu wa Nyirabwana wo mu Kagali ka Kibagabaga mu Murenge wa Kimironko ho mu Karere ka Gasabo ahahoze ari ingoma ngabe y' igihugu cy' u Bwanacyambwe mu bihe byo hambere .
Hariho nka kimwe mu bimenyetso bibitse amateka akomeye agaragaza imiterere y' igihugu cy' u Bwanacyambwe mbere y' uko gihangwamo igihugu , n' ikimenyetso kigaragaza bene cyo uburyo bakuturanyije bakagitunganya kikaba igihugu kiganje .
Ubu butaka butaraba igihugu cy' u Bwanacyambwe bwari ubutaka bw' imigina n' ibishanga by' imifunzo by' amasanzure y' umugezi wa Nyabugogo n' Akagera , n' ikiyaga cya Mugesera .
Mu bihe byo hambere , igihugu cy' u Bwanacyambwe cyari gikikijwe n' ingoma y' i Gisaka cy' Abagesera b' Abazirankende mu Burasirazuba , Gasabo y' Abanyiginya mu Majyaruguru , Nduga y' Ababanda mu Burengerazuba bw' Amajyepfo , u Buliza bw' Abongera mu Majyaruguru y' u Burengerazuba n' ingoma y' u Bugesera bw' Abahondogo yari mu Majyepfo .
Igihugu cy' u Bwanacyambwe kimwe n' icy' u Buliza , byagengwaga n' Ibikomangoma by' Abongera , bakomoka kuri Mwongera wa Rurenge Sekuruza wabo .
Aho cyari giherereye kugeza ubwo aya mateka yandikwaga , ni mu Karere ka Nyarugenge , Akarere ka Kicukiro , Akarere ka Gasabo y' Amajyepfo ( Mu Mirenge ya Gisozi , Kinyinya , Kimihurura , Remera na Kimironko ) hamwe n' Akarere ka Rwamagana y' Iburengerazuba ( Mu mirenge ya Karenge , Nyakariro , Nzige , Muyumbu na Gahengeri ) .
Amacishirizo y' ihangwa ry' icyo gihugu , akaba agaragaza ko cyahanzwe mu mizo ya mbere y' iyaguka ry' ibihugu byagengwaga n' Abasinga b' Abasangwabutaka , aho cyahanzwe ahasaga mu wa 450 , nyuma ya Yezu Kirisitu .
Mu ihangwa ry' igihugu cy' u Bwanacyambwe , ryanzuwe n' umuhungu wa Rurenge witwaga Mwongera n' umugore we w' inkundwakazi Nyirabwanacyambwe , ari na we wakurijweho kwitirirwa icyo gihugu kikitwa " u Bwanacyambwe ' .
Agasozi gakuru ari nako kabarwa nk' ubutaka gakondo bw' Abongera , kitwaga Nyirabwanacyambwe , niko ubu kabumbye imidugudu ya Nyirabwana , Ramiro , Rindiro na Kageyo yo mu Kagali ka Kibagabaga , mu Murenge wa Kimironko wo mu Karere ka Gasabo .
Ingoma ngabe y' Abongera ikaba yari itetse mu Mudugudu wa Nyirabwana ( Nyirabwanacyambwe ) wiswe izina ry' impine , aho kuryuzuza ngo witwe " Nyirabwanacyambwe " " " " .
Nyuma y' imyaka amagana , ingoma ngabe yaje kwimurirwa mu Mudugudu wa Amahoro mu Kagali ka Rukiri II mu Murenge wa Remera wo mu Karere ka Gasabo ko mu Mujyi wa Kigali , ari naho hashyiriweho iherezo ryayo ubwo u Bwanacyambwe bwatsindwaga n' u Rwanda mu gitero cyagabwe na Kigeli Mukobanya ahasaga mu wa 1378 , akivugana Nkuba ya Nyabakonjo watwaraga u Bwanacyambwe muri ibyo bihe .
Ubutaka bw' Umudugudu wa Nyirabwana , ni kimwe mu bimenyetso karundura , kigaragaza ko ingoma y' u Bwanacyambwe yabayeho , kandi ikagaragaza n' inkomoko y' iryo zina , n' aho yatangiriye mu bwaguke bwayo .
Imyaka 26 irashize umwamikazi wa nyuma w' u Rwanda , Rosalie Gicanda yishwe
Tariki 20 Mata 1994 nibwo inkuru mbi yakwirakwiye ko umwamikazi wa nyuma w' u Rwanda , Rosalie Gicanda yishwe n' ingabo za Leta yakoraga Jenoside , azizwa ko ari umututsi .
Tariki 20 Mata 1994 nibwo inkuru mbi yakwirakwiye ko umwamikazi wa nyuma w' u Rwanda , Rosalie Gicanda yishwe n' ingabo za Leta yakoraga Jenoside , azizwa ko ari umututsi .
Gicanda yashakanye n' Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa Charles L√©on Pierre Kuwa 13 Mutarama 1942 .
Yabayeho nabi asuzugurwa nyuma y' urupfu rw' umwami Rudahigwa , ubwo yatangiraga i Bujumbura ku buryo bw' amayobera tariki 25 Nyakanga 1959 .
Nyuma yo gutanga kw' umugabo we byajyanye n' ihurura ry' abarwaniraga Repubulika , ariko barushaho gutesha agaciro ingoma ya Cyami n' ibimenyetso byayo .
Mu 1961 Perezida Kayibanda Gr√©goire yirukanye mu rukari Umwamikazi Gicanda .
Yaje gutura mu Mujyi wa Butare mu Karere ka Huye , ari naho abahoze ari abasirikare ba Habyarimana hamwe n' Interahamwe bamusanze bakamwica kuwa 20 Mata 1994 .
Urupfu rw' Umwamikazi Rosali Gicanda
Muri Repubulika ya mbere n' iya kabiri , umwamikazi Gicanda nubwo yari mu gihugu , yabayeho nta gaciro afite nk' uwahoze mu buyobozi bukuru bw' igihugu .
Gicanda wari umuyoboke ukomeye wa Kiliziya Gatolika , yabayeho mu buzima bworoheje mu mujyi wa Huye , abana n' umubyeyi we ndetse n' abandi bagore bake bamufashaga mu mirimo itandukanye .
Ubwo Jenoside yatangiraga , Umwamikazi Gicanda yagiye yishingikiriza Jean Baptiste Habyarimana wari Perefe wa Butare , warwanyije cyane umugambi wo gutsemba Abatutsi .
Tariki 17 Mata , Perefe Habyarimana yatawe muri yombi , nyuma aza kwicwa .
Umwamikazi Rosalia Gicanda yatangiye guterwa ubwoba ko nawe agiye kwicwa n' umuryango we .
Raporo ya Human Rights Watch yasohotse mu 1999 , ivuga ko Umwamikazi Gicanda wari ufite imyaka 66 yasabye Joseph Kanyabashi wari Burugumesitiri wa Komini ya Ngoma i Butare kumurinda , undi akabyanga .
Tariki 20 Mata ahagana saa tanu z' amanywa , abasirikare bayobowe na Lt Pierre Bizimana binjiye mu rugo rw' umwamikazi Gicanda ku mabwiriza yari yatanzwe na Capt Ildephonse Nizeyimana wari umuyobozi ushinzwe ubutasi n' ibikorwa mu ishuri rikuru rya gisirikare , ESO ubwo Jenoside yakorwaga .
Abo basirikare bamaze kwinjira mu rugo rw' umwamikazi , baramufashe we n' abandi bagore batandatu babanaga barabatwara .
Muri urwo rugo hasigaye mama wa Gicanda wari ufite imyaka 80 n' undi mukobwa wo kumwitaho .
Abasirikare bafashe Gicanda n' abo bari bafatanywe bajyana inyuma y' ingoro y' inzu ndangamurage y' u Rwanda barabarasa , barapfa .
Ku gicamunsi abasirikare bagarutse mu rugo rwa Gicanda gusahura , hashize iminsi ibiri baragaruka bica umubyeyi we .
Raporo ya Huma Rihgts Watch ivuga ko hari umupadiri wasabye ko umubiri wa Gicanda washyingurwa mu cyubahiro , burugumesitiri Kanyabashi yohereza abagororwa bo kuwujyana bawushyingura hafi y' urugo rwe .
Umwe mu baganiriye n' umukobwa wabashije kurokoka witaga ku mubyeyi wa Gicanda , ngo yamubwiye ko mbere y' uko Gicanda n' abo bari kumwe bicwa babanje kuvuga isengesho bishyira mu maboko y' Imana .
Muri 2012 , urukiko rwashyiriweho u Rwanda rwakatiye Capt Ildephonse Nizeyimana igifungo cya burundu ashinjwa kwica Umwamikazi Gicanda n' abandi batutsi muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Nizeyimana yari yafatiwe muri Uganda mu 2009 .
Mu 1998 Lt Pierre Bizimana yakatiwe urwo gupfa n' urukiko rwa gisirikare i Kigali ariko icyo gihano kiza guhindurwamo igifungo cya burundu nyuma y' uko u Rwanda rukuyeho igihano cy' urupfu .
Umwamikazi wicishaga bugufi , akagira impuhwe
Ababanye n' abazi neza Umwamikazi Gicanda , bavuga ko yari umubyeyi wicisha bugufi kandi agakunda abantu bose atarobanuye .
Mu buhamya Perezida Paul Kagame yatanze mu 2017 avuga ku mateka y' ubuto bwe kuva afite imyaka ine y' amavuko ubwo yatangiraga ubuzima bw' ubuhunzi , yashimiye na Gicanda nk' umwe mu bamufashije akabasha kurokoka .
Ubwo buhamya bugaragara mu nimero 2944 ya Jeune Afrique yasohotse ku wa 11 Kamena 2017 , yiswe amabanga y' ubuto [ Secrets de Jeunesse ] bw' abakuru b' ibihugu barimo Perezida Kagame , Ali Bongo Ondimba , Umwami Mohammed VI wa Maroc na Alpha Cond√© .
Perezida Kagame yasobanuye ko mu 1961 mbere gato y' uko u Rwanda rubona ubwigenge , ubwo yari afite imyaka ine , Abahutu bari batuye ku musozi wa Tambwe bashyigikiwe n' ubuyobozi , bigabije aho umuryango we wari utuye batwika inzu zaho ndetse bagirira nabi Abatutsi .
Icyo gihe umubyeyi we yatangiye kumutegura ngo bahunge .
Hahise haza imodoka , umushoferi wayo ashyikiriza umubyeyi wa Perezida Kagame ibaruwa ivuga ko atumwe n' Umwamikazi Gicanda wari utuye i Nyanza mu rugendo rw' iminota nka 45 uvuye aho bo bari batuye .
Rosalie Gicanda yari amusabye kubahungisha muri ibyo bihe by' amakuba .
Perezida Kagame n' abantu bari baturanye binjiye muri iyo modoka mu gihe igihiriri cy' ababahigaga cyaturukaga ku wundi musozi , gihita cyirara mu byo bari batunze .
Icyo gihe ngo basanze Umwamikazi i Nyanza , mbere y' uko bafata inzira bakerekeza mu Mutara aho naho ubwicanyi bwabasanze bakabuhungira muri Uganda .
Gicanda yavukiye i Rwamagana mu 1928 .
Yakuze arangwa n' ikinyabupfura ari nabyo byatumye abengukwa n' Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa .
Umwamikazi Gicanda aruhukiye i Mwima ya Nyanza ahatabarijwe Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa na Kigeli V Ndahindurwa .
Buri mwaka tariki 20 Mata hategurwa gahunda yo kwibuka Umwamikazi Rosalie Gicanda , itegurwa ku bufatanye bw' umuryango we n' ubuyobozi bw' Ikigo cy' Igihugu cy' Ingoro Ndangamurage z' u Rwanda .
Ibigwi n' ibirindiro : Amateka n' ibigwi by' inka mu Rwanda ( Igice cya mbere )
Abatekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda n' abayatekererezwa , bakunze gutangaza byinshi ku mateka y' ibigwi by' inka mu Rwanda rugari rwa Gasabo , inka yafatiweho ibintu byinshi mu mateka y' u Rwanda no mu ruhando mpuzamahanga .
Abatekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda n' abayatekererezwa , bakunze gutangaza byinshi ku mateka y' ibigwi by' inka mu Rwanda rugari rwa Gasabo , inka yafatiweho ibintu byinshi mu mateka y' u Rwanda no mu ruhando mpuzamahanga .
Muri iki gice tugiye kubavunguriraho gato ku bigwi n' ibirindiro by' amateka y' ibigwi by' inka mu Rwanda , dore ko utabikuyeho akamanyu nibura gato gato , utashobora kubiva imuzi ngo ubigere imuzingo .
Nk' uko tubikesha igitabo " Intwari z' imbanza , zubatse u Rwanda rugahamya igitinyiro " cyanditswe n' Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere ku Muco , ubusizi n' amateka , tubimburiye ku iyinjira ry' inka mu Rwanda n' uko zatejwe imbere zikaba urufatiro rukomeye rw' ibintu byinshi mu mateka .
Inka ifite ibisekuruza byinshi mu mateka y' Afurika , aho bisaga imyaka 3000 .
Inka zahanganywe n' u Rwanda , aho zadukanywe n' Abasangwabutaka b' Abasinga n' Abazigaba ahasaga mu wa 300 .
Abanyiginya bahasesekaye , bateje imbere cyane ubworozi bw' inka bituma inka zose zo mu gihugu bazitirirwa , aho mu mateka bagira bati " Gihanga niwe wahanze inka n' ingoma " .
Bikomoye ku kuba Abanyiginya aribo bahaye intera ndende n' urwego rw' ikirenga ubworozi bw' inka , ziba nyinshi mu gihugu .
Inka yahawe intera iyingayinga iy' umuntu .
Aho mu Bucurabwenge bw' inka , bagiraga bati " Inka ni imfura , kuko upfa ikakurerera , wabumbira ( wabura amashereka ) ikakugoboka , ikakurwanyiriza indwara z' ibyorezo n' ubujyahabi " " " " .
Inka niyo yarangaga ubukire , Inka niyo yari ipfundo ry' ubuhake nk' akazi ko hambere , Intwari yo ku rugamba yagororerwaga inka , Inka yungaga inshuti , Inka yahuzaga inshuti ( abahanaga inka , babaga babaye inshuti ) , Inka bayikwaga umugeni nk' ikimenyetso cy' uburere bwiza .
Mu Kinyejana cya Munani nyuma ya Yezu , ni ukuvuga ahasaga mu wa 700 , nibwo hadutse ishyanga rishya mu Rwanda , ari ryo ryaje kuvamo umuryango mugari w' Abanyiginya , baza n' ubundi , bagowe n' iyimukayimuka ryabo n' umutungo wabo urangajwe imbere n' inka bagendaga bashakira inzuri zitoshye kandi ngari .
Mu gusesekara mu Rwanda , binjiriye bwa mbere mu Gihugu cy' u Rweya rw' u Mubali ( mu mirenge ya Murundi na Mwili yo mu Karere ka Kayonza na Rwimbogo yo mu Karere ka Gatsibo ) .
Kuko ubutaka bubereye ubworozi bw' inka zabo bari babugezeho , bishimiye umukenke w' Iburasirazuba bw' u Rwanda , ugaragiwe n' ubutohe bw' umurambi w' ubutaka bwiganjemo icyogogo cy' uruzi rw' Akagera , ibiyaga bya Rwanyakiziga , Nasho , Ihema n' ibindi .
Imyaka isaga 300 ( 700 - 1091 ) , umuryango mugari w' Abanyiginya wamaze mu busembere mu ngoma y' u Rweya rw' Abazigaba , nta kindi cyera cyangwa se cyirabura bakoze , usibye guteza imbere ubworozi bw' inka , bakora ubugenge n' ubuhanga bwo kuzibangurira kugira ngo zirusheho kororoka , maze nazo zirabakundira ziroroka karahava ! !
Aha akaba ari naho , bakuye umwihariko w' inka zitirirwa u Rwanda z' Inyambo aribyo bivuga " Itungo ry' intoranywa " .
Imisozi yose bacumbikiwemo , yari yiganjemo inzuri z' inka , aho gutura ari hato , ku buryo aribo ba mbere bateje imbere gutura mu nsisiro mu rwego rwo kurinda akajagari mu miturire byari kugabanya ingano y' inzuri z' inka zabo .
Mu misozi batuyemo myinshi kuri ubu ibarizwa mu Karere ka Gatsibo ¬æ byayo byari inzuri z' inka .
Muri yo twavuga Imisozi ya Nyagihanga , Rugarama , Ngarama , Kabarore , Gitoki , Gatsibo na Kageyo
Imisozi batuyemo muri ibyo bihe , ari nayo baremyemo insisiro , ni mu mu Murenge wa Remera na Muhura yo mu Karere ka Gatsibo .
Uko imyaka yashiraga indi igataha , niko Abanyiginya barushagaho guteza imbere ubworozi bw' inka , ari nako butuma bagira ijambo ry' icyizerabuhake mu Rweya , kugeza ubwo byabahesheje ijambo mu nzu y' ubwami bwabo , banashakamo abagore b' ibikomangoma .
Muri bo twavuga nka Nyirarukangaga rwa Nyamigezi ya Kabeja , washatswe na Kazi ka Kizira , bakabyarana Gihanga .
Abanyiginya bakomeje kugwiza ubutunzi bw' inka , amashyo n' amagana , bibaha imbaraga n' icyubahiro cy' ikirenga , kugeza ubwo ibwami batangiye kubakeka amababa ko bashobora kuzabambura ingoma , ari nabwo Gihanga yabimenyaga agashyira nzira akabahunga ajya guhanga igihugu cye mu bisigara by' ubutaka Abasangwabutaka banennye , akabuhangaho igihugu cy' i Gasabo .
Gihanga , akimara guhanga Gasabo , Umuryango mugari w' Abanyiginya akomokamo akawukura mu busembere mu ngoma y' u Rweya , yashyizeho igenamigambi ryeruye rishingiye ku nka mu kubaka igihugu cye .
Inka ihabwa umwanya ukomeye mu buzima bwose bw' igihugu , aho yifashishwaga muri Politiki z' igihugu zitandukanye nko mu Bubanyi n' amahanga , mu kubaka ubukungu bw' igihugu , mu mutekano no mu ntambara zo kwigarurira amahanga , mu mibereho myiza y' abaturage , mu mibanire n' ubumwe bw' abenegihugu n' ibindi .
Inka yayishyize mu igamigambi ry' ububanyi n' amahanga n' ubutwererane n' abami b' ibindi bihugu bituranyi by' u Rwanda ku buryo yagombaga guhuza u Rwanda n' ibihugu by' inshuti kandi ikagabirwa abami b' ibihugu byanga u Rwanda , bityo bikagabanya urwango , ubundi rukabasha gukora ibikorwa by' iterambere rwifuza .
Inka yabaye inkingi ya mwamba yo kurwanya umwanzi w' imbere mu gihugu .
Umwanzi w' imbere mu gihugu , burya ni ubukene .
Iyo umunyarwanda atakennye , nta nabi agira , kandi umwanzi wo hanze y' igihugu ntiyabona aho yinjirira , kuko uwakamubereye icyitso wo mu gihugu hagati , baba baramugushije ruhabo .
Nuko Gihanga , agena gahunda zo kugabira abaturage inka ku buntu , kugira ngo biteze imbere , ubundi amahoro ahinde mu miryango yabo .
Inka yashyizwe mu rwego rwo gufasha igihugu mu kugera ku mutekano n' intwaro yo guhashya amahanga adakunda u Rwanda .
Niho Gihanga , yahereyeho ashyiraho gahunda yo kugabira inka Ingabo zose z' igihugu , kugira ngo zirusheho kwitabira intambara zo kwivuna abanzi , no kugira imbaduko ku rugamba rwo kwagura igihugu .
Inka yafatiweho umurongo mugari wo kwigarurira imitima y' abaturage b' ibindi bihugu u Rwanda rwashakaga kwigarurira .
Aho buri muturage u Rwanda rwabaga rwanyaze mu bitero byo kurwagura , yahabwaga inka nyinshi zo korora zikamufasha kwikura mu bukene , bityo akinjira muri Paradizo nshya y' igihugu cy' u Rwanda , irimo amata n' ubuki , umutima akawukura kuri gakondo y' iwabo , akaganza i Rwanda .
Gahunda yo kugabira abaturage b' ibindi bihugu banyazwe n' u Rwanda , yatumye benshi mu baturage batoroka ibihugu byabo , biyizira mu Rwanda , bahabwa inka zo korora , ubundi batangira gutanga amakuru y' imbamutima y' uburyo u Rwanda ruzigarurira ibihugu bakomokamo .
Ubukungu bw' ibihugu mu bihe byo hambere , bwari abaturage ku isonga , ubundi butunzi bugakurikiraho , ari nayo mpamvu u Rwanda , rwihatiye kwigarurira abaturage b' ibindi bihugu , rwifashishije inka .
Impamvu igitabo kidakwiriye kubura mu mpano uha uwo ukunda
Mu buzima bw' umuntu bwa buri munsi , akenera kugura ikintu akeneye kimuneza , kimukemurira ibibazo , kimuteza imbere ndetse kinamwubaka .
Mu buzima bw' umuntu bwa buri munsi , akenera kugura ikintu akeneye kimuneza , kimukemurira ibibazo , kimuteza imbere ndetse kinamwubaka .
Abantu bamwe baha agaciro kadakwiye igitabo , ntibazi ko igitabo aricyo shingiro ry' iterambere rirambye , ishingiro ry' ubuzima bwiza , ishingiro ry' ubwenge , ishingiro ry' imibereho myiza , ishingiro ryo kubaka igihugu , ishingiro ryo gusigasira igihango ndetse igitabo ni ishingiro ryo kugira igenamigambi rirambye .
Njya nibaza ibibazo bikurikira : Kuki umuntu agura umwenda w' ibihumbi ijana ariko akumva atagura igitabo cy' ibihumbi ijana ?
Kuki umuntu agura mudasobwa y' ibihumbi magana atanu ariko akumva atagura igitabo cy' ibihumbi magana atanu ?
Kuki umuntu agura ururabo rwo guha inshuti ye ariko akaba atamuha impano y' igitabo ?
Mu mwaka wa 2016 , hari inshuti yanjye yitwa Ken Chartrand twigeze kuganira turi gutembera i New York , ambwira ko mu mpano nziza ashobora guha umuntu akunda ko hadashobora kuburamo igitabo , mubajije impamvu arambwira ngo igitabo ni inshuti nziza muganira ukunguka ubwenge n' ubuhanga , kikaba urwibutso rurambye kandi rudashira .
Ken yambwiye ko igitabo ari urwibutso rw' ubushuti , ko buri kwezi agura ibitabo bibiri byo gusoma kandi ko adashobora kuryama adasomye igitabo kuko gituma aruhuka neza , akunguka ubumenyi burushijeho .
Nyuma y' ikiganiro twagiranye , nahise nkunda birushijeho igitabo , mpitamo kwimakaza umuco wo kwandika , kugura ndetse no gusoma ibitabo .
Kugeza ubu maze kwandika ibitabo bine .
Mu biro byanjye harimo ibitabo naguze nsoma kenshi , mu rugo umuryango wanjye nawuguriye ibitabo byo gusoma kandi bamaze kubikunda .
Birakwiye ko twimakaza uyu muco mwiza ufasha kubaka u Rwanda twifuza ndetse n' Afurika , tugura ibitabo , tubiha agaciro gakomeye , tubitangamo impano ku nshuti dukunda , tubisoma aho turi hose , bityo bizadufashe kurushaho gutera imbere dufite ubuhanga bwimbitse .
Ibi kandi bizadufasha kwihuta mu iterambere ndetse turusheho kumenya aho tuva , aho tugeze ndetse n' icyerekezo cy' u Rwanda na Afurika .
Bizadufasha kurushaho kuba abarinzi b' ibyagezweho mu Rwanda no muri Afurika bityo tubisigasire ndetse tunabyubakireho ibindi bikorwa byinshi kandi byiza .

Imiryango yahamije ubuhangange mu mateka : Igicumbi cy' Umuryango w' Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka
Mu mateka y' abakurambere mpangarwanda , hari imiryango yagiye ihamya ibirindiro , ikavugwa cyane ku bw' ibigwi n' ibirindiro yabaga yarakoreye igihugu , hagati mu muryango mugari ikomokamo .
Mu mateka y' abakurambere mpangarwanda , hari imiryango yagiye ihamya ibirindiro , ikavugwa cyane ku bw' ibigwi n' ibirindiro yabaga yarakoreye igihugu , hagati mu muryango mugari ikomokamo .
Muri iki gice tukaba tugiye kubimburira ku mateka y' igicumbi cy' umuryango mugari ufite inkomoko ku Mwami Yuhi Mazimpaka twifashishije igitabo " Iyororoka ry' Abanyarwanda , inkomoko y' imiryango migari " dukesha Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere mu Busizi , Umuco n' Amateka y' u Rwanda .
Yuhi III Mazimpaka ni mwene Sekarongoro Gisanura cya Kigeli Nyamuheshera , Umunyiginya wo mu nzu y' Abaganzu na Nyamarembo ya Majinya , ukomoka mu muryango mugari w' Abakono , wategetse ahasaga mu wa 1642 kugeza mu wa 1675 .
Ni umwami wa 18 muri 28 bategetse u Rwanda , akaba n' umwami wa 18 mu Berekeza 34 b' umushinga wo kubaka u Rwanda , kugeza ubwo aya mateka yandikwaga .
Izina rye ry' ubutwari ryari " Insarikanamakuza .
Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka ni umwe mu Bami b' u Rwanda bagize inzu z' imiryango nyinshi ugereranyije n' abandi bami , akaba akurikira Ndoba na we wagize inzu z' imiryango ntabarika .
Amateka atugaragariza ko Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka ya Gisanura , yabyaye abana benshi , biganjemo abahungu 10 barimo Rwaka , Rujugira , Nyarwaya , Gakomba , Mureganshuro , Gapfizi , Mukungu , Mukuku , Rushara na Bukombe .
Umuryango w' Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka wabayemo ingabo z' ibikongote ku ngoma ye n' iy' umuhungu we Cyilima Rujugira wamuzunguye ku ngoma .
Banabaye abagaba b' ingabo b' intahusha mu gihe cye .
Imitwe y' Ingabo yatwarwaga n' abahungu be , irimo Indara zatwarwagwa na Mukungu wa Yuhi Mzimpaka ,
Inkoramaraso : Zatwarwaga na Mukungu wa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Abashahuzi : Batwarwaga na Nyarwaya Karuretwa wa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Ababaga : Batwarwaga na Nyarwaya Karuretwa wa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Ababanda : Batwarwaga na Nyarwaya Karuretwa wa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Inkuba : Zatwarwaga na Mureganshuro ya Yuhi Mazimpaka
Abakungu : Batwarwaga na Mureganshuro ya Yuhi Mazimpaka
Abatabaga : Batwarwaga na Yuhi Mazimpaka za Gisanura
Intaremba : Zatwarwaga na Yuhi Mazimpaka ya Gisanura
Hari n' ababaye abagaba b' ingabo ku ngoma y' umuhungu we akaba n' umuvandimwe wabo Cyilima Rujugira , aribo aba bakurikira :
Abakemba : Batwarwaga na Sharangabo ya Cyilima Rujugira ,
Imvejuru : Zatwarwaga na Sharangabo ya Cyilima Rujugira ,
Indirira ( Rugamba ) : Zatwarwaga na Muciye ya Serutaro rwa Mukuku wa Mazimpaka ,
Abarima : Batwarwaga na Mitunga ya Cyilima Rujugira n' umugabo we Seruhuga ,
Abatanyagwa : Batwarwaga na Gihana cya Cyilima Rujugira ,
Intarindwa : Zatwarwaga na Ndabarasa ba Cyilima Rujugira ,
Ababito : Batwarwaga na Ndabarasa ba Cyilima Rujugira ,
Indara : Zatwarwaga na Cyilima Rujugira rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ,
Ababanda : Batwarwaga na Cyilima Rujugira rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Aba bagabo b' Intarumikwa , ni bo babaye inkomoko y' inzu z' imiryango zo kwa Mazimpaka zikomoka mu muryango mugari w' Abanyiginya .
Inzu z' imiryango zikomoka kwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ni izi zikurikira :
Abanyiginya b' ABAKA bakomoka kuri Karemera Rwaka rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka
Abanyiginya b' ABAYA bakomoka kuri Nyarwaya rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya b' ABASIGAYE bakomoka kuri Nsigaye ya Gakombe ka Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya b' Abahwege bakomoka kuri Segahwege ka Nsigaye ya Gakombe ka Yuhi mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya b' ABAPFIZI bakomoka kuri Gapfizi ka Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya b' ABAREGANSHURO bakomoka kuri Mureganshuro ya Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya b' Abashamakokera bakomoka kuri Shamakokera ya Ndabaramiye wa Bukombe bwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya b' ABASAMANZI bakomoka kuri Rwasamanzi rwa Mukungu ya Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya b' Abakuku bakomoka kuri Mukuku wa Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Abanyiginya b' Abashara bakomoka kuri Rushara rwa Yuhi Mazimpaka ;
Izindi nzu zihamye mu mateka y' u Rwanda zikomoka kwa Yuhi Mazimpaka , harimo n' izo kwa Cyilima Rujugira umuhungu we w' ubuheta wabaye umwami wa Rubanda akamuzungura ku ngoma .
Inzu zimukomokaho zirimo Abanyiginya b' Abadenge bakomoka kuri Mudenge wa Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyiginya b' Abakore bakomoka kuri Kanyankore ka Kanyoni ka Baziga ba Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyiginya b' Abahabanyi bakomoka kuri Bihabanyi bya Gashikazi ka Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyiginya b' Abamo bakomoka kuri Rwamo rwa Gihana cya Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyiginya b' Abanana bakomoka kuri Munana wa Gihana cya Cyilima Rujugira ;
Abanyigiya b' Abasharangabo bakomoka kuri Sharangabo ya Cyilima Rujugira .
Abanyabugeni b' abagore bahawe umwihariko mu kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w' Ingoro Ndangamurage
U Rwanda ruritegura kwifatanya n' Isi mu birori by' Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Ndangamurage uzizihizwa hatangizwa imurika ry' ibihangano by' ubugeni by' abahanzi b' abari n' abategarugori .
U Rwanda ruritegura kwifatanya n' Isi mu birori by' Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Ndangamurage uzizihizwa hatangizwa imurika ry' ibihangano by' ubugeni by' abahanzi b' abari n' abategarugori .
Buri mwaka tariki 18 Gicurasi Isi yizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Ndangamurage , hazirikanwa umuco , amateka n' imibereho gakondo by' abatuye Isi .
U Rwanda narwo rwifatanya n' amahanga mu kwizihiza uwo munsi ushimangira agaciro ko guhererekanya amateka no guteza imbere umuco ufatwa nk' umusingi w' imibereho y' igihugu .
Urwa Gasabo rubarizwa mu Muryango Mpuzamahanga w' Ingoro Ndangamurage ( ICOM ) uhuriyemo abanyamuryango basaga 44 000 bakora mu ngoro ndangamurage 20 000 zo mu bihugu 138 .
Muri uyu mwaka , uyu munsi wahawe insanganyamatsiko ivuga ku kugira " Ingoro ndangamurage zigamije uburinganire , ubudasa no kudaheza " .
Kuri iyi nshuro iki gikorwa cyateguwe mu buryo bwihariye aho hazifashishwa ikoranabuhanga bitewe n' ingamba zashyizweho zo guhangana n' ikwirakwira ry' icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Ni muri urwo rwego Ingoro ndangamurage zo mu bihugu binyamuryango bya ICOM zasabwe kucyizihiza hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga .
Ikigo cy' Ingoro z' Igihugu z' Umurage w' u Rwanda ( INMR ) cyizizihiza ibi birori hafungurwa ku mugaragaro imurika rishya mu Ngoro y' Ubugeni n' Ubuhanzi iherereye i Kanombe , ku wa 18 Gicurasi 2020 .
Iri murika ry' ibihangano by' ubugeni ryahawe insanganyamatsiko ivuga iti " Ubutumwa bw' abanyabugeni b' Abanyarwandakazi : Uburinganire kuri bose .
Ni insanganyamatsiko yari yagenwe ku Munsi Mpuzamahanga w' Abari n' Abategarugori [ yasubitswe kubera ingamba zo guhangana na Coronavirus ] , ariko inahurirana n' iyatanzwe na ICOM uyu mwaka wa 2020 .
Iyo urebye mu byiciro bitandukanye bibarizwamo abari n' abategarugori mu Rwanda , usanga baragize uruhare mu bikorwa by' iterambere ry' ubukungu n' imibereho myiza y' abaturage nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ; ariko basigara inyuma mu bijyanye n' ubugeni bitewe n' impamvu zirimo ubushobozi buke , kubura amahugurwa ahagije mu bijyanye n' ubugeni n' izindi mbogamizi zo mu buzima busanzwe .
Ushingiye no ku bihangano bimuritse mu Ngoro y' Ubugeni n' Ubuhanzi y' i Kanombe " Hari icyuho kinini hagati y' ibihangano by' abagore n' abagabo .
Ibi ntibisobanuye ko badashoboye , bafite impano muri bo kuko na bake bari muri uwo mwuga bakora ibihangano byiza cyane , bimwe muri byo bifite ubwiza burenze ibya basaza babo .
Imurika rizakorwa nk' uburyo bwo gukora ubukangurambaga mu bari n' abategarugori , binyuze mu butumwa bukubiye mu nsanganyamatsiko y' imurika no mu bihangano byabo byateguwe kandi bizamurikwa , bakangurirwa kwigirira icyizere , gutinyuka no kugaragaza impano bafite mu by' ubugeni .
Iri murika ryateguwe hagamijwe gufasha abahanzikazi bato no kubaharurira inzira zo kungukira mu bikorwa byabo ; gufasha abanyabugeni b' abagore gutegura ibikorwa byo kumurika ibihangano byabo ; kwerekana agaciro ko gushora mu bushobozi bw' umugore no kubafasha kugeza imishinga yabo ku rwego mpuzamahanga , byanafasha abandi kubigiraho .
Rizahuza abanyabugeni b' abari n' abategarugori 35 bo mu bihugu bitandatu birimo u Rwanda , Amerika , u Bufaransa , u Bubiligi , Serbia na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
INMR yateguye iri murika ifatanyije n' Ikigo Ndangamuco cy' Abadage Goethe Institut - Kigali .
Ibyo bigo byombi byafashije abari n' abategarugori b' abanyabugeni mu kuritegura , kubaha amahugurwa n' ubushobozi bwo gukora ibihangano byabo no gutunganya imurika riboneye .
Umuhango wo kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w' Ingoro Ndangamurage uzanyuzwa kuri murandasi ( Webex ) ku wa 18 Gicurasi 2020 saa Cyenda .
Abifuza kuwukurikirana baziyandikisha bohereza ubutumwa kuri [ email protected ] cyangwa bakandikira ikigo banyuze ku mbuga nkoranyambaga .
Biteganyijwe ko umukozi w' Ingoro ndangamurage azasobanurira abazakurikira iki gikorwa ibijyanye n' imurika , ababwira ubutumwa bukubiye mu bihangano bigize imurika nkuko bigenda mu gihe bari gusura bisanzwe .
U Rwanda rufite Ingoro z' Umurage umunani zimuritse umurage n' amateka by' igihugu ku mibereho y' abagituye , imyemerere , imyidagaduro , imyambarire , imiziro n' imiziririzo , amateka yacyo .
Nyuma ya gahunda ya Guma mu rugo yashyizweho mu kwirinda ikwirakwira rya COVID - 19 , ibikorwa byo gufungura imiryango ku basura ingoro ndangamurage byarasubukuwe ku wa 5 Gicurasi 2020 .
Imihango n' imigenzo yakorwaga n' Abanyarwanda mu kwirukana ibiza n' ibyorezo
Mu bihe byo ha mbere mu Rwanda iyo hadukaga ibiza by' umwuzure n' amapfa n' ibyorezo by' indwara z' abantu n' amatungo bikayogoza igihugu , habagaho imihango n' imigenzo yakorwaga kugira ngo ibyo byorezo bigende .
Mu bihe byo ha mbere mu Rwanda iyo hadukaga ibiza by' umwuzure n' amapfa n' ibyorezo by' indwara z' abantu n' amatungo bikayogoza igihugu , habagaho imihango n' imigenzo yakorwaga kugira ngo ibyo byorezo bigende .
Imihango yakorwaga ahanini yabaga ishingiye ku biteganywa n' Ubwiru , umwuga w' Ubupfumu , Ubuvubyi Ubuhennyi , Ubuhoryo n' Ubuhaditsi .
Igitabo " Imizi y' u Rwanda " " " " cyanditswe n' Umusizi Nsanzabera Jean de Dieu , inzobere mu muco , amateka n' Ubuvanganzo , havugwamo ko buri cyorezo cyateraga u Rwanda , habaga hari uburyo bwateguwe bwo kucyohera cyangwa kukirukana bakoreshejwe imwe muri iyo migenzo n' imihango yashyizwe u Rwanda rwahangwaga .
Inzira ya Kivu : Ni inzira yabagamo urwunge rw' imihango yakorwaga mu gihe mu gihugu habaga hateye umwuzure ukangiza byinshi mu gihugu .
Bakoraga imihango yo kwirunka uwo mwuzure .
Inzira ya Muhekenyi : Ni inzira yabagamo urwunge rw' imihango yakorwaga mu gihe habaga hateye ibyonnyi n' indwara z' amatungo , bityo hagakorwa imihango n' imigenzo yo kuyohera .
Nyuma y' imihango y' ibwami ijyanye n' ubwiru bwo kohera ibiza n' ibyorezo , hakurikiragaho abahanga gakondo mu kuvura icyateye icyo cyorezo no kucyohera ntikizagaruke .
Bamwe muri bo bakoraga iyo mihango , ni aba bakurikira :
Abavubyi : Mu Rwanda rwo ha mbere , abavubyi bari bafite umumaro uhanitse mu mibereho myiza y' abaturage cyane cyane mu buhinzi .
Umwuga wabo gakondo wari uwo kuvuba imvura ikagwa iyo yabaga yahagamye , no kuyohera ikagenda iyo yabaga yaciye ibintu .
Iyo habaga hateye amapfa cyangwa se umwuzure , icyo gihe nibwo abavubyi nk' inzobere mu kumanura imvura bahagurukaga bagakora imihango yo kuyimanura ikagwa , amapfa akagenda .
Iyo yabaga yaciye ibintu hakaba umwuzure , nabwo bakoraga imihango yo kuyohera .
Abahoryo : Abahoryo nabo ni bamwe mu banyamihango b' ibwami bagiraga uruhare runini ku gukurikirana ibihingwa mu murima no kuvura ibyonnyi by' indwara zabaga zadutse mu myaka .
Barahagurukaga bagakora imihango yo kuvuma ibyo byonnyi no kuvuguta imiti yo kubyamurura ku butaka bw' u Rwanda .
Abahaditsi : Ni bamwe mu banyamihango b' ibwami bari bagiraga uruhare runini ku gukurikirana indwara z' amatungo zabaga zadutse mu bworozi bw' I Rwanda .
Icyo gihe nibwo Abahaditsi barahagurukaga bagakora imihango yo kuvuguta imiti yo kubyamurura mu Rwanda .
Abahennyi : Abahennyi nabo bari bamwe mu banyamihango b' ibwami bifashishwaga mu kuvura indwara z' ibyorezo zibasiye abantu no kuvuma ababisha banga u Rwanda .
Iyo habaga hateye ibyorezo by' indwara , icya mbere bakoraga ni ukumenya inkomoko yabyo , basanga ari ibirogano bagahenera uwabikoze akaba ikivume , basanga ari icyorezo cy' inzaduka bakagishakira amasubyo yo kucyohera .
Nibo batangaga amasubyo yo kuvura amahumane , ibinyoro , ubushita n' izindi .
Mu kwamurura no kohera ibyozezo by' indwara z' abantu n' amatungo , Abanyarwanda bifashishaga kandi amazi y' ubuhoro , yeza igihugu agakiza ubwandure akamurura ibiza by' indwara n' umuze byazengereje igihugu .
Bigaragaza ko kuva kera Abanyarwanda bari bafite ubuhanga n' ubushobozi bifashishaga mu guhashya umwanzi w' ubuzima bwabo n' ibyabo .
Ni abantu bakoresheje ubwenge bw' umwimerere mu kwirwanaho bahagarara ku buzima bwabo ngo butaganzwa n' ibyorezo by' indwara n' ibiza by' amapfa n' imyuzure .

Ikibazo ni uko barakariye umuntu utari we .
Yavuze ko abayobozi icyo bashinzwe ari ugushyiraho imirongo migari no gufasha abagize igitekerezo kizima ariko badashinzwe gutekerereza umuntu .
Mutabazi yagaragaje ko ikibazo kiri ahantu hatandukanye harimo n' uburezi , aho umwarimu atanga bike ku munyeshuri cyangwa se umwanya munini bakawumara biga ibyo batazakoresha mu buzima .

Simba SC ikinamo Kagere Meddie yegukanye Shampiyona ya Tanzania ku nshuro ya gatatu yikurikiranya
Simba SC ikinamo Umunyarwanda Kagere Meddie , yegukanye igikombe cya gatatu cyikurikiranya cya Shampiyona y' Icyiciro cya Mbere muri Tanzania nyuma yo kunganya ubusa ku busa na Tanzania Prisons mu mukino wabaye kuri iki Cyumweru kuri Stade Sokoine i Mbeya .
Simba SC ikinamo Umunyarwanda Kagere Meddie , yegukanye igikombe cya gatatu cyikurikiranya cya Shampiyona y' Icyiciro cya Mbere muri Tanzania nyuma yo kunganya ubusa ku busa na Tanzania Prisons mu mukino wabaye kuri iki Cyumweru kuri Stade Sokoine i Mbeya .
Muri uyu mukino w' umunsi wa 32 , umuholandi Sven Vandenbroeck yari yagiriye icyizere Kagere Meddie wakinnye iminota yose y' umukino .
Simba SC yari ikeneye inota rimwe kugira ngo yegukanye igikombe nyuma y' uko Azam FC yanganyije na Biashara United igitego 1 - 1 ikagira amanota 59 mu gihe Yanga SC yatsinze Ndanda FC ibitego 3 - 2 ku wa Gatanu , ikagira amanota 60 .
Umunyezamu wa Tanzania Prisons , Jeremiah Kasubi na Aishi Manula urinda izamu rya Simba SC bagize uruhare rukomeye mu gutuma uyu mukino urangira nta gitego kiwubonetsemo .
Kunganya byatumye Simba SC igira amanota 79 mu mikino 32 , yegukana igikombe harimo ikinyuranyo cy' amanota 19 mu gihe hasigaye imikino itandatu .
Ni ku nshuro ya gatatu yikurikiranya iyi kipe yegukanye iki gikombe mu gihe ari ku nshuro ya 21 yegukanye shampiyona ya Tanzania , irushwa inshuro eshanu na Yanga SC igifite inshuro 26 .
Kuri Kagere Meddie , ni igikombe cya kabiri cya shampiyona yegukanye ari kumwe na Simba SC nyuma yo kuyigeramo mu mwaka w' imikino wa 2018 / 19 , avuye muri Gor Mahia FC yo muri Kenya .
Biteganyijwe ko Simba SC izashyikirizwa igikombe mu mikino iri imbere bitewe n' ibiganiro bizahuza ubuyobozi bwayo n' abayobora Ishyirahamwe ry' Umupira w' Amaguru muri Tanzania ( TFF ) .

Kuri iki Cyumweru tariki ya 27 Kamena nibwo hashyizwe ahagaragara imikino izakinwa hagati ya tariki ya 30 Nyakanga n' iya 14 Kanama 2020 .

Muri iri subukurwa rya NBA , buri munsi hazajya hakinwa imikino igera kuri irindwi ku bibuga bitatu bitandukanye byo muri ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex .
Buri kipe izabarwa nk' iyakiriye imikino ine ndetse yongere kugirwa nk' iyakiniye hanze mu yindi mikino ine .
Ubwo NBA yasubikwagwa tariki ya 11 Werurwe , hari hasigaye imikino 259 mu mwaka usanzwe w' imikino ariko hazakinwa 88 gusa .
Amakipe 22 azakina iyi mikino ni umunani yari aya mbere muri buri gace ( conference ) [ ni ukuvuga ane muri buri gace ] kongeraho andi atandatu ( atanu yo mu Burengerazuba n' imwe yo mu Burasirazuba ) hagendewe ku manota yari afite .

Inama ya Komite Nyobozi y' Impuzamashyirahamwe y' Umupira w' Amaguru ku Mugabane w' Uburayi ( UEFA ) yabaye kuri uyu wa Gatatu , yanzuye ko amarushanwa yayo ya Champions League na Europa League azasubukurwa mu ntangiriro za Kanama nyuma y' uko ahagaritswe muri Werurwe kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Inama ya Komite Nyobozi y' Impuzamashyirahamwe y' Umupira w' Amaguru ku Mugabane w' Uburayi ( UEFA ) yabaye kuri uyu wa Gatatu , yanzuye ko amarushanwa yayo ya Champions League na Europa League azasubukurwa mu ntangiriro za Kanama nyuma y' uko ahagaritswe muri Werurwe kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
UEFA yemeje ko aya marushanwa yombi ahuza amakipe akomeye i Burayi , azasozwa akinwa mu buryo bw' Igikombe cy' Isi .
Hemejwe ko imikino isigaye kugira ngo irushanwa rya Champions League rirangire izakinirwa mu Mujyi wa Lisbon .
Umurwa mukuru wa Portugal uzakira imikino ya kimwe cya kane , iya kimwe cya kabiri n' umukino wa nyuma , yose izakinwa hagati ya tariki ya 12 n' iya 23 Kanama uyu mwaka mu gihe imikino ya kimwe cy' umunani yo kwishyura yari isigaye , izakinirwa aho yagombaga kubera cyangwa muri Portugal kuri Est√°dio do Drag√£o y' i Porto na Est√°dio D .
Afonso Henriques y' i Guimar√£es hagati ya tariki ya 7 n' iya 8 Kanama .
Imikino yose isigaye muri kimwe cya kane na kimwe cya kabiri izajya ikinwa ari umwe ( nta mukino wo kwishyura ) , izabera ku bibuga bibiri byo muri Lisbon - Estadio da Luz na Estadio Jose Alvalade .
Champions League yakomwe mu nkokora na Coronavirus kuva tariki ya 11 Werurwe , ubwo imikino ya kimwe cy' umunani yari igeze hagati .
Manchester City yagombaga kwakira Real Madrid mu mukino wo kwishyura wari kuba tariki ya 17 Werurwe nyuma y' uko yari yatsindiye muri Espagne ibitego 2 - 1 .
Bayern Munich yari yatsinze Chelsea ibitego 3 - 0 , Juventus itsindwa na Lyon igitego 1 - 0 mu gihe FC Barcelone yari yanganyije na Napoli igitego 1 - 1 .
Amakipe ya Paris Saint - Germain , Atalanta , Atl√©tico Madrid na RB Leipzig yari yamaze kubona itike ya kimwe cya kane .
Umujyi wa Istanbul ( Atat√ºrk Olympic Stadium ) wagombaga kwakira umukino wa nyuma wa UEFA Champions League uyu mwaka , wahawe kwakira uw' umwaka utaha .
Europa League izakinirwa mu Budage
UEFA yemeje ko kandi irushanwa rya Europa League naryo rizakinwa muri ubu buryo bumeze nk' Igikombe cy' Isi , aho guhera muri kimwe cya kane imikino izabera mu Budage mu Mijyi ya Cologne , Duisburg , D√ºsseldorf na Gelsenkirchen muri Kanama , haba umukino umwe .
Imikino yo kwishyura yari isigaye nayo izakinirwa aho yagombaga kubera cyangwa mu Budage mu gihe Inter Milan na Getafe , Seville FC na AS Roma zitakinnye umukino n' umwe , zizahura inshuro imwe ( nta mukino wo kwishyura uzabaho ) .
Umujyi wa Gda≈Ñsk wo muri Pologne wagombaga kwakira umukino wa nyuma w' uyu mwaka , wahawe kwakira uw' irushanwa ry' umwaka utaha .
Europa League yahagaze tariki ya 12 Werurwe , izasubukurwa tariki ya 5 n' iya 6 Kanama haba imikino yo kwishyura ( ahabaye imikino ibanza ) mu gihe umukino wa nyuma uzakinwa tariki ya 21 Kanama 2020 .
Siporo zikorwa abantu bategeranye zakomorewe : Ni ryari amakipe ashobora gutangira imyitozo ?
Inama y' Abaminisitiri yateranye ku wa Kabiri tariki ya 16 Werurwe yafatiwemo umwanzuro uvuga ko ibikorwa bya siporo zikorerwa hanze abantu bategeranye zemerewe gukomeza .
Icyakora siporo ikorerwa mu nyubako z' imyidagaduro irabujijwe .
Inama y' Abaminisitiri yateranye ku wa Kabiri tariki ya 16 Werurwe yafatiwemo umwanzuro uvuga ko ibikorwa bya siporo zikorerwa hanze abantu bategeranye zemerewe gukomeza .
Icyakora siporo ikorerwa mu nyubako z' imyidagaduro irabujijwe .
Imyanzuro y' iyi nama ivuga ko " " " " Amabwiriza arambuye kuri iyi ngingo azatangwa na Minisiteri ya Siporo .
Ni amabwiriza yitezweho kureba niba ashobora gutanga umurongo nk' amakipe ashobora gukoramo imyitozo , abakinnyi bategeranye , mbere y' uko imikino imwe n' imwe yazasubukurwa .
Tariki ya 15 Werurwe 2020 nibwo ibikorwa byose by' imikino byahagaritswe mu Rwanda , umunsi umwe nyuma y' uko Minisiteri y' Ubuzima itangaje ko hari umurwayi wa mbere wa Coronavirus wabonetse mu gihugu .
Tariki ya 5 Gicurasi , Minisiteri ya Siporo yagiranye inama na Komite Olempike n' abahagarariye imikino , hemezwa ko hafi imikino ishobora gusubukurwa ari muri Nzeri mu gihe imyitozo yatangira muri Kanama .
Ku wa 4 Kamena Minisiteri ya Siporo yatangaje ko guhera ku wa 8 Kamena , imikino ikorwa abantu bategeranye irimo uwo kunyoga igare , gutwara imodoka , Tennis , Golf , kugenda n' amaguru ( Hiking ) n' imikino ngororamubiri ishobora gusubukurwa ariko hakurikizwa amabwiriza yo kwirinda .
Amwe mu bwiriza yari yashyizweho yarimo kuba nk' abasiganwa ku maguru bagomba guhana intera mu gihe bakorera muri Stade Amahoro n' ahandi haba inzira y' abasiganwa no kuba buri wese akoresha ibikoresho bye ku bajugunya .
Muri Tennis hemejwe ko buri mukinnyi azajya azana imipira ye , akaba ariyo akina ( ashobora gufata mu ntoki ) itari iye akayitanga kuri mugenzi we akoresheje ikirenge cyangwa racket , kuba abakinnyi batemerewe guhinduranya ibibuga no gusiga intera ya metero eshatu hagati yabo ( Tennis ikinwa na babiri ntiyemewe ) .
Hari n' abibajije impamvu umukino wa Cricket utabamo kwegerana , utigeze ushyirwa mu yemerewe gusubukura .

Amakipe ashobora kongera gusubukura imyitozo ?
Nk' uko no mu bindi bihugu birimo iby' i Burayi biri gukorwa muri iyi minsi , hari ibyiciro bacamo mu kongera gusubukura ibikorwa by' imikino .
Ni intambwe amakipe yo mu Rwanda ategereje kuzahabwaho umurongo .
Mu Bwongereza , u Budage , Espagne n' ahandi imikino yasubukuwe , babanje kwemerera abakinnyi gukora ku giti cyabo imikino irimo ngorangingo nko kwiruka .
Icyiciro cya kabiri cyabaye kwemerera amakipe gusubukura imyitozo , bigakorwa abakinnyi bategerena , aho mu cyumweru cya mbere imyitozo yakorwaga mu matsinda ku buryo mu kibuga hatarenga abakinnyi batanu mu gihe mu cyumweru cya kabiri batarengaga 10 .
Iki cyiciro cyakurikiwe no kwemerera amakipe gukorera imyitozo hamwe , ariko hakagira ingamba zo kwirinda zubahirizwa zirimo no gupimwa kenshi kw' abakinnyi dore ko ibi bihugu byo mu Burayi biri mu byazahajwe cyane na Coronavirus .
Hari icyo byafasha amakipe yitegura amarushanwa
Lomami Marcel utoza Gorilla FC yo mu cyiciro cya kabiri izakina imikino ya Playoffs yo guhatanira kuzamuka mu cyiciro cya mbere , yabwiye IGIHE ko nyuma y' amezi atatu imikino imaze ihagaze hari abakinnyi biyongereye ibiro ku buryo baramutse bemerewe gusubukura imyitozo hubahirizwa gusiga intera hagati y' abantu , hari icyo byafasha amakipe .
